# Introduction to BotPenguin | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

Welcome to **BotPenguin**—your all-in-one platform for building smart, powerful, and automated chatbots without writing a single line of code. Whether you want to engage website visitors, automate customer support, streamline lead generation, or manage conversations across multiple channels, BotPenguin makes it effortless.

This page will walk you through what BotPenguin is, what it can do, and why it’s the perfect choice for your business.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#about-botpenguin)

About BotPenguin?

**BotPenguin** is a no-code chatbot and AI Agent builder that allows businesses to create automated conversational experiences.

Using BotPenguin, you can:

*   Build chatbots and AI agents using a visual chatflow builder
    
*   Automate responses to common customer questions
    
*   Capture and manage leads from conversations
    
*   Integrate with external tools and business platforms
    
*   Allow human agents to take over conversations when needed
    

Bots created using BotPenguin can be deployed across several messaging platforms, enabling businesses to manage conversations from multiple channels in one place.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#key-highlights)

Key Highlights

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#no-code-chatbot-and-ai-agent-builder)

🧩 No-Code Chatbot & AI Agent Builder

Create chatbots and AI agents using a visual **chatflow builder**. Design conversations, define responses, and configure actions without writing code.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#ai-powered-responses)

🤖 AI-Powered Responses

Automate responses to common questions and guide users through structured conversation flows.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#multi-channel-deployment)

🌐 Multi-Channel Deployment

Deploy your chatbot across multiple communication channels from one platform:

*   🌍 Website
    
*   💬 WhatsApp
    
*   📘 Facebook Messenger
    
*   📸 Instagram
    
*   ✈️ Telegram
    
*   📧 SMS
    
*   🧑‍🤝‍🧑 MS Teams
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#lead-generation-and-qualification)

🎯 Lead Generation & Qualification

Collect user details during conversations and qualify leads directly through chatbot interactions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#integrations-that-work-for-you)

🔧 Integrations That Work for You

Easily connect BotPenguin with tools such as:

*   CRM systems (Hubspot, Zendesk, Salesforce, Zoho-crm)
    
*   Email marketing platforms
    
*   Ticketing tools
    
*   Google Sheets
    
*   Webhooks and APIs
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#live-chat-handoff)

💬 Live Chat Handoff

Switch from automation to human support instantly using built-in Live Chat.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#analytics-and-insights)

🔍 Analytics & Insights

Track conversations, performance, engagement, and lead data to improve your customer interactions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#id-24-7-automated-support)

📈 24/7 Automated Support

Let your AI bot handle customer queries around the clock—no downtime, no manual intervention.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#why-botpenguin)

Why BotPenguin?

BotPenguin helps businesses:

*   Improve customer experience with instant responses
    
*   Automate repetitive support tasks
    
*   Reduce operational costs
    
*   Increase conversions and lead capture
    
*   Personalize communication at scale
    
*   Provide consistent service across multiple messaging channels
    

Whether you’re a startup, small business, or enterprise, BotPenguin adapts to your needs.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#what-you-can-build-with-botpenguin)

What You Can Build With BotPenguin

BotPenguin enables businesses to automate and manage different types of conversations with users.

Common uses include:

*   💬 **Answer frequently asked questions** automatically
    
*   🧾 **Capture leads from website visitors** during conversations
    
*   🛠 **Automate customer support responses**
    
*   🧭 **Guide users through onboarding or information flows**
    
*   📊 **Collect feedback and user responses**
    

These workflows can be designed using the **chatflow builder**, where you define how the chatbot or AI agent should respond to different user inputs.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/#get-started)

Get Started

To start using BotPenguin:

1️⃣ Log in to your BotPenguin dashboard 2️⃣ Create or select a bot 3️⃣ Build your chatflow 4️⃣ Connect your preferred messaging platforms 5️⃣ Deploy your chatbot or AI agent

You can access your dashboard here:

👉 [**https://app.botpenguin.com/home**arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)

From the dashboard, you can create bots, design chatflows, connect integrations, and manage conversations with your users.

[NextSupported Platforms Overviewchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/supported-platforms-overview)

**🌐 Website**

BotPenguin allows you to install a chatbot directly on your website.

**Features**

*   One-line installation script
    
*   Fully customizable chat widget
    
*   AI Agent support for instant replies
    
*   Lead capture & qualification
    
*   Real-time chat via the Inbox

# Website / Mobile app Bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot#website-chatbot)

Website Chatbot:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A website chatbot on BotPenguin is an AI-powered virtual assistant embedded directly into your website to engage visitors in real-time. It helps automate customer interactions, answer queries, collect leads, and guide users through your offerings—all without human intervention. Designed to work 24/7, the BotPenguin website chatbot ensures consistent support, boosts user engagement, and enhances customer satisfaction by delivering personalized, instant responses.

# System Requirements & Setup Checklist | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **System Requirements & Setup Checklist** helps you verify that your browser, accounts, and connected platforms meet the minimum requirements to use BotPenguin efficiently. It ensures your environment is properly configured before creating, deploying, or testing any chatbot.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#botpenguin-setup-checklist)

BotPenguin Setup Checklist

Below is a structured guide to help you understand and verify all required conditions before starting with BotPenguin.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-1.-verify-your-browser-compatibility)

1\. Verify Your Browser Compatibility

**1.** Ensure you are using a supported browser:

*   Chrome (recommended)
    
*   Firefox
    
*   Microsoft Edge
    
*   Safari
    
*   Brave
    

**2.** Make sure the following settings are enabled:

*   Pop-ups (allowed for BotPenguin dashboard)
    

**3.** Confirm your internet connection is stable (recommended: **10 Mbps+**).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-2.-confirm-general-account-requirements)

2\. Confirm General Account Requirements

*   Ensure you have a valid email address or phone number to access the application. If not, create one to complete the login or signup process.
    
*   Make sure your BotPenguin account is active.
    
*   Verify that your email address and phone number are accessible for verification and communication.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-3.-check-platform-specific-requirements)

3\. Check Platform-Specific Requirements

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#choose-the-requirements-from-the-bot-you-want-to-opt)

Choose the Requirements from the Bot you want to opt:

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#website)

🔹 Website

*   Ability to add a script snippet to your website header/footer
    

circle-info

A **script snippet** is a small piece of code—usually written in JavaScript—that you add to your website’s **header or footer** section.

*   Supported site builders:
    
    *   WordPress
        
    *   Wix
        
    *   Shopify
        
    *   Custom HTML/CSS
        
    *   Webflow
        
    *   Squarespace
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#whatsapp)

**🔹 WhatsApp**

*   A valid phone number that is not currently on Whatsapp.
    
*   Meta Business Manager account
    

**Why this is important:**

*   Meta (Facebook) owns WhatsApp and controls API access.
    
*   Business Manager is used to:
    
    *   Verify your business
        
    *   Manage WhatsApp numbers
        
    *   Create and approve message templates
        
    *   Control access and permissions
        
    
*   **Without this account, WhatsApp API setup is not possible.**
    
    **Why this is important:**
    
    *   Meta uses your website to verify that your business is **legitimate and compliant**.
        
    *   It helps during:
        
        *   Business verification
            
        *   WhatsApp API approval
            
        
    *   The website should clearly display:
        
        *   Business name
            
        *   Products or services
            
        *   Contact details and policies
            
        
    
    > If you don’t have a website, Meta may reject or delay your WhatsApp API approval.
    
*   **Business Website**
    

**Why this is important:**

*   These APIs allow businesses to:
    
    *   Send and receive WhatsApp messages programmatically
        
    *   Automate conversations
        
    *   Use chatbots, broadcasts, and notifications
        
    
*   BotPenguin integrates with these APIs to enable:
    
    *   Customer support automation
        
    *   Marketing campaigns
        
    *   Transactional messaging
        
    
*   **OR Access to WhatsApp Business API or Cloud API**
    

[WhatsApp Bot Creation with Automated onboardingchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-bot-creation-with-automated-onboarding)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#facebook)

**🔹 Facebook**

*   Facebook Page admin access
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#instagram)

**🔹 Instagram**

*   Instagram Business Account
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#telegram)

**🔹 Telegram**

*   Telegram Bot Number
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#ms-teams)

**🔹 MS Teams**

*   MS Teams Admin Center Access
    
*   Ability to add custom apps or connectors
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#sms)

**🔹 SMS**

*   SMS provider credentials (e.g., Twilio)
    
*   Verified sender ID (depending on region)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-4.-prepare-your-ai-agent-requirements)

4\. Prepare Your AI Agent Requirements

To ensure a smooth and effective AI Agent setup, make sure the following are ready:

*   **Define your business clearly** Prepare a concise business description so the AI Agent understands your offerings, use cases, and customer intent accurately.
    
*   **Organize knowledge sources** Gather FAQs, documents, help guides, and relevant website links. Providing structured information helps the AI deliver more accurate and consistent responses.
    
*   **Set communication guidelines** Decide the tone of voice (formal, friendly, professional), response style, and any rules the AI should follow while interacting with users.
    
*   **Define allowed actions** Clearly specify what the AI Agent is permitted to do, such as capturing leads, booking appointments, sharing links, or handing over chats to live agents.
    
*   **Ensure clean and structured data** Well-organized, up-to-date, and clearly formatted data improves AI training quality and overall response accuracy.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-5.-perform-pre-launch-testing)

5\. Perform Pre-Launch Testing

Before publishing your chatbot:

*   Run tests for 10+ conversations
    
*   Validate all chat flows & decision branches
    
*   Test AI responses for accuracy
    
*   Verify integrations (CRM, Google Sheets, etc.)
    

circle-info

**Verify Integrations (CRM, Google Sheets, etc.)**

*   Complete a test chat that sends data to the integration
    
*   Check that the data appears correctly in the CRM or Google Sheet
    
*   Confirm fields are mapped properly (name, email, phone, etc.)
    
*   Ensure entries are created without errors or duplicates
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-6.-complete-final-deployment-checks)

6\. Complete Final Deployment Checks

Fulfill these deployment checks before making your Bot live :

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#website-bot)

**Website Bot**

*   Script snippet added successfully
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#whatsapp-bot)

**WhatsApp Bot**

*   Number connected OR API connection verified
    
*   Green tick applied (optional)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#other-channels)

**Other Channels**

*   Bot connected to platform
    
*   Permissions approved
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/getting-started/system-requirements-and-setup-checklist#id-7.-apply-recommended-best-practices)

7\. Apply Recommended Best Practices

*   Update AI training materials monthly.
    
*   Use modular chat flow design to avoid complexity.
    
*   Monitor chatbot analytics weekly.
    
*   Maintain consistent tone and response rules.
    
*   Keep platform integrations up-to-date.
    

* * *

🎉 **Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section! You're one step closer to mastering BotPenguin.**

[NextCreating Your First Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/creating-your-first-chatbot)

# Install your Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#what-is-website-chatbot-installation)

What is Website Chatbot Installation?

Website Chatbot Installation in BotPenguin allows you to integrate your chatbot directly into your website. Once installed, the chatbot can engage visitors, answer queries, collect leads, and provide instant support — all without needing additional software or manual intervention.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#benefits-of-installing-your-website-chatbot)

Benefits of Installing Your Website Chatbot

*   **Engage visitors instantly**: Start conversations with website users in real time.
    
*   **Generate leads efficiently**: Capture user details automatically during interactions.
    
*   **Provide 24/7 support**: Ensure visitors get help even when your team is offline.
    
*   **Boost conversions**: Guide users through products or services directly in chat.
    
*   **Simplify management**: One integration handles all website interactions seamlessly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#methods-to-install-your-chatbot)

Methods to Install Your Chatbot:

1.  [Install your Website Chatbot](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot)
     : Use this option to add the chatbot to your **entire website**. By installing the website chatbot script, the bot appears on all selected pages of your site and allows visitors to chat in real time. This method is ideal for business websites, blogs, and eCommerce stores where you want continuous customer engagement.
    
2.  [Install your Landing Page Bot](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot)
    : This option lets you embed the BotPenguin chatbot code directly into the **HTML of a specific landing page**. It enables live chat only on that page, making it perfect for campaigns, product launches, or lead-generation pages where focused interaction is required.
    
3.  [Install your Mobile App Chatbot](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot)
    : Use this method to integrate the chatbot into your **mobile application**. The chatbot can be embedded within Android or iOS apps using the provided integration details, allowing users to chat without leaving the app.
    
4.  [Install Embedded Chatbot](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot)
    : The Embedded Chatbot allows you to place the chatbot inside a **specific section of a webpage**, such as a support page or dashboard, instead of showing it as a floating widget. This provides a seamless and controlled chat experience within your page layout.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#faqs-for-website-chatbot-installation)

FAQs for Website Chatbot Installation

chevron-rightDo I need coding knowledge to install the chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-install-the-chatbot)

Yes, basic understanding of how to paste code into your website is helpful, but BotPenguin is compatible with most CMS platforms and website builders without coding.

chevron-rightCan I install multiple chatbots on one website?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#can-i-install-multiple-chatbots-on-one-website)

No, it’s recommended to install only one chatbot per website to avoid conflicts and overlapping messages.

chevron-rightDoes the chatbot work on mobile devices?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#does-the-chatbot-work-on-mobile-devices)

Yes, the BotPenguin website chatbot is fully responsive and works on desktop, tablet, and mobile screens.

chevron-rightCan I remove or update the chatbot later?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#can-i-remove-or-update-the-chatbot-later)

Yes. Simply remove or replace the embed code in your website HTML. Updates from the dashboard will reflect automatically if the code remains.

chevron-rightHow do I troubleshoot if the chatbot doesn’t appear?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#how-do-i-troubleshoot-if-the-chatbot-doesnt-appear)

Check that the code is correctly pasted, clear your browser cache, and ensure there are no script-blocking plugins. Contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** if issues persist.

chevron-rightCan I install the chatbot on a custom-built website, WordPress, Wix, or Squarespace?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#can-i-install-the-chatbot-on-a-custom-built-website-wordpress-wix-or-squarespace)

Yes, BotPenguin provides platform-specific instructions for each: custom HTML embed for custom websites, plugin or code embed for WordPress, Custom Code section for Wix, and Code Injection for Squarespace.

chevron-rightWill the chatbot automatically update after installation?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot#will-the-chatbot-automatically-update-after-installation)

Yes, any updates you make to the chatbot on the BotPenguin dashboard will reflect on your website automatically, as long as the embed code remains in place.

[PreviousBot Setup and installationchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation)
[NextInstall your Website Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot)

# Creating Your First Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/creating-your-first-chatbot#what-is-chatbot-description)

What is Chatbot Description?

The **Chatbot Description** provides a clear understanding of BotPenguin’s AI-powered conversational assistant. It explains how BotPenguin chatbots automate interactions, offer instant support, capture user data, and guide customers across multiple digital channels—without manual involvement.

Chatbots built using BotPenguin leverage advanced NLP to understand intent, respond accurately, and deliver smooth, personalized conversations across websites, WhatsApp, Facebook, Instagram, Telegram, MS Teams, and SMS.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/creating-your-first-chatbot#how-to-use-chatbot-description)

How to Use Chatbot Description

Below is the step-by-step guide to creating your chatbot inside BotPenguin.

1.  **Open the Bots Section**
    

From the left sidebar, click on **“Bots”**.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fw3xh7dlIH7gbtXohkb2d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a5ede9-d5fd-4b32-ae45-0ea81aa27d82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e2c2eca&sv=2)

1.  **Create a New Bot**
    

Click on **“Create New Bot”** to start building a new chatbot.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwMk3srA05zMdBIjmcA7v%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfd82e11-856e-4741-b9ec-b215a780646e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4da199de&sv=2)

1.  **Select Chatbot Platform**
    

Choose the type of bot you want to connect with (Website, WhatsApp, Facebook, Instagram, Telegram, MS Teams, SMS).

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fo7jTHJTELfCU332JTnKF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5dc5bc61-383e-4afe-9828-d96e59f0184a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72a4fc3&sv=2)

1.  Select the Usecase of the Chatbot and accordingly it will apply the Chatflow to the Chatbot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F7gtxVPJE79MCPX6F9X6T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea34dbcd-1ec8-4a0d-b3d1-6663fe67cc8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c1aa09&sv=2)

1.  Configure the chatflow.
    

[comments-questionManage Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fk9Auq6CbIXtdC3djU3lO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ce7fd5b-3695-4ee9-9c2b-ac69a0976477&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12720734&sv=2)

1.  Double Click on the Component to open the Configure window of the particular Component.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FKVUaeApaQulQ3Nev4SGU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbec0aefd-6142-488b-acea-3be6ddfad414&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe511771&sv=2)

1.  Configure the General and Advance settings of the particular component.
    
2.  Click on Classic Builder button to switch to Classic mode.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFAt8CYpcwluIevRd4J7E%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D494c635f-39db-4cbf-83f8-2655febb7b98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2863175&sv=2)

1.  And the mode will be switched to classic.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FG50PgNkWNySYWGSAbw6y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D516a7a3d-e7e8-403f-80eb-9416aa6d0e9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a576c424&sv=2)

1.  Click on Import Template button to import the existing Chat Templates into your Chatflow or create new one from the scratch.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLVaQQqIeaT1dI0taJYQy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46271c41-6320-4218-b2a3-fe1daf1ac5ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97b29344&sv=2)

You may select from existing templates or skip this step to build your bot from scratch.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F7NVU5zRB1d8RO4GO7YE3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De76a52a8-9d97-4ca8-a267-66547b8bf480&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35af8f87&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMeNgRgYGbkERjEb2hlZa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a71b12a-2c36-44fa-9db1-551a30fe108d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f06ef23f&sv=2)

1.  Click on **"Test"** button to test your chatflow on website or Landing Page.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fc8s0m6l71Q23q6ybYCnm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfba2434b-db29-4ced-ac49-00a463d037ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d0334c8&sv=2)

1.  Click on Install button to install the Chatbot on different platforms.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUCEBZB7UCSeUVysb4co6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23be9b3e-eeef-4a4b-9acc-a91121525a63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a571de9&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWdRAR9DsEXXQhBaIvjk6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c9b322f-20b8-4a64-9070-fc2a6c16c875&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b9836e&sv=2)

[spider-webBot Setup and installationchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation)

1.  **Navigate to Your Created Chatbot**
    

Navigate to the chatbot you just created. BotPenguin organizes all bots clearly so you can find yours easily.

* * *

🎉 **Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section! You're one step closer to mastering BotPenguin.**

# Install your Mobile App Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot#what-is-install-mobile-app-chatbot)

What is Install Mobile App Chatbot?

The **Mobile App Chatbot** allows you to integrate your BotPenguin chatbot directly into a mobile application. Based on your app’s development framework, BotPenguin provides platform-specific installation guidance to ensure smooth chatbot integration and optimal performance.

You can choose from **iOS**, **Android**, **React Native**, or **Other** depending on how your mobile app is built.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot#how-to-use-install-mobile-app-chatbot)

How to Use Install Mobile App Chatbot

Follow the steps below based on the mobile platform used to build your app.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot#id-1.-open-mobile-app-chatbot-installation)

1\. Open Mobile App Chatbot Installation

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fs8FczsWxhpeqrJdUvNZf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca3d150b-6cea-40e1-bd5f-fbffd1dca1e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1d9995f&sv=2)

1.  Click on Bots from the Left menu and select the bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZmLdcxPFEodJeMreFAKp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8567c327-344f-495d-9263-8d311c493803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57ffeefe&sv=2)

1.  Now click on **“Install Your Chatbot.”**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnySbpv3zBrItfl8rgo6L%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D940db384-ae93-4dd1-9f6d-a82ab555c4e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=417500cc&sv=2)

1.  Select the **“Mobile App Chatbot”** tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVHbmaFIDCqMPsocCXEdf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D415b1707-4072-42a9-985b-ef27ae703e1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2d900c7&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot#id-2.-select-your-mobile-platform)

# Install your Landing Page Bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#what-is-install-landing-page-bot)

What is Install Landing Page Bot?

The **Landing Page Bot** provides you with a unique, ready-to-use chatbot link hosted by BotPenguin. This link opens a standalone chatbot page that users can interact with instantly—without requiring website integration or code installation.

You can share this link across social media, contact pages, emails, QR codes, or business cards to start conversations immediately.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#how-to-use-install-landing-page-bot)

How to Use Install Landing Page Bot

Follow the steps below to access, test, and share your Landing Page Bot.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#id-1.-open-landing-page-bot-installation)

1\. Open Landing Page Bot Installation

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fs8FczsWxhpeqrJdUvNZf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca3d150b-6cea-40e1-bd5f-fbffd1dca1e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1d9995f&sv=2)

1.  Click on Bots from the Left menu and select the bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZmLdcxPFEodJeMreFAKp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8567c327-344f-495d-9263-8d311c493803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57ffeefe&sv=2)

1.  Now click on **“Install Your Chatbot.”**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnySbpv3zBrItfl8rgo6L%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D940db384-ae93-4dd1-9f6d-a82ab555c4e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=417500cc&sv=2)

1.  Click on the **“Landing Page Bot”** tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FkxDIXy1iOyvfmvJR4oHi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8be23748-9590-4cd9-bcc1-1978a07e4ae1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46c5406e&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#id-2.-access-your-unique-bot-link)

2\. Access Your Unique Bot Link

*   You will see a message confirming your **unique Landing Page Bot URL**. This link is automatically generated for your chatbot.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#id-3.-test-the-landing-page-bot)

3\. Test the Landing Page Bot

*   Click **“Test”** to preview how the chatbot appears and interacts with users.
    
*   Test view of the Landing Bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FEGJrOOXNA9ksRt4JI4Cz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D149a4287-c9ad-425b-9541-38a8aeeee409&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=548836b5&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#id-4.-copy-and-share-the-bot-url)

4\. Copy and Share the Bot URL

*   Click **“Copy URL”** to copy the chatbot link.
    
*   Share this link on:
    

1.  Social media platforms
    
2.  Contact or support pages
    
3.  Email campaigns
    
4.  QR codes
    
5.  Business cards
    

Once shared, users can start chatting instantly.

🎉 **Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section! You're one step closer to mastering BotPenguin.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#faqs)

FAQ's

Here are some common questions asked regarding training with FAQ's:

chevron-rightWhat is a Landing Page Bot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#what-is-a-landing-page-bot)

A Landing Page Bot is a standalone chatbot hosted by BotPenguin that users can access via a direct link without installing it on a website.

chevron-rightDo I need a website to use a Landing Page Bot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#do-i-need-a-website-to-use-a-landing-page-bot)

No. The Landing Page Bot works independently and does not require a website.

chevron-rightWhere can I share the Landing Page Bot link?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#where-can-i-share-the-landing-page-bot-link)

You can share it on social media, emails, contact pages, QR codes, or printed materials like business cards.

chevron-rightCan I customize the chatbot before sharing the link?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#can-i-customize-the-chatbot-before-sharing-the-link)

Yes. You can fully customize the chat flow, messages, and branding before sharing the link.

chevron-rightCan I test the bot before sharing it publicly?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#can-i-test-the-bot-before-sharing-it-publicly)

Yes. Use the **“Test”** button to preview and verify the chatbot experience.

chevron-rightWill the same link work for all users?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#will-the-same-link-work-for-all-users)

Yes. The generated Landing Page Bot URL can be accessed by unlimited users.

chevron-rightCan I disable or regenerate the Landing Page Bot link?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-landing-page-bot#can-i-disable-or-regenerate-the-landing-page-bot-link)

You can stop or modify chatbot behavior by editing the bot, but the link remains tied to the same chatbot.

If you still have questions for our team, write to us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#33404643435c414773515c4743565d54465a5d1d505c5e)
. We’ll get back to you within 48 hours.

[NextInstall your Mobile App Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot)

# Manage Chatflow | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Edit and Manage Chatflow** section allows you to view, update, organize, and control all conversation flows created for your chatbot. From here, you can fine-tune how your bot interacts with users by editing messages, managing multiple flows, and defining how and when each flow is triggered.

This section is essential for maintaining accurate, engaging, and goal-driven chatbot conversations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#what-you-can-do-here)

What You Can Do Here

Using the **Edit and Manage Chatflow** page, you can:

*   Edit existing chat flows
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCYGKdxDBiAsU29S8J4Rg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De28090ef-0aa6-45d0-b962-98b95571271c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c23feadf&sv=2)

*   Clicking on Visualise Flow will switch the mode.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fk9Auq6CbIXtdC3djU3lO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ce7fd5b-3695-4ee9-9c2b-ac69a0976477&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12720734&sv=2)

*   ​Double Click on the Component to open the Configure window of the particular Component.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FKVUaeApaQulQ3Nev4SGU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbec0aefd-6142-488b-acea-3be6ddfad414&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe511771&sv=2)

*   Configure the General and Advance settings of the particular component.
    
*   Click on Classic Builder button to switch to Classic mode.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFAt8CYpcwluIevRd4J7E%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D494c635f-39db-4cbf-83f8-2655febb7b98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2863175&sv=2)

1.  And the mode will be switched to classic.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FvX2kyQfXTI1DAEkTr6CZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16d19287-9730-4695-873e-69198ccb555e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=937f39f8&sv=2)

*   Create and manage multiple flows with the help of Redirect Component
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FAJ9ieCY57MUu3vfiL2EQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44f3f8d9-b486-401d-a899-959554b0be40&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2df39777&sv=2)

[Multiple Flows (Redirect Component)chevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component)

*   Set a default chat flow
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLmH2JqRmnz1qm1rI8WEM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4e49703-9fcd-4594-a65b-1cce9b516569&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9217f7b&sv=2)

*   Enable or disable revisit flows
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FogOcLRtHouvRv2sWuPwl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e7cc0dd-baed-47b2-a007-726f9fc35375&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0ece494&sv=2)

*   Import and export chat flows
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fi6QZy6lKS98ydJNy7meZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7108d8ea-3a7b-4e54-8ad8-87c14101f945&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcf35144&sv=2)

[Create Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow)
[Components in Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow)

*   Delete unused or outdated flows
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fx8uuczqHuvrSwXMBlzhw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df731b1ab-0825-41dd-ba6b-95bb6c74a70d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1677697&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightCan I edit a live chat flow?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#can-i-edit-a-live-chat-flow)

Yes. Any saved changes are applied immediately to the chatbot.

chevron-rightCan I have multiple chat flows?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#can-i-have-multiple-chat-flows)

Yes. You can create and manage multiple flows, but only one can be the default.

chevron-rightWhat happens if I delete a flow?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#what-happens-if-i-delete-a-flow)

The flow is permanently removed and cannot be restored.

chevron-rightCan I reuse chat flows in another bot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#can-i-reuse-chat-flows-in-another-bot)

Yes. Download the flow and import it into another bot of the same type.

chevron-rightWhy should I use revisit flows?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow#why-should-i-use-revisit-flows)

Revisit flows allow returning users to access the same conversation again, improving continuity and user experience.

# Install your Website Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide:

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#what-is-website-chatbot-deployment)

What is Website Chatbot Deployment?

Website Chatbot Deployment in BotPenguin allows you to integrate your chatbot directly into your website. Once deployed, the chatbot can assist visitors, answer queries, collect leads, and provide support in real time, making your website more interactive and user-friendly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#benefits-of-deploying-your-website-chatbot)

Benefits of Deploying Your Website Chatbot

*   **Engage visitors instantly:** Start conversations with website users in real time.
    
*   **Generate leads efficiently:** Capture user details automatically during interactions.
    
*   **Provide 24/7 support:** Ensure visitors get help even when your team is offline.
    
*   **Boost conversions:** Guide users through products or services directly in chat.
    
*   **Simplify management:** One integration handles all website interactions seamlessly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#what-does-deploying-a-chatbot-mean)

What does Deploying a Chatbot Mean?

Deploying a chatbot on a website means making your chatbot live and available on your site, so customers can interact with it directly. This process involves adding the chatbot to your website, enabling it to assist visitors, answer questions, and provide support in real time.

Your chatbot will be live on your website like this:-

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FNPPWYtep9WN6YaHSeQML%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8866ccd7-8db1-4f6e-b312-f029af400186&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c1361d3&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before you begin installing your chatbot, ensure you have completed the following steps:

*   **Create Your Website Chatbot**: Ensure that your chatbot is fully developed and tested.
    
*   **Complete the "Edit Your Chat Flow" Section**: Make sure you have configured your chatbot's conversation flow to handle customer interactions effectively.
    

Once these prerequisites are met, you can proceed with the installation of your chatbot.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#steps-to-install-your-website-chatbot)

Steps to Install Your Website Chatbot

1.  To manage all your chatbots, you first need to visit the BotPenguin Dashboard: [https://app.botpenguin.com/homearrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fs8FczsWxhpeqrJdUvNZf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca3d150b-6cea-40e1-bd5f-fbffd1dca1e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1d9995f&sv=2)

1.  Click on Bots from the Left menu and select the bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZmLdcxPFEodJeMreFAKp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8567c327-344f-495d-9263-8d311c493803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57ffeefe&sv=2)

1.  Now click on **“Install Your Chatbot.”**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnySbpv3zBrItfl8rgo6L%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D940db384-ae93-4dd1-9f6d-a82ab555c4e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=417500cc&sv=2)

1.  You can select the platform where you need to deploy your chatbot.
    
2.  Click on **“Custom Built”** to install your chatbot on your website.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F42lHurqIhtUjQikAEcDU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a606cce-5ac5-4f51-b774-2187de6110a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6a381f0&sv=2)

*   Website Chatbot: The chatbot is embedded and active on the website interface.
    
*   Landing Page Bot: The chatbot is embedded and active on the landing page interface.
    
*   Mobile App Chatbot: The chatbot is embedded and active on the mobile app interface.
    
*   Embedded Chatbot: The Embedded Chatbot allows you to place the chatbot inside a specific section of a webpage, such as a support page or dashboard, instead of showing it as a floating widget.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#test-your-code)

Test Your Code

1.  To see how your chatbot will function and appear on your website and landing page, click on the **"Test"** button and select whether you want to test the Website or Landing Page bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FTEhbHeMb0DIUtahY22aj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf698abb-d47f-48fa-bd29-8c34142edfbf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73b928e&sv=2)

1.  Now let’s move ahead with the installing part.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#how-to-install-your-website-chatbot)

**How to Install Your Website Chatbot**

Follow these steps to install your chatbot on your website using the **Website Chatbot** option.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-1-go-to-the-bots-section)

**Step 1: Go to the Bots Section**

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**.
    
2.  From the left-hand menu, click on **Bots**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FyUmwCN3wvArj56TCCP2I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c193ecd-5fab-4fff-9410-0d9c646127ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e51beffe&sv=2)

1.  Select the bot you want to install.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-2-open-the-install-your-chatbot-screen)

**Step 2: Open the Install Your Chatbot Screen**

1.  After selecting the bot, click on **Install Your Chatbot**.
    
2.  By default, the **Website Chatbot** tab will be selected.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F4WxIQJrOEADJb0y05ai8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f21205f-8df7-4afa-9b14-e57ecec67c86&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a233bec5&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-3-choose-your-website-platform)

**Step 3: Choose Your Website Platform**

Under the **Website Chatbot** section, select the platform where you want to install the bot:

*   **Custom Built** – For custom or self-hosted websites
    
*   **WordPress** – For WordPress websites
    
*   **Shopify** – For Shopify stores
    
*   **Wix** – For Wix websites
    
*   **Squarespace** – For Squarespace websites
    
*   **None / Not Sure** – If your platform is not listed or you’re unsure
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-4-follow-platform-specific-instructions)

**Step 4: Follow Platform-Specific Instructions**

1.  Click on your website platform.
    
2.  Copy the chatbot script or follow the on-screen installation instructions provided.
    
3.  Paste the script into your website as instructed (usually before the closing `</body>` tag).
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fp6hGzkC8MmgKqrbnxrQR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03ab76e3-40f6-46ca-b33c-674e2f394622&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc086bf3&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-5-publish-your-website)

**Step 5: Publish Your Website**

1.  Save the changes on your website.
    
2.  Publish or deploy your site to make the chatbot live.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-6-test-your-chatbot)

**Step 6: Test Your Chatbot**

1.  Click on the **Test Bot** button at the bottom-right of the screen.
    
2.  Open your website and verify that the chatbot appears and responds correctly.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#step-7-check-connection-status)

**Step 7: Check Connection Status**

Once installed successfully, the platform card will no longer show Not Connected, confirming the chatbot is live.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#faqs-for-website-chatbot-deployment)

FAQs for Website Chatbot Deployment

chevron-rightDo I need coding knowledge to install the chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-install-the-chatbot)

Basic understanding of how to paste code into your website is helpful, but BotPenguin is compatible with most CMS platforms and website builders without coding.

chevron-rightCan I install multiple chatbots on one website?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#can-i-install-multiple-chatbots-on-one-website)

No, it’s recommended to install only one chatbot per website to avoid conflicts and overlapping messages.

chevron-rightDoes the chatbot work on mobile devices?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#does-the-chatbot-work-on-mobile-devices)

Yes, the BotPenguin website chatbot is fully responsive and works on desktop, tablet, and mobile screens.

chevron-rightCan I remove or update the chatbot later?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#can-i-remove-or-update-the-chatbot-later)

Yes. Simply remove or replace the embed code in your website HTML. Updates from the dashboard will reflect automatically if the code remains.

chevron-rightHow do I troubleshoot if the chatbot doesn’t appear?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#how-do-i-troubleshoot-if-the-chatbot-doesnt-appear)

Check that the code is correctly pasted, clear your browser cache, and ensure there are no script-blocking plugins. Contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** if issues persist.

chevron-rightCan I install the chatbot on a custom-built website, WordPress, Wix, or SquareSpace?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#can-i-install-the-chatbot-on-a-custom-built-website-wordpress-wix-or-squarespace)

Yes, BotPenguin provides platform-specific instructions for each: custom HTML embed for custom websites, plugin or code embed for WordPress, Custom Code section for Wix, and Code Injection for Squarespace.

chevron-rightWill the chatbot automatically update after installation?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-website-chatbot#will-the-chatbot-automatically-update-after-installation)

Yes, any updates you make to the chatbot on the BotPenguin dashboard will reflect on your website automatically, as long as the embed code remains in place.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b1c2c4c1c1dec3c5f1d3dec5c1d4dfd6c4d8df9fd2dedc)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How to create a Website chatbot

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#steps-to-make-a-website-chatbot)

Steps to Make a Website Chatbot


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  To create your Website chatbot , you first need to visit the BotPenguin Dashboard: [https://app.botpenguin.com/homearrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)
    
2.  To start creating your new chatbot, Click on Bots then click on **"Create New Bot."**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fw3xh7dlIH7gbtXohkb2d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a5ede9-d5fd-4b32-ae45-0ea81aa27d82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e2c2eca&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwMk3srA05zMdBIjmcA7v%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddfd82e11-856e-4741-b9ec-b215a780646e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4da199de&sv=2)

1.  Select the platform.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fo7jTHJTELfCU332JTnKF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5dc5bc61-383e-4afe-9828-d96e59f0184a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72a4fc3&sv=2)

1.  Select the Usecase for creating your bot and proceed further.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F7gtxVPJE79MCPX6F9X6T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea34dbcd-1ec8-4a0d-b3d1-6663fe67cc8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c1aa09&sv=2)

1.  You will be redirected to the Chatflow. You can change the flow to the Classic Builder according to your convenience.
    
2.  You can configure the chatflow and test it accordingly.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fk9Auq6CbIXtdC3djU3lO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ce7fd5b-3695-4ee9-9c2b-ac69a0976477&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12720734&sv=2)

​

1.  Double Click on the Component to open the Configure window of the particular Component.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FKVUaeApaQulQ3Nev4SGU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbec0aefd-6142-488b-acea-3be6ddfad414&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe511771&sv=2)

1.  Configure the General and Advance settings of the particular component.
    
2.  Click on Classic Builder button to switch to Classic mode.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFAt8CYpcwluIevRd4J7E%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D494c635f-39db-4cbf-83f8-2655febb7b98&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2863175&sv=2)

1.  And the mode will be switched to classic.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FvX2kyQfXTI1DAEkTr6CZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16d19287-9730-4695-873e-69198ccb555e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=937f39f8&sv=2)

You may select from existing templates or skip this step to build your bot from scratch.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLVaQQqIeaT1dI0taJYQy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46271c41-6320-4218-b2a3-fe1daf1ac5ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97b29344&sv=2)

1.  Click on Import Template button to import the existing Chat Templates into your Chatflow or create new one from the scratch.
    

​

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F7NVU5zRB1d8RO4GO7YE3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De76a52a8-9d97-4ca8-a267-66547b8bf480&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35af8f87&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMeNgRgYGbkERjEb2hlZa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a71b12a-2c36-44fa-9db1-551a30fe108d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f06ef23f&sv=2)

1.  Click on **"Test"** button to test your chatflow on website or Landing Page.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fc8s0m6l71Q23q6ybYCnm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfba2434b-db29-4ced-ac49-00a463d037ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d0334c8&sv=2)

1.  Click on Install button to install the Chatbot on different platforms.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUCEBZB7UCSeUVysb4co6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23be9b3e-eeef-4a4b-9acc-a91121525a63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a571de9&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWdRAR9DsEXXQhBaIvjk6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c9b322f-20b8-4a64-9070-fc2a6c16c875&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b9836e&sv=2)

[Install your Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot)

🎉 Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section!

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#faqs-for-website-chatbot-creation)

FAQs for Website Chatbot Creation

chevron-rightDo I need coding knowledge to create a Website Chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-create-a-website-chatbot)

No, BotPenguin provides a no-code builder. You can create and configure your chatbot using drag-and-drop components without any technical expertise.

chevron-rightCan I switch between Flow Builder and Classic Builder anytime?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#can-i-switch-between-flow-builder-and-classic-builder-anytime)

Yes, you can switch to **“Classic Builder”** from the Chatflow screen whenever required. However, ensure your flow logic is reviewed after switching modes.

chevron-rightCan I build a chatbot from scratch instead of using a template?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#can-i-build-a-chatbot-from-scratch-instead-of-using-a-template)

Yes, you can skip template selection and create your chatbot completely from scratch using the builder.

chevron-rightHow can I test my chatbot before going live?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#how-can-i-test-my-chatbot-before-going-live)

Click on the **“Test”** button inside the Chatflow builder to preview how the chatbot will respond on your website or landing page.

chevron-rightWhat does the “Install” button do?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#what-does-the-install-button-do)

The **“Install”** button generates the integration script or platform-specific installation method required to deploy the chatbot on your website or other supported platforms.

chevron-rightCan I edit my chatbot after installing it on my website?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation#can-i-edit-my-chatbot-after-installing-it-on-my-website)

Yes, you can update the chatflow anytime. Changes will reflect automatically once saved and published.

* * *

If you still have questions for our team, write to us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#33404643435c414773515c4743565d54465a5d1d505c5e)
. We’ll get back to you within 48 hours.

# Install Embedded Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Embedded Chatbot** allows you to place your chatbot directly inside any webpage using a simple HTML `<iframe>` snippet. This is ideal for dashboards, support pages, or custom layouts where you want the chatbot to appear inline.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#access-the-embedded-chatbot-installation)

Access the Embedded Chatbot Installation

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**.
    
2.  Click on Bots from left menu then Select the bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZmLdcxPFEodJeMreFAKp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8567c327-344f-495d-9263-8d311c493803&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57ffeefe&sv=2)

1.  Now click on **“Install Your Chatbot.”**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnySbpv3zBrItfl8rgo6L%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D940db384-ae93-4dd1-9f6d-a82ab555c4e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=417500cc&sv=2)

1.  Select the **Embedded Chatbot** tab from the top menu.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FidlasoCklPZxq9N8Bq1A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d5bcff7-582c-43cf-b887-5318e432dbc7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef9c0fbc&sv=2)

You will see the installation options for embedding your chatbot into a website.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#get-the-installation-code)

Get the Installation Code

In the **Get Chatbot Installation Code** section:

1.  Copy the iframe code provided.
    
2.  This code is unique to your chatbot.
    

Example:

> 💡 **Tip:** You can adjust the `width` and `height` values to match your page layout.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#add-the-code-to-your-website)

Add the Code to Your Website

Paste the copied iframe code into the HTML of every page where you want the chatbot to appear.

**Common placements include:**

*   Inside the `<body>` tag
    
*   Within a specific container or section
    
*   Embedded inside CMS editors (WordPress, Webflow, etc.)
    

> ⚠️ Make sure the page allows iframes and does not block third-party embeds.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#share-installation-code-with-your-developer-optional)

Share Installation Code with Your Developer (Optional)

If a developer manages your website:

1.  Enter their email address in the **Share Installation Code** section.
    
2.  Click **Send Email**.
    

The developer will receive the installation instructions directly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#request-botpenguin-installation-support)

Request BotPenguin Installation Support

If you prefer hands-on assistance:

1.  Click **Help me in Installing ChatBot**.
    
2.  The BotPenguin support team will handle the installation for you.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#verify-the-installation)

Verify the Installation

Once added:

*   Reload your webpage
    
*   Confirm the chatbot appears correctly
    
*   Test a conversation to ensure it responds as expected
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

If the chatbot does not appear:

*   Confirm the iframe code is pasted correctly
    
*   Check that your website allows external embeds
    
*   Ensure no ad blockers or CSP rules are blocking the iframe
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#faqs)

FAQ's

Here are some common questions asked regarding training with FAQ's:

chevron-rightDo I need coding knowledge to install it?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-install-it)

No. If you can copy and paste HTML code, you can install the embedded chatbot. For advanced customization or CMS setups, a developer may help

chevron-rightWhere can I embed the chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#where-can-i-embed-the-chatbot)

You can embed the chatbot on:

*   Any HTML webpage
    
*   Dashboards or internal tools
    
*   CMS platforms like WordPress, Webflow, or Wix
    
*   Customer support or help pages
    

chevron-rightCan I change the size of the embedded chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#can-i-change-the-size-of-the-embedded-chatbot)

Yes. You can modify the `width` and `height` values in the iframe code to fit your page layout.

chevron-rightWill the chatbot work on mobile devices?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#will-the-chatbot-work-on-mobile-devices)

Yes. The embedded chatbot is responsive and works on mobile devices as long as the iframe is placed inside a responsive container.

chevron-rightCan I embed the chatbot on multiple pages?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#can-i-embed-the-chatbot-on-multiple-pages)

Absolutely. You can use the same iframe code on as many pages as you want.

chevron-rightCan I send the installation code to my developer?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#can-i-send-the-installation-code-to-my-developer)

Yes. Use the **Share Installation Code** option to email the iframe code directly to your developer.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-embedded-chatbot#support)

Support

If you still have questions for our team, write to us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#46353336362934320624293236232821332f286825292b)
. We’ll get back to you within 48 hours.

[PreviousOther / Native Appschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/bot-setup-and-installation/install-your-chatbot/install-your-mobile-app-chatbot/other-native-apps)
[NextManage Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow)
