# Create Chatflow | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#customize-your-chatbot)

Customize Your Chatbot


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your bot looks great—now let’s make it even smarter. This guide will help you edit and customize your chat flow so your chatbot speaks exactly the way you want.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#what-is-a-chat-flow)

What Is a Chat Flow?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A **Chat Flow** is the structured sequence of messages that shapes how your chatbot interacts with users. It defines the order of questions, messages, and actions, guiding the entire conversation.

Here’s an example of how a chat flow might look:

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FDZd51ECcpBNa8nqkqaM6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff50cfe1-9961-4aad-9ef7-e266faae7e4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e173cf6&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#how-to-customize-the-chat-flow)

How to Customize the Chat Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-1.-access-the-chat-flow-editor)

1\. Access the Chat Flow Editor

1.  Click on the Bots and Select your bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FjFWBpHJVlOtZyp0zYRQs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8cee412-4611-463f-8f7a-46385b3f3a87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3a59f5b&sv=2)

1.  Click on the Chatflow tab from the expanded menu.
    
2.  Select the flow you want to edit or create a new flow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FcVaXt8w7YwxGqnUBOe5n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfffe16f5-571d-4990-b02f-e8a88434bd03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71775876&sv=2)

1.  Select your pre-created chatbot from the list (you can also search by name).
    
2.  To start fresh, you have two choices:
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-2.-import-an-existing-flow)

2\. Import an Existing Flow

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#a.-import-flow)

a. Import Flow

*   Click **Import flow** button on the top-right.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F1JYgCERH8q7ueNYkZDYh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D166e7ee0-cd48-45bb-b126-5d6d183ef245&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=150b2405&sv=2)

*   Upload a `.json` file containing the chatflow you want to reuse.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrMATg3loLBuhiALSc1KP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bba2907-82c4-4273-80ad-521885eed3f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56aa5ffe&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#b.-create-a-new-flow)

b. Create a New Flow

*   Click **Create New Flow**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR1DaxLUIcZBkZf6l7yyL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db78036c0-391e-49e0-a0f5-311fe9c222f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4868b300&sv=2)

*   Enter a name for your flow, then click **Create Flow**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fu2cliF1udxSmhVlUlcyc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d06e702-2600-4654-a4e0-074db1117586&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50507f1a&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#tools-to-edit-the-chat-flow)

Tools to Edit the Chat Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Chat Flow Editor includes a set of tools to help you build, manage, and refine every part of the conversation.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-1.-add-chat-components)

1\. Add Chat Components

Select components from the menu to insert elements such as:

*   User input fields (name, email, phone number)
    
*   Single-choice or multi-choice questions
    
*   Web links
    
*   Smart questions
    
*   Live Chat transfers
    
    These components help you collect valuable data and create meaningful conversational journeys.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIpRYjP2qRXHhjBTgIUdY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd135a25f-35e2-4831-a292-9ffe9184934b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1abca93&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-2.-navigation-and-design-tools)

2\. Navigation & Design Tools

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#toolbar-bottom-left-corner)

**Toolbar (Bottom-left corner)**

This toolbar helps you navigate and manage your flow:

*   **Fit View** – Center the flow on screen
    
*   **Zoom In / Zoom Out** – Adjust visibility
    
*   **Delete Flow** – Remove the entire flow and start fresh
    
*   **Lock Flow** – Prevent accidental edits
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#mini-map-bottom-right-corner)

**Mini Map (Bottom-right corner)**

Shows your flow’s position, making it easy to find components even in large, branching chat flows.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#line-connectors)

**Line Connectors**

Drag connectors between components to define conversation paths.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#test-flow)

**Test Flow**

Click **Test Flow** to preview how the chatbot will interact with users.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FfaVdVQjfVJjecpqCcCMh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bcc0a5c-8283-4625-9e26-46135ee65697&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3be14a55&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-3.-edit-and-customize-components)

3\. Edit & Customize Components


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#a.-editing-existing-components)

a. Editing Existing Components

Click any component (e.g., Welcome Message) to edit its content.

Update text, add your brand name, customize buttons, and click **Save**.

To view the brief details about the component , view this link:

[Components in Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#b.-create-reorder-chat-flow)

b. Create/Reorder Chat Flow

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fw8fmRIxZEtjRz0iGgJpK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27994bf5-e070-4734-ab7f-5c6badac9443&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fdf5e27b&sv=2)

This section visually represents your chatbot conversation as a **top-to-bottom flow**. Each block represents a message, question, or action that the bot performs.

You can:

*   Add new components
    
*   Reorder existing messages
    
*   Duplicate or delete steps
    
*   Control the conversation sequence without writing code
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#c.-adding-components-to-the-flow)

c. Adding Components to the Flow

To add a new step in the conversation:

1.  Click the **➕ (Plus)** icon between components.
    
2.  Select a component from the **Add Chat Component** panel on the left.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FedcE068dGUopmpYLW201%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50daaa42-edac-4502-99dc-17661b2aa2a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=138f5166&sv=2)

1.  The component is instantly added to the flow.
    

Available components include:

*   Message
    
*   Phone Number
    
*   Email
    
*   Name
    
*   Text Question
    
*   Single Choice / Multiple Choice
    
*   Trigger Actions (Live Chat, Assign Chat, Redirect, AI Response)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#d.-reordering-chat-flow)

d. Reordering Chat Flow

You can easily rearrange the flow to match your desired conversation order.

**How to reorder:**

*   Drag and move components up or down
    
*   Place them between existing blocks using the dotted layout grid
    

> 🔁 Reordering updates the execution sequence automatically.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F73gBDVgHoyUA4WQxsg79%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaa700a5-b9da-4670-b14d-8c1433869171&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8775599&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#e.-duplicating-and-deleting-components)

e. Duplicating & Deleting Components

Each component includes quick action icons:

*   **Duplicate** – Creates a copy of the selected component
    
*   **Delete** – Removes the component from the flow
    

Use duplication to quickly reuse similar messages or questions.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQvlvdUxD91RuOggpL2cX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da54b5760-cc60-4e78-8aa7-fd3f313c88ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b08cb4f1&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#connecting-the-flow)

Connecting the Flow

Each component can be linked to the next step using:

*   **Go to next message** (from Customize settings)
    
*   Conditional logic using **If/Else Branch**
    
*   Actions like **Assign Chat** or **Redirect**
    

This ensures users are guided smoothly without confusion or dead ends.

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#id-4.-ending-the-chat-flow)

4\. Ending the Chat Flow


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To finalize your flow:

1.  Go to the last component.
    
2.  In **Go to next message**, select **End Chat**.
    

⚠️ **Important:**

> The flow must end with **End Chat** to avoid system errors or incomplete conversations.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FqRLW2BFLwSJuvtXIVbiA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71aaeeda-2061-4926-aa7e-ee61913fe271&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e975b6a&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow#how-to-transfer-flows-between-bots)

How to Transfer Flows Between Bots


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Good news—you don’t need to rebuild your flow from scratch!

To transfer flows from one bot to another doesn't require complete reconstruction, it just needs some BotPenguin magic! Use the "Download chatflow" button to download your flows, and import them into the new bots!

circle-info

Chats cannot be transferred between different kinds of bot. A website bot flow can only be transferred to another website bot

* * *

If everything looks correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

* * *

# Multiple Flows (Redirect Component) | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#multiple-flows-redirect-component)

Multiple Flows (Redirect Component)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page explains how to create multiple flows within your Website Bot and connect them using the **Redirect** component. With multiple flows, you can build modular conversations and trigger different flows based on user interactions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#creating-a-trigger-flow)

Creating a Trigger Flow

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#id-1.-create-a-new-flow)

1\. Create a New Flow

1.  Click on the Bots and Select your bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FjFWBpHJVlOtZyp0zYRQs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8cee412-4611-463f-8f7a-46385b3f3a87&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3a59f5b&sv=2)

1.  Click on the Chatflow tab from the expanded menu.
    
2.  Select the flow you want to edit or create a new flow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FcVaXt8w7YwxGqnUBOe5n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfffe16f5-571d-4990-b02f-e8a88434bd03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71775876&sv=2)

1.  Select your pre-created chatbot from the list (you can also search by name).
    
2.  Configure this new flow as needed—it will now appear in your list of available flows.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#setting-up-a-redirect-in-an-existing-flow)

Setting Up a Redirect in an Existing Flow

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#id-1.-open-the-previous-flow)

1\. Open the Previous Flow

*   Go to the flow from which you want to trigger your newly created flow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F9PlkC7fZlTb1Ji7YBG3Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8906d0f6-a3a5-4c5a-a317-6382f6543279&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d2f7590&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#id-2.-add-the-redirect-component)

2\. Add the Redirect Component

*   Insert the **Redirect** component into the chat flow.
    
*   From the dropdown inside the component, select the flow you want the conversation to jump to.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fd6iBrq28HdsMKzs7DVfd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148f5360-5431-41e1-8d34-6204ea72559f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9489aa1f&sv=2)

*   Select the Chatflow to connect next.
    
*   And after this flow the flow will be redirected to the next selected Chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FXyYv5A737WYgoUF0Mzj7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64e8b3c7-3fc4-4187-9129-448c37ca7329&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38cc907&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#how-flow-redirection-works)

How Flow Redirection Works

When the redirect component is triggered during a conversation, the bot will seamlessly move to the selected flow. This lets you:

*   Break complex conversations into smaller, manageable flows
    
*   Create personalized conversation paths
    
*   Build dynamic, flexible chatbot interactions across your website
    

Using multiple flows and redirect connections helps you structure conversations more efficiently and deliver a smoother experience for users.

[PreviousCreate Chatflowchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/create-chatflow)
[NextComponents in Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow)

Last updated 16 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Multiple Flows (Redirect Component)](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#multiple-flows-redirect-component)
    
*   [Creating a Trigger Flow](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#creating-a-trigger-flow)
    
*   [Setting Up a Redirect in an Existing Flow](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#setting-up-a-redirect-in-an-existing-flow)
    
*   [How Flow Redirection Works](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/multiple-flows-redirect-component#how-flow-redirection-works)

# Components in Chatflow | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

There are different chat components which can be used in chat and have different use cases.

Some components are used to:

chevron-rightRequest Information[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#request-information)

> Note: Flow will not move ahead until the user gives the requested information to the bot.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-1.-name)

1\. Name

*   It is used to request "name" as information from the user.
    
*   Click on "Name" from the Add Chat Component.
    
*   Then you can customize the name request message from the customize bot message.
    

**Use Case:** In case of entering the user’s name, this component is used to request the **name** as input from the user.

![Name](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUQGppXQ9Fduln1puS91z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28435dc4-3fc7-41e9-8d4d-39b033a47287&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b621889f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-2.-phone-number)

2\. Phone Number

*   It is used to request a "phone number" as information from the user.
    
*   Click on "Phone Number" to add into your flow.
    
*   Then you can customize the phone number request message from customize bot message.
    
*   You can also select a specific country code for the same by clicking on the drop down.
    

**Use Case:** In case of collecting the user’s phone number, this component is used to request a **valid phone number** from the user.

![Phone number](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FehZEbuUyZvFFOBAvURfg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05d09def-d578-487c-a606-160cebffa6d6&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7d9aae7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-3.-email)

3\. Email

*   It is used to request "Email" as information from the user.
    
*   Click on "Email" to add it in your flow.
    
*   You can customize the email request message from the customize bot message panel.
    

**Use Case:** In case of collecting the user’s email address, this component is used to request an **email** from the user.

![Email](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnSIJuqle4hMvqmPAowLJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d7d497b-ea14-4270-9d5c-b1513969dd54&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d7001a9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-4.-single-choice)

4\. Single Choice

*   It is used to give a single choice selection request from the user.
    
*   Click on "Single Choice" to add it in your flow.
    
*   You can customize the message, title for your options and link the next component with them.
    
*   You can add up to 5 options.
    

**Use Case:** In case the user needs to select **only one option** from multiple choices, this component is used.

![Single Choice](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FkqtCgtZWdQQmQTNk8S1w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ac71012-b1d2-4b88-b1a3-25bc71bd80dd&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d70f8c5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-5.-multiple-choice)

5\. Multiple Choice

*   It is used to give a multiple choice selection request from the user.
    
*   Click on "Multiple Choice" to add it in your flow.
    
*   You can customize the message, title for your options and link the next component with them.
    
*   You can add up to 5 options.
    

**Use Case:** In case the user needs to select **more than one option**, this component is used.

![Multiple Choice](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVPYCeUp5dDelatCcdTq4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df13deee7-1475-4cf3-ae8f-67fc2aae748f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95fc0047&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-6.-text-questions)

6\. Text Questions

*   It is used to request "any answer" as information from the user.
    
*   Click on "Text Question" to add it in your flow.
    
*   You can customize the information request message to ask for an answer from the user accordingly.
    

**Use Case:** In case you need a **custom or open-ended answer** from the user, this component is used.

![Text Question](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fckf4AlhL3OyKzD6pdUYF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b89e118-5e45-442e-a3e2-a16540183dc4&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81ee066d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-7.-file-upload)

7\. File Upload

*   It is used to request a "file, image or video" as information from the user.
    
*   Click on "File" to add it in your flow.
    
*   You can customize the file request message from the right panel.
    

**Use Case:** In case you need the user to upload a **file, image, or video**, this component is used.

![File](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FXF64pMgSfK1qVsYWyoOJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De309fc36-7ad3-407b-943d-643223224dac&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73bd1e4b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-8.-iframe)

8\. Iframe

It is used to create an iframe.

*   You can add a text message about iframe you are adding.
    
*   Paste the URL for the web page.
    
*   Give a title to the iframe.
    
*   Add a CTA button on which user can click and can be redirected.
    
*   Once clicked web page will be opened.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to display an **external webpage or embedded content** inside the chat, this component is used.

![iframe](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F48ybLZSwEQiUP6PdhhPH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D492b5484-f6fd-4b11-bf92-2afc62094a30&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1aaf7bc3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-9.-appointment)

9\. Appointment

The **Appointment component** allows you to let users book appointments directly through the chatbot by connecting it with your calendar provider (such as Google Calendar). It automates date selection, time slot availability, and event creation, making appointment scheduling seamless for both users and businesses.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#what-is-the-appointment-component)

What is the Appointment Component?

The Appointment component enables your chatbot to:

*   Show available dates and time slots to users
    
*   Book appointments in real time
    
*   Create events directly in your connected calendar
    
*   Collect attendee details automatically (Name, Email, Phone)
    

This component is ideal for appointment booking, consultations, demos, service scheduling, and support calls.

**Use Case:** In case you want users to **book an appointment or time slot**, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FzK55HSNze7v7p9WuZgcS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De76f76b3-90ff-4a24-82dc-4982e30d0617&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3ae7331&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-10.-location)

*   You can enter a message text to request the same and checkbox to show time selection option.
    
*   User will get option in calendar to select the date and exact time for that date.
    

**Use Case:** In case you need the user to select a **date or date with time**, this component is used.

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-13.-range)

13\. Range

It is used to ask user a range according to the requirements.

*   You can enter a text message for the same.
    
*   Add a prefix and suffix text to be used in range.
    
*   Then select the starting point and highest point to be selected in the range.
    
*   You can also select a step you want to use as gap in the range slider.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want users to select a value **within a specific range**, this component is used.

![Range](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FclwRHd0oxJMo3RKf5tZv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7703e040-b690-425e-b4d3-adee39e3daa5&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6820b860&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-15.-smart-question)

15\. Smart Question

It is used to ask user answer according to which the next chat flow will be decided.

*   You can enter a text message or your question.
    
*   Then enter keywords based on which next chat component will be selected.
    
*   You can select smart keyword match type, it can be either exact or the keywords should be present in the answer.
    
*   You can add multiple smart keywords.
    

**Use Case:** In case the next flow depends on the user’s **textual answer**, this component is used.

![Smart Questions](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMROeUSYRWqlrvidZKVBS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9228dc7e-5906-455b-9a9e-bf27e8b84c88&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1c003d6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-16.-redirect)

16\. Redirect

*   It is used to start a new flow which is created for this same bot.
    
*   You can enter a text message and select the pre-build chat flow from the drop down.
    
*   Once the component is triggered, the other selected chatflow will continue in the chat.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **move the user to another pre-built chat flow**, this component is used.

![Redirect](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Ftr8LQxaPTUTfSdFllRcd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45a4a2d7-c070-4b2c-8d45-be9f8ff95c2c&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cf715f7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-17.-api)

17\. API

It is used to use a third party integration in chat flow.

*   You can select the API.
    
*   You can then add text to response code and select the next message.
    
*   Response Code 200 is for success and 400 is for error.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **connect a third-party system** within the chat flow, this component is used.

You can also check DEVELOPERS section for more information.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F5qsKD9MCcaV5O26iuy1P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D973cff60-1f8e-4739-a65b-f9390612ee5d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c494d75&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-1.-message)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-3.-video)

3\. Video

It is used to send a video message in the chat flow.

*   You can enter a text message to be sent along with the video.
    
*   Add a video link or upload it from your device.
    

Size of the video should not be more than 15 MB.

**Use Case:** In case you want to send a **video message** to the user, this component is used.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-4.-web-link)

4\. Web Link

It is used to send a web link in the chat.

*   You can enter a text message which you want to send along with the link.
    
*   You have to select the platform from the drop down for which you are adding the link.
    
*   Also add a title for the link and insert the URL. You can add multiple links.
    
*   When user clicks on the title they will be redirected on the page.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to redirect the user to a **website or external page**, this component is used.

![Web Link](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0KfmfDuYiarTNENKf2Be%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0163409c-1bca-4ad6-8466-cefb3e3cbcd5&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=918b1ad7&sv=2)

chevron-rightTrigger Actions[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#trigger-actions)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-1.-live-chat)

1\. Live Chat

It is used to initiate live chat with your available agent.

*   It will create a live chat request.
    
*   You can enter a text message that will inform user that request has been triggered.
    
*   Also by clicking on "Manage Team" you will be redirected to Team's Section where you can assign roles and manage your team.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **connect the user with a live agent**, this component is used to initiate a live chat request.

![Live Chat](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fpc3PdmVAwKGOf17ArJuS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ebff4eb-2d62-4848-a235-38f609a9839d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17c5cbfb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-2.-chat-gpt)

2\. Chat GPT

It is used to trigger AI in chat flow.

*   You can enter the first message that will be sent before starting the AI generated questions.
    
*   Select the number of queries to be resolved using AI.
    
*   If query suggestion box is checked. You have to provide up to 3 chat suggestions that will be used initially.
    
*   After that, ChatGPT will provide query suggestions based on the prompt you will enter.
    
*   You can also train your AI and the query suggestions and replies will be based on that.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **trigger AI-powered conversations** inside the chat flow, this component is used.

![Chat GPT](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FK7JYxfbRk8v6oF6yCai3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75865db8-4482-4b01-8b39-a09801738a4b&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0d2af8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-3.-assign-chat)

3\. Assign Chat

It is used to automatically assign live chat request among team members.

*   You can either assign to a team member and then select his/her name. or
    
*   You can assign by department, then select the department and assignment logic will be set to "Round Robin" in which every team member will be automatically assigned a live chat request one by one in a round.
    
*   You can select not to assign to offline agents and assign to agents only in business hours.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **automatically assign live chat requests** to team members, this component is used.

![Assign Chat](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMHroidLyUrVq0xvYdvIZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1a97369-02d8-431d-a40f-2bb4733e5ce6&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cbc8bc57&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-4.-if-else-branch)

4\. If/Else Branch

It is used to make decisions based on user inputs or other conditions and according to that condition is applied and the next component in flow will be sent.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F1t3Nd1FyeXCFrKmLbnTp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da25bafaf-26b9-4287-bb5e-fb1423f6ed20&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36a1c5f7&sv=2)

*   By clicking on "Please select a condition" or "Add If/Else Branch".
    
*   You can select Visitor's Response, Custom Attribute, Contact Property and Chat Property to apply conditions on.
    
*   Conditions can be equal, not equal, greater than or less than
    
*   Then add a value with which conditions will be compared
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8c2U4me6xlPuFNYtMLnP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e0153de-0a14-4b5a-aa65-6859a846ed39&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14b00bb0&sv=2)

*   You can click on "+" to add "AND" condition or you can click on "Add OR condition" to add the same.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want the conversation to **change based on user input or conditions**, this component is used.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#id-5.-redirect)

5\. Redirect

It is used to create multiple flows within your Website Bot and connect them using the **Redirect** component. With multiple flows, you can build modular conversations and trigger different flows based on user interactions.

**Use Case:** In case you want to **connect or trigger another chat flow** within the same bot, this component is used.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#using-go-to-next-message)

Using go to next message

This setting is available in every component which helps to connect components and create a flow. You can click on the drop down and select which chat component you want to send after.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FE4vkvErQCTCilwSXMeBQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3b4f2a1-7682-4647-8be5-7ca0d3ca8c6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aad9a917&sv=2)

Go to next message

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow#using-custom-variables-in-message)

Using Custom Variables in message

This setting is available in message under customization settings. Type "/" in message customize box and a drop down will be shown from which you can select your pre-built variables.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVBdkofJdIj06VwEziYOw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a6c9f91-490c-41d5-bafe-494f921ab6fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=83192b6a&sv=2)

# Send Information | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#id-1.-message)

1\. Message

*   It is used to send the information message to the user.
    
*   Select the "Message" component under send information.
    
*   You can add a text message which you want to send as information in the customize section.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to send an **informational message** to the user, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPLUzWb26vtkh0dCX4Lv6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b218c2f-ddee-4223-8c55-7c16e61cd07f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2164d421&sv=2)

Message

chevron-right**Advanced Settings (Message)**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#advanced-settings-message)

The **Advanced** tab for the Message component lets you fine-tune how and when a message is delivered in the chat flow. These settings help improve clarity, pacing, and conversational quality.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#rephrase-messages)

Rephrase Messages

When enabled, the chatbot can automatically rephrase the message if needed to improve clarity or natural language flow.

**Use this when:**

*   You want the message to sound more conversational
    
*   The same message may appear in different contexts
    
*   You want to avoid repetitive or robotic phrasing
    

> 💡 Best suited for greeting messages, guidance text, and instructional messages.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#add-delay-before-message)

Add Delay Before Message

Adds a delay (in seconds) before the message is displayed to the user.

**Why this is useful:**

*   Makes conversations feel more human
    
*   Prevents messages from appearing too quickly
    
*   Improves readability in multi-step flows
    

**Recommended values:**

*   `1–2 seconds` → Natural conversation pacing
    
*   `3+ seconds` → Emphasis before important information
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#best-practices-for-message-advanced)

Best Practices for Message (Advanced)

*   Add small delays between consecutive messages to avoid overwhelming users
    
*   Enable **Rephrase Messages** for welcome and help texts
    
*   Keep delays short for transactional or time-sensitive flows
    
*   Use consistent timing across similar messages for a smooth experience
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRSiSHW5pKvkGfAU4TIyP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da86ea145-3474-4bb2-99b9-554d19cf3d11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ad881b6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#id-2.-image-gif)

2\. Image/GIF

It is used to send a GIF or an Image.

*   You can add a text message for your image or GIF.
    
*   Select "Image/GIF" from the send information section.
    
*   Add the text message you want to send along with the image/GIF.
    
*   To send a GIF, search for it by name in the GIF section.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUyokK82qZmg13OtFty6v%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56642d44-47f4-433f-9bd8-7de9461f6a6d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d290128e&sv=2)

GIF

*   Or you can scroll down and upload an image from your device or paste the URL of the image.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to send an **image or GIF** to the user, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMl641RmlmJPI6f7mKqt0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2dcde299-0fba-409b-99a0-5e5f54e4b49b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2313f262&sv=2)

Image

chevron-rightAdvanced Settings (Image / GIF)[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#advanced-settings-image-gif)

The **Advanced** tab for the Image/GIF component lets you control how media is displayed, described, and timed within the chat flow. These options help improve accessibility, clarity, and conversation pacing.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#show-media-caption)

Show Media Caption

When enabled, a text caption is displayed along with the image or GIF.

**Use this when:**

*   You want to explain what the image shows
    
*   You need to add context or instructions
    
*   You want better accessibility for users
    

**Examples of captions:**

*   “Here’s how to reset your password”
    
*   “Sample product image”
    
*   “Step 2: Select your plan”
    

> 💡 Captions are especially helpful for instructional images and support flows.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#rephrase-messages-1)

Rephrase Messages

When enabled, the chatbot can automatically rephrase the accompanying text message to sound more natural or conversational.

**Use this when:**

*   The image is reused in multiple flows
    
*   You want to avoid repetitive or robotic captions
    
*   The message is informational rather than transactional
    

**Not recommended when:**

*   The caption contains exact instructions or compliance text
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#add-delay-before-message-1)

Add Delay Before Message

Adds a delay (in seconds) before the image or GIF is displayed.

**Why this matters:**

*   Creates a natural pause before visual content
    
*   Prevents media from appearing too abruptly
    
*   Improves readability when multiple messages appear in sequence
    

**Recommended values:**

*   `1–2 seconds` → Smooth, natural pacing
    
*   `3+ seconds` → Emphasis before important visuals
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#best-practices-for-image-gif-advanced)

Best Practices for Image/GIF (Advanced)

*   Always enable **Show Media Caption** for clarity and accessibility
    
*   Keep captions short and descriptive
    
*   Use small delays to improve conversation flow
    
*   Avoid rephrasing captions that contain step-by-step instructions
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2JcJ40vuW78arWB9bZlc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98299a5f-eeb0-4638-851e-be52cf1aca89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc63463&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#id-3.-video)

3\. Video

It is used to send a video message in the chat flow.

*   You can enter a text message to be sent along with the video in the customize message menu.
    
*   You can add a video link or upload it from your device.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to send a **video message** to the user, this component is used.

circle-exclamation

Size of the video should not be more than 15 MB

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FXTNkDfCK9mqGdgWvQxOO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd7c256d-8a43-48e9-9e6f-312b236361e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e70a8b&sv=2)

Video

chevron-right**Advanced Settings (Video)**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#advanced-settings-video)

The **Advanced** tab for the Video component lets you control how videos are presented, described, and timed within your chat flow. These options help ensure videos are shown with proper context and smooth conversational pacing.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#show-media-caption-1)

Show Media Caption

When enabled, a text caption is displayed along with the video.

**Use this when:**

*   You want to explain what the video is about
    
*   You are sharing tutorials, demos, or walkthroughs
    
*   You need to guide users on what to watch for
    

**Example captions:**

*   “Watch this quick demo to get started”
    
*   “Here’s a short video explaining our pricing”
    
*   “Step-by-step setup guide”
    

> 💡 Captions improve clarity and accessibility, especially for first-time users.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#rephrase-messages-2)

Rephrase Messages

When enabled, the chatbot may automatically rephrase the video’s accompanying message to sound more natural or conversational.

**Use this when:**

*   The same video is used across multiple flows
    
*   You want a friendly, less repetitive tone
    
*   The caption is informational rather than instructional
    

**Avoid enabling if:**

*   The caption contains precise instructions or compliance-related wording
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#add-delay-before-message-2)

Add Delay Before Message

Adds a delay (in seconds) before the video message appears in the chat.

**Why this helps:**

*   Prepares users for rich media content
    
*   Prevents sudden or overwhelming transitions
    
*   Improves readability in multi-step flows
    

**Recommended values:**

*   `1–2 seconds` → Natural conversational pacing
    
*   `3+ seconds` → Emphasis before important or longer videos
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#best-practices-for-video-advanced)

Best Practices for Video (Advanced)

*   Always include a clear caption explaining the purpose of the video
    
*   Keep captions short and action-oriented
    
*   Use small delays to improve user experience
    
*   Avoid rephrasing captions with strict or time-sensitive instructions
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRltzupxRwLjflZRITNrm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2db43721-dc9c-480d-8070-9af7b5190860&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36267485&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#id-4.-web-link)

4\. Web Link

It is used to send a web link in the chat.

*   You can enter a text message to send along with the link.
    
*   Select the platform from the dropdown for which you are adding the link.
    
*   Also, add a title for the link and insert the URL.
    
*   You can add multiple links. When the user clicks on the title, they will be redirected to the page.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to redirect the user to a **website or external page**, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0KfmfDuYiarTNENKf2Be%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0163409c-1bca-4ad6-8466-cefb3e3cbcd5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=918b1ad7&sv=2)

Web Link

chevron-right**Advanced Settings (Web Link)**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#advanced-settings-web-link)

The **Advanced** tab for the Web Link component lets you control how external links are presented and timed within the chat flow. These options help ensure links are shared clearly and at the right moment in the conversation.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#rephrase-messages-3)

Rephrase Messages

When enabled, the chatbot may automatically rephrase the message text associated with the web link to make it sound more natural or conversational.

**Use this when:**

*   The same link is reused in multiple flows
    
*   You want a friendly, less repetitive tone
    
*   The link is informational or supportive in nature
    

**Avoid enabling if:**

*   The message contains exact wording (legal, compliance, or instructions)
    
*   The link text must remain unchanged
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#add-delay-before-message-3)

Add Delay Before Message

Adds a delay (in seconds) before the web link message is displayed.

**Why this is useful:**

*   Prepares users before sharing an external link
    
*   Prevents the link from appearing too abruptly
    
*   Improves readability in multi-step conversations
    

**Recommended values:**

*   `1–2 seconds` → Natural conversational pacing
    
*   `3+ seconds` → Emphasis before important or critical links
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/send-information#best-practices-for-web-link-advanced)

Best Practices for Web Link (Advanced)

*   Use clear, action-oriented link text (e.g., “Visit our pricing page”)
    
*   Add a short delay before important external links
    
*   Avoid rephrasing when sharing official URLs or policies
    
*   Keep link messages concise and purposeful
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJjiuOt0e4SyR3x48BgmS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb41f7d0-368a-405c-8fd6-7395e5bdedb1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a144aec&sv=2)

# Sending Emoji's On BotPenguin | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#what-are-emojis-in-chatflow)

What are Emoji's in Chatflow


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Emojis add personality, tone, and emotional context to your chatbot conversations. They help make the bot feel more human and engaging, especially when used for greetings, confirmations, prompts, or feedback messages.

In BotPenguin, you can add emojis directly to **message blocks**, **options**, **buttons**, and even **quick replies** across any chatbot flow.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#where-to-use-emojis)

Where to Use Emoji's?

You can use emojis in the following components of your chatbot:

*   **Text Message Blocks**
    
*   **Option Buttons**
    
*   **Quick Replies**
    
*   **Welcome Messages**
    
*   **Error or Fallback Messages**
    
*   **Thank You/Confirmation Blocks**
    
*   **Broadcasts**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#how-to-add-emojis-in-your-chatflow)

How to Add Emoji's in your Chatflow:

1.  Log in to your account at [https://app.botpenguin.comarrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
    
2.  Select the chatbot you want to edit, and navigate to the specific flow you want to modify.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FruBKwEX1YZAoKcqW74Ev%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5af10d6e-9b78-4589-b359-d04af271e6d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af8ea3fd&sv=2)

1.  Select the Chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FzE94rsEVT2mwqYoXxqDK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b1aa83d-6fe4-44bd-9453-938ce2bf9627&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a6022e&sv=2)

1.  Click on the message block (Text, Option, Button, etc.)
    
2.  In the text editor, place your cursor where you want to insert the emoji
    
3.  Add the emoji using one of the following methods:
    
    *   **Windows:** Press `Windows Key + .` to open the emoji picker
        
    *   **Mac:** Press `Control + Command + Space` to open the emoji picker
        
    *   **Alternate Method:** Go to [https://emojipedia.orgarrow-up-right](https://emojipedia.org/)
        , copy the emoji, and paste it into the text field
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FTlPkM7u3x3jwY3UKdSih%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61e7143c-d7e2-4b0b-a531-82d2c1780796&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55b93234&sv=2)

1.  Test your flow in to confirm the emoji displays correctly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#best-practices)

Best Practices:

*   ✅ Use emojis to make replies friendly and expressive (e.g., 👍, 😊, 🎉)
    
*   ✅ Place emojis **after or before** key phrases to improve visibility
    
*   ✅ Limit emoji use in formal flows or B2B support bots
    
*   ❌ Avoid using too many emojis in a single message—it may look unprofessional
    
*   ❌ Do not replace important words with emojis—always keep the meaning clear
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#example-use-cases)

Example Use Cases

Use Case

Message

Welcome Message

"Hi there! 👋 Welcome to our page!"

Confirmation

"Great! Your booking is confirmed ✅"

Feedback Request

"How did we do? 😊 Let us know!"

Error Message

"Oops! Something went wrong ❌"

Thank You Note

"Thanks for chatting with us 🙌"

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#faqs)

FAQ's

chevron-rightEmoji not showing properly[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#emoji-not-showing-properly)

Try a different emoji—some are not supported by all devices

chevron-rightEmoji shows as a square or box[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#emoji-shows-as-a-square-or-box)

Ensure the emoji is supported by your OS and browser

chevron-rightCan’t access emoji keyboard[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#cant-access-emoji-keyboard)

Use copy-paste method from [https://emojipedia.orgarrow-up-right](https://emojipedia.org/)

chevron-rightEmoji placement looks awkward[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/sending-emojis-on-botpenguin#emoji-placement-looks-awkward)

Reposition in your sentence for better readability

# Customize your Bot widget | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#what-is-the-design-section)

What is the Design Section

The **Design section** in Website Chatbot Settings allows you to fully customize the visual appearance and layout of your chatbot and its landing page. You can adjust chat window styles, colors, fonts, icons, and landing page content to match your brand identity and create a cohesive experience for your website visitors.

Whether it’s choosing a chat window layout, updating your bot’s theme, or customizing the landing page header and description, the Design section ensures your chatbot looks professional, engaging, and aligned with your brand.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#benefits-of-the-design-section)

Benefits of the Design Section

*   **Brand Consistency:** Ensure your chatbot and landing page reflect your brand’s colors, fonts, and style.
    
*   **Enhanced User Experience:** A visually appealing chat window encourages users to interact with the bot.
    
*   **Flexible Customization:** Update chat window layout, theme, icons, and landing page content easily without coding.
    
*   **Improved Engagement:** Custom call-to-action text, chat bubble styling, and landing page content drive visitor interaction.
    
*   **Quick Updates:** Make changes to the bot’s look and landing page in real-time and save instantly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

To Customize the Website and Landing Page Bot, Please visit these pages:

[Customize Website Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot)
[Customize Landing Page Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#design-faqs)

Design FAQs

chevron-rightCan I customize the chat window layout without coding?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#can-i-customize-the-chat-window-layout-without-coding)

Yes, the Design section provides a visual editor that allows you to select chat window styles, positions, and layouts without any coding knowledge.

chevron-rightHow can I change the chatbot theme colors?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#how-can-i-change-the-chatbot-theme-colors)

You can update the chatbot window, chat background, and landing page theme colors directly in the Design section.

chevron-rightCan I upload a custom bot icon or logo?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#can-i-upload-a-custom-bot-icon-or-logo)

Yes, you can choose from preloaded bot icons or upload your own image to personalize your chatbot.

chevron-rightHow do I customize the landing page content?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#how-do-i-customize-the-landing-page-content)

In the Design section, you can update the landing page name, header, description, toggle visibility for logos or headers, and add social media links.

chevron-rightCan I change the chatbot font style?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#can-i-change-the-chatbot-font-style)

Yes, the Design section allows you to select a font style for the chat window and landing page text to match your branding.

chevron-rightDo I need to save changes manually?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget#do-i-need-to-save-changes-manually)

Yes, after making any customization, click on **Save Changes** to apply updates to the chat window and landing page.
