# Trigger Actions | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-1.-live-chat)

1\. Live Chat

It is used to initiate live chat with your available agent.

*   It will create a live chat request.
    
*   You can enter a text message to inform the user that the request has been triggered.
    
*   By clicking on "Manage Team," you will be redirected to the Team's Section, where you can assign roles and manage your team.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **connect the user with a live agent**, this component is used to initiate a live chat request.

circle-info

Do not set next message to "End Chat" after using the live chat component.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVTIlpSkQrpOkxVrHcGMo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D406051a4-a074-424f-bab2-08359b461801&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5842a97&sv=2)

Live Chat

chevron-right**Advanced Settings (Live chat)**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#advanced-settings-live-chat)

The **Advance** tab allows you to control how bot messages behave after they are sent. These settings help improve response handling, timing, and team collaboration.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#send-notification-for-the-user-reply)

Send Notification for the User Reply

**What it does:** When enabled, your team will receive a notification whenever a user replies to this message.

**Use this when:**

*   You want agents to respond quickly to user messages
    
*   The message expects an important or time-sensitive reply
    
*   Live chat or human handoff is involved
    

**Example use cases:**

*   Sales inquiries
    
*   Support questions
    
*   Appointment or order confirmations
    

✅ Recommended for flows that require human attention.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#rephrase-messages)

Rephrase Messages

**What it does:** Automatically rewrites bot messages to sound more natural, conversational, or context-aware while keeping the original meaning.

**Use this when:**

*   You want messages to feel less scripted
    
*   You are using AI-assisted conversations
    
*   You want tone consistency across the chatbot
    

**Important notes:**

*   The core intent of the message remains unchanged
    
*   Minor wording variations may occur
    
*   Best used for friendly or conversational bots
    

⚠️ Avoid enabling this for legal, compliance, or fixed-copy messages.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#manage-team)

Manage Team

**What it does:** Allows you to manage which team members can receive notifications or take action when users reply.

**You can:**

*   Assign specific agents to handle replies
    
*   Control access to conversations
    
*   Route replies to the correct team (sales, support, etc.)
    

**Use this when:**

*   Multiple team members manage the chatbot
    
*   You want clear ownership of conversations
    
*   Live chat is enabled
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#add-delay-seconds)

Add Delay (Seconds)

**What it does:** Adds a delay before this message is shown to the user.

**Why use a delay:**

*   Makes conversations feel more natural
    
*   Simulates human typing behavior
    
*   Prevents message overload
    

**How it works:**

*   Enter the delay time in seconds
    
*   The message will appear only after the delay
    

**Best practices:**

*   1–2 seconds for short replies
    
*   3–5 seconds for longer or important messages
    
*   Avoid excessive delays that slow down conversations
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#when-to-use-advanced-settings)

When to Use Advanced Settings

Use **Advance settings** when you want to:

*   Improve response handling
    
*   Control message timing
    
*   Involve human agents
    
*   Enhance conversational quality
    

You can leave these settings unchanged if your flow is fully automated.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FhkPAPMPxGJ6V6B0bkMQM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22fddd1e-17c1-41ed-94fa-57edb3b5d663&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37cf1006&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-2.-if-else-branch)

2\. If-Else Branch:

*   Introduces logic-based decision-making in the chatflow.
    
*   Branches the chat base**d on various parameters.**
    
*   Users can set conditions by clicking **"Please choose one"** and selecting a decision rule.
    
*   Additional If-Else branches can be added using the **"Add If/Else Branch"** button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F9jcrVT8kF1KyIpj6k0w3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D462c1fa3-ab7f-427e-a77b-e7fba7f245bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0669ac0&sv=2)

If/Else Branch

*   The available "**Condition On**" options include:
    
    *   **Visitor Response** – Based on the response given by the user to the chat message.
        
    *   **Custom Attribute** – Evaluates the values of custom attributes created by the user.
        
    *   **Contact Property** – Includes standard properties such as name, phone number, email, etc.
        
    *   **Chat Property** – Considers chat-based properties such as tags, status, or weekday.
        
    *   **Team Availability** – Checks whether a team member is currently available of a particular team.
        
    *   **Business Hour Availability** – Determines if the chat occurs within predefined business hours as specified by user.
        
    
*   Conditions can be compared against **fixed values** using the following operators:
    
    *   **Equals** (Exactly matches the given value)
        
    *   **Not Equals** (Does not match the given value)
        
    *   **Is Any Of** (Matches any value from a predefined list)
        
    *   **Is Not Any Of** (Does not match any value from a predefined list)
        
    
*   The value for comparison is entered in the final input box, where users can also incorporate dynamic elements (e.g., user name) or custom attributes by using the **"/"** symbol.
    
*   Additionally, users can define OR conditions using the **"Add OR Condition"** option. This allows for multiple conditions to be evaluated, ensuring flexibility even if the first condition is false.
    
*   Finally, users must **select the next message** to determine the chatflow's progression after a condition is met.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want the conversation to **change based on user input or conditions**, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIeZX7ooAwJI6kx6yRO4b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfac77b5f-faa7-4fe5-96fd-a8ba77223987&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f952583&sv=2)

Customizing If condition

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-3.-ai-agent-previous-chatgpt)

3\. AI Agent (Previous ChatGPT)

It is used to trigger AI in chat flow.

*   You can enter the first message that will be sent before starting the AI-generated questions.
    
*   Select the number of queries to be resolved using AI.
    
*   If the query suggestion box is checked, you must provide up to 3 chat suggestions to be used initially.
    
*   After that, the AI Agent will provide query suggestions based on the prompt you enter.
    
*   You can also train your AI, and the query suggestions and replies will be based on that training.
    
*   Integrate your preferred LLM directly from here using the "AI Provider Integration Required" box
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FEsA7VB84ZYDxl0mkbrU3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45e15360-4194-4189-9055-e2d599b26901&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=126b09f&sv=2)

chevron-right**Advanced Features (AI Message Settings)**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#advanced-features-ai-message-settings)

The **Advanced** tab gives you fine control over how AI messages behave, are tracked, and are delivered to users.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#send-notification-for-the-user-reply-1)

🔔 Send Notification for the User Reply

When enabled, the system sends a notification whenever a user replies to this message. **Use case:**

*   Alert support teams instantly
    
*   Monitor high-intent or important conversations
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#rephrase-messages-1)

✍️ Rephrase Messages

Allows the AI to intelligently rephrase the message before sending it to the user. **Benefits:**

*   More natural and human-like responses
    
*   Avoids repetitive or robotic wording
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#include-in-email-transcript)

📧 Include in Email Transcript

Adds this message and the user’s reply to the email conversation transcript. **Use case:**

*   Conversation history tracking
    
*   CRM or support record keeping
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#use-suggestions-history-for-default-suggestion)

💡 Use Suggestions History for Default Suggestion

Uses past successful suggestions as the default response option. **Benefits:**

*   Smarter AI replies over time
    
*   Improved consistency based on real user interactions
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#enable-disclaimer-for-ai-responses)

⚠️ Enable Disclaimer for AI Responses

Displays a disclaimer with AI-generated replies to set correct user expectations. The default disclaimer shown in the image is:

> _“AI can make mistakes. Check important info.”_

**Best for:**

*   Legal compliance
    
*   Transparency and trust
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#add-message-delay)

⏱️ Add Message Delay

Add a delay (in seconds) before this message is displayed. **Benefits:**

*   Creates a more human typing effect
    
*   Improves conversational flow and realism
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#ai-provider-llm-integration-required)

🤖 AI Provider (LLM) Integration Required

This section indicates that an AI provider (such as **ChatGPT**) must be connected to use AI responses.

**What it enables:**

*   Context-aware replies
    
*   Natural language understanding
    
*   Dynamic, personalized conversations
    

The **“Integrate Now”** button allows instant setup.

* * *

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8Gin2wvgLkh8qwWDkNFS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda290b3c-5727-485e-b2a4-fac9b90a1c57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c98b923&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-4.-redirect)

4\. Redirect:

The "**Redirect**" component allows for the chat to be transferred between the several flows that the user makes:

*   You can select the chatflow to redirect to through the drop-down menu and selecting the desired chat.
    
*   Upon reaching this component, the chat will go to the starting point of the selected chat.
    

chevron-right**Advanced Features – Redirect**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#advanced-features-redirect)

The **Redirect** action sends users from the current step to another chat flow. The **Advanced** settings control how flexible and natural that transition feels.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#allow-back)

🔙 Allow Back

Allows the visitor to return to the previous step after being redirected.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Lets users recover if they enter the wrong flow
    
*   Improves navigation in complex chat journeys
    
*   Reduces frustration and drop-offs
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#allow-visitor-to-skip)

⏭️ Allow Visitor to Skip

Lets users skip the redirect and continue with the current flow instead.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Ideal when the redirect is optional
    
*   Keeps users in control of their experience
    
*   Prevents forced navigation
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#add-redirect-delay)

⏱️ Add Redirect Delay

Adds a delay (in seconds) before the redirect happens.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Gives users time to read the last message
    
*   Creates a smooth, human-like transition
    
*   Avoids abrupt flow changes
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#seamless-flow-switching)

🔁 Seamless Flow Switching

When used with **If/Else Branch** or **User Reply**, Redirect can:

*   Send users to the right flow automatically
    
*   Handle FAQs, sales, or support separately
    
*   Scale complex journeys without duplication
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#common-use-cases)

🎯 Common Use Cases

*   Redirect users to **Live Chat**
    
*   Move users into a **product-specific flow**
    
*   Route visitors based on intent or responses
    
*   Send users to onboarding or checkout flows
    

* * *

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3ptfiG4qbuq0er2cAbKG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1e05dda-48b2-4314-87eb-03be828bcb67&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3fa4ffa0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-5.-payment)

5\. Payment

The **Payment Component** allows your chatbot to collect payments from users directly within the chat flow. It provides a smooth and secure way to accept payments for products, services, subscriptions, or donations without redirecting users to external pages.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#use-case)

Use case:

*   Collect payments via supported payment gateways (Razorpay, Stripe, PayPal, etc.).
    
*   Accept both one-time and recurring payments.
    
*   Send payment links, invoices, or QR codes directly in chat.
    
*   Track payment status (success, failure, or pending).
    
*   Customize messages and instructions for a personalized experience.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#how-to-use)

How to Use

1.  **Add the Payment Component**
    
    *   Open your bot flow in BotPenguin.
        
    *   Drag and drop the **Payment** component where you want to collect payment.
        
    
2.  **Select Payment Method:** Choose the payment service we are going to use. You have the option to choose between
    
    *   All Pay
        
    *   RazorPay
        
    *   Peach Payments
        
    *   Telr Pay
        
    *   Tilo Pay
        
    
    triangle-exclamation
    
    Make sure to go to the third party integrations and integrate the chosen method in the bot as well! Else, the payment may through unexpected errors.
    
    *   Select Currency: Select the currency of you choice from the dropdown.
        
    *   Payment amount: Enter the amount that needs to be paid. If the amount is variable, we recommend you create a custom attribute that takes in the amount form the user, and use that here.
        
    *   Choosing Flows: Choose the flows to redirect to when the payment is successful and unsuccessful.
        
    
    And that's it! Once you configured the payment gateway as well in the "Third Party Applications", you can start using the "Payments Component" just like any other component.
    
3.  **Customize User Message**
    
    *   Compose the message that will be sent to the user along with the payment request.
        
    *   Example: “Hello \[User Name\], please complete your payment of ₹500 to confirm your order.”
        
    
4.  **Set Payment Actions**
    
    *   **On Payment Success**: Define what happens after a successful payment (e.g., send a confirmation, trigger next component).
        
    *   **On Payment Failure**: Set fallback actions (e.g., retry, notify admin, or provide alternative instructions).
        
    
5.  **Test Your Payment Flow**
    
    *   Test your chatbot using sandbox mode or real accounts to ensure payments are processed correctly and confirmations are sent.
        
    

[WhatsApp Payment Componentschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/whatsapp-payment-components)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FS11JpNQLWAm6AhxjO4Er%252FScreenshot%25202025-12-23%2520at%25201.07.32%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71ec73ea-cc2f-4b39-8a22-2a6d0a598725&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e92f73c&sv=2)

chevron-right**Advanced Features – Payment Component**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#advanced-features-payment-component)

The **Advanced** settings let you control how this message behaves, how it’s tracked, and how it interacts with other system features.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#send-notification-for-the-user-reply-2)

🔔 Send Notification for the User Reply

When enabled, a notification is triggered whenever the user replies to this message.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Alert admins or agents about user activity
    
*   Monitor high-intent messages (pricing, payments, onboarding)
    
*   Improve response time
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#rephrase-messages-2)

✍️ Rephrase Messages

Allows the system or AI to intelligently rephrase this message before sending it.

**Benefits:**

*   Makes messages sound more natural
    
*   Reduces repetition across conversations
    
*   Improves overall conversational tone
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#map-order-attributes)

🧾 Map Order Attributes

Maps user input from this message to order or transaction attributes.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Capture payment-related details
    
*   Store structured data (location, plan type, preferences)
    
*   Enable seamless checkout or order processing
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#add-message-delay-1)

⏱️ Add Message Delay

Adds a delay (in seconds) before this message is displayed to the user.

**Why it’s useful:**

*   Creates a human-like typing pause
    
*   Improves message readability
    
*   Makes conversations feel less robotic
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#works-with-other-flow-actions)

🔗 Works with Other Flow Actions

When combined with **Payment**, **Redirect**, **If/Else Branch**, or **Assign Chat**, this message can:

*   Collect data before payments
    
*   Route users intelligently
    
*   Trigger automated actions
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FcNvETQwTvK0u28Egv6F3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e01b9b3-6a3f-4d2d-8902-0e0bf312b748&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e39825d6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-6.-whatsapp-payment)

6\. Whatsapp Payment

The **WhatsApp Payment Component** allows your chatbot to collect payments directly from users within WhatsApp. This enables seamless transactions without redirecting users to external websites, improving conversion rates and user experience.

**Use Case:**

*   Collect payments via supported payment gateways integrated with WhatsApp.
    
*   Send payment links or QR codes directly in chat.
    
*   Track payment status in real-time.
    
*   Customizable messages and instructions for users.
    
*   Supports multiple currencies (depending on your payment gateway setup).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#how-to-use-1)

How to Use

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#adding-a-whatsapp-payments-step)

Adding a Whatsapp Payments step

1.  In the left panel, open the Trigger Action section.​
    
2.  Drag the “Whatsapp Payments” block into your flow where you want to ask for payment.​
    
3.  Place it after any message that explains the product, price, or offer so users know what they are paying for.​
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#customizing-the-payment-message)

Customizing the payment message

*   Click the “Whatsapp Payments” block in the middle canvas to open its settings on the right.​
    
*   In the Message field, type the text you want users to see (for example, “Complete your payment to confirm your order”).​
    
*   Optionally add an image URL or upload an image (like a product photo or logo) to show with the payment message.​
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#linking-a-payment-configuration)

Linking a payment configuration

1.  In the right panel, open the “Select Payment Configuration” dropdown.​
    
2.  Choose the payment configuration you have already set up in BotPenguin (gateway, amount logic, etc.).​
    
3.  This configuration controls how the payment link or button is generated and processed inside WhatsApp.​
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#routing-after-payment)

Routing after payment

*   Use the “Go to next message” dropdown (bottom-right panel) to pick what message the bot should send after this payment step.​
    
*   Typical next messages include: order confirmation, failure/retry instructions, or a thank-you message.​
    

[WhatsApp Payment Componentschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/whatsapp-payment-components)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F06WjdbErxrHMvYfZz5jj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabbd178f-5009-4784-b48c-75bb6bb8830f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10acb1a1&sv=2)

chevron-right**Advanced Features – Whatsapp Payment Component**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#advanced-features-whatsapp-payment-component)

The **Advanced** settings let you control how this message behaves, how it’s tracked, and how it interacts with other system features.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#send-notification-for-the-user-reply-3)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow/components-in-chatflow/trigger-actions#id-5.-assign-chat)

5\. Assign Chat

It is used to automatically assign live chat request among team members.

*   You can either assign the task to a team member by selecting their name.
    

or

*   You can assign it by department, select the department, and set the assignment logic to "Round Robin," where each team member will be automatically assigned a live chat request one by one in a round.
    
*   You can choose not to assign tasks to offline agents and assign them only during business hours.
    

**Use Case:** In case you want to **automatically assign live chat requests** to team members, this component is used.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZ4KDnWSqaggwairj5i6l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D769b4e0b-e825-4dbf-8ff1-89a55b0c61ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=784b4215&sv=2)

Assign Chat

# Transfer Chat to WhatsApp Functionality | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window/transfer-chat-to-whatsapp-functionality#chat-transfer-to-whatsapp)

Chat Transfer to Whatsapp


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click on bots and select a website bot.
    
2.  Click on Settings
    
3.  Click on "Chat Window" tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F5rH39DljhrMfVbSImXd4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c856d8a-6295-477b-a0a6-6a679198b665&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b053af4&sv=2)

1.  You can toggle ON/OFF "Enable Transfer to WhatsApp" button. Once switched ON, user can select to transfer chat to whatsapp.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FERAhX3K9AYUeimXLDndC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2428071a-7948-452f-8222-9afefc712e11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79b26b6b&sv=2)

1.  Now while chatting with a Website bot, user can click on three dots and select "Transfer to Whatsapp". As shown below
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FfK6rfQHDVjuHW2wi434a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5998cefe-b063-4b5a-9ba2-0ff01f34bec4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=572f1843&sv=2)

Chat Window

1.  In the Inbox, a message will be shown indicating that chat has been transferred to whatsapp by the user.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fmbj9PkH0cDkZ4UBEiDFP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D926955ee-ad3f-461d-8791-e43225ff71fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c8c819d&sv=2)

Done! You have completed setting up Transfer Chat to WhatsApp Functionality.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#4e3d3b3e3e213c3a0e2c213a3e2b20293b2720602d2123)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousChat Windowchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window)
[NextAI settingschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings)

Last updated 15 days ago

# Configuring Chatbot Scenarios | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The inputs of users are varying, but certain inputs, such as those which the chatbot cannot provide an answer to, or those that may be offensive, can be configured to give a pre-defined response. This is done through the use of AI, which analyses the input to understand its intent, and responds back with the correct pre-defined response. Additionally, for better organization, you can have different flows. Utilizing the power of artificial intelligence, we can use flow redirection to analyze the users input, and then redirect them to the appropriate flow at any time.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios#steps-for-setup-of-dynamic-chatflow-configuration)

Steps for Setup of Dynamic Chatflow Configuration:

1.  **Create Your Bots**
    

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

1.  **Chatbot Settings**
    

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  **Configure Bot's Personality**
    

*   Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up:
    
*   Go to Configure Bot's personality
    
*   Toggle off "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed option" to create your own AI persona
    

1.  Disable the toggle “Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed”, as we need to customize the responses of our chatbot to certain intents. Then, go to “**Create Persona**”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FEnPBJhXpgL29GTpcuwp0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3a32ef7-1d27-4523-975a-dbcf2c04e613&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37774cda&sv=2)

1.  Upon reaching the main screen here, go to “**Chat Scenarios**”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFi5GE6YY5cHLl9bDsIX7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fbe8e76-5e17-401c-8369-9a5058c55615&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba457cd0&sv=2)

circle-info

If you are configuring the bot for the first time, then the above fields (Persona Details, Communication Style) also need to be filled for the redirection to work.

1.  Click on the “**Add-Action button**” to proceed to the configuration of the chatbot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIBneq4NtNd4AiSWtbDW0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f428c55-33a4-4305-8ba2-12f597a5e846&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61b004de&sv=2)

1.  Complete the form with the relevant details for the bot. The fields to fill are as follows:
    
    1.  **Name**: Specify the name of the chat. This name will be the primary description of the trigger. E.g.: “Flowers” for redirection to flowers chat
        
    2.  **Trigger**: Define the action to be executed when the specified condition is met. Options include triggering a specific message or an entire chat flow.
        
        1.  **Message**: Enter the message to be displayed in the chat.
            
        2.  **Flow**: Select the chat flow to be triggered.
            
        
    3.  Based on the previous Trigger input:
        
        1.  **Message**: Enter the message that is to be displayed when triggered. Eg. If the message is offensive, the response message can be "I am not quite used to this language".
            
        2.  **Flow**: Select the flow onto which the chat should be redirected to.
            
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrwixSwDzxZRv3ACnOhvU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0277fae4-cb39-4353-ad82-62b71d4bf519&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd92805&sv=2)

1.  Click on “**Add Intent**” to finish setup.
    

circle-info

Remember to toggle on the button to enable the message/flow redirection.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZMtBHUlZVH2FckJVGHnJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0cd1380-795d-4765-8aa2-04efffd676c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb504a11&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios#still-not-working-lets-troubleshoot)

Still Not Working? Let's Troubleshoot

If the chat is not responding as expected, consider the following troubleshooting steps:

1.  **Verify Triggers and Conditions**: Ensure that the trigger conditions are correctly set and aligned with the intended message types or user inputs.
    
2.  **Check Message and Flow Settings**: Confirm that the correct message or chat flow is selected and configured properly.
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a8dbddd8d8c7dadce8cac7dcd8cdc6cfddc1c686cbc7c5)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousBasic Configurationchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration)
[NextChatbot Personachevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona)

Last updated 15 days ago

# Train Your AI Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\

Interactive Guide


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot#what-is-train-your-ai-chatbot)

What is Train Your AI Chatbot?

**"Train Your AI Chatbot"** refers to the process of providing your AI chatbot with relevant resources, such as your website, files, Google Sheets, or FAQs. By doing so, you equip your chatbot with the necessary information to effectively answer user queries. This ensures that the responses are accurate and aligned with the data you have provided. Proper training enhances the chatbot's ability to assist users, improving overall user satisfaction and efficiency.

**Navigation:**

1.  Go to Bots.
    
2.  Select the Bot which you want to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

# File Upload | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#what-is-training-via-file-upload)

What is Training via File Upload?

Training your AI chatbot via **File Upload** allows you to provide documents, PDFs, spreadsheets, or other text-based files containing the data your chatbot needs to respond accurately to user queries.

By uploading files:

*   Your chatbot can reference the content directly.
    
*   Responses are aligned with the information in your uploaded resources.
    
*   You ensure consistent and accurate automation of responses.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#benefits-of-file-upload-training)

Benefits of File Upload Training

*   🎯 **Accurate Knowledge Base:** Chatbot learns directly from the content of your files.
    
*   🟢 **Time-Saving:** Upload multiple files at once instead of manually entering data.
    
*   ⚡ **Comprehensive Training:** Support for various file formats, enabling richer context.
    
*   🔧 **Easy Updates:** Add or replace files anytime to update the chatbot’s knowledge.
    
*   📈 **Improved User Experience:** Provides precise and context-aware responses automatically.
    

* * *

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot-on-file-upload)

**How to train your AI Chatbot on File Upload?**

1.  Log into your BotPenguin, and choose the bot you wish to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "**File Upload**' tab to add the file.
    
2.  Click on Add Files option to add a file.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWSoH2y3Fy0wyIzNftJyU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eeca74e-a266-447d-9489-ea775353cad9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44fc2d1c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#file-upload)

File Upload

1.  Click on **“File Upload”** to add the file according to which you want to train your AI Chat Bot.
    
2.  Upload the file from your device.
    
3.  And click on **“Train”** to train your AI Chat Bot with this file.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fy80uWgvO9xIu1VFSxBr7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6fdf2e9-4e32-423d-a7ca-861d866ad240&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f17a55c&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some common FAQ's regarding upload of files:

chevron-rightHow long does it take for the chatbot to start using my uploaded data?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#how-long-does-it-take-for-the-chatbot-to-start-using-my-uploaded-data)

Once your file or website data is uploaded, the system typically marks the training as "complete" within a few seconds to a couple of minutes. After that, your chatbot can start using the data.

chevron-rightWhy does it say "training complete" but responses are still slow?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#why-does-it-say-training-complete-but-responses-are-still-slow)

“Training complete” means the data has been processed and stored. However, depending on the AI model you’re using, it might still take a few minutes to generate smart responses based on that data.

chevron-rightWhich AI model gives the fastest responses after training?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#which-ai-model-gives-the-fastest-responses-after-training)

The GPT-4o model is the fastest — it usually gives responses in under a minute. It’s ideal for speed and efficiency.

chevron-rightWhat’s the difference between GPT-4o and the default Assistant in terms of response time?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#whats-the-difference-between-gpt-4o-and-the-default-assistant-in-terms-of-response-time)

GPT-4o responds almost instantly. The Assistant model (used by default) takes about **2–5 minutes** to fully reflect changes and provide optimized answers from the newly trained data.

chevron-rightWhich model should I use for best results with my uploaded content?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#which-model-should-i-use-for-best-results-with-my-uploaded-content)

For the most accurate and stable responses based on your trained data, we recommend using the **Assistant model**, even though it may take slightly longer to respond.

chevron-rightHow may documents can I train my bot on?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload#how-may-documents-can-i-train-my-bot-on)

There is essentially no limit on the number of documents you can train your bot on. It depends on the size of the document, your plan, and the time taken for the training.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#36454346465944427654594246535851435f581855595b)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousWebsitechevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website)
[NextGoogle Sheetschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets)

# Triggers | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/triggers#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

The **Triggers** section allows you to define when the chatbot should appear on the website or mobile screen.

Here’s how you can configure it:

*   Go to the “Bots” section from the left sidebar.
    
*   Select any website bot
    
*   Select your bot and click on “Settings”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3B5ReW0tKSXREqjUWUjk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D535d89e6-c4b0-434e-94a1-0cde3bf0e17c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7059e934&sv=2)

1.  **Timing for Desktop Trigger**:
    
    *   Set the delay (in seconds) after which the bot should trigger on the desktop screen.
        
    
2.  **Timing for Mobile Trigger**:
    
    *   Set the delay (in seconds) after which the bot should trigger on the mobile screen.
        
    
3.  **Chat Bubble Automatic Opening Behavior**:
    
    *   Choose from the following options using the dropdown:
        
        *   **Always Open After Specified Time**: The bot will trigger automatically based on the timing you’ve set in the fields above.
            
        *   **Automatically After Selected Amount of Time**: If the bot is opened and then closed by the user, it will reopen automatically after the time specified in this field.
            
        *   **Never Open Automatically**: The bot will not open automatically. It will only open if the user clicks on it.
            
        
    
4.  **Disable Trigger Toggles**:
    
    *   Use these toggles to disable the bot’s trigger separately for the desktop screen or mobile screen.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F6pCugecn210Tg7yOlf6K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4939e350-f6be-4c45-8002-704213cdd9ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bcd687b&sv=2)

[PreviousAlertschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/alerts)
[NextUser Accesschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/user-access)

# Customize Landing Page Bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#what-is-the-landing-page-design-section)

What is the Landing Page Design Section

The **Landing Page Design section** in Website Chatbot Settings allows you to fully customize the visual appearance and content of your chatbot’s landing page. You can edit text, headings, descriptions, logos, social media links, layout, chat window style, theme colors, fonts, and background colors to ensure your chatbot’s landing page is visually appealing and aligned with your brand.

Whether it’s updating the landing page header, changing the chatbot icon, or selecting a layout, this section ensures your landing page creates a professional and engaging experience for website visitors.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#benefits-of-the-landing-page-design-section)

Benefits of the Landing Page Design Section

*   **Brand Consistency:** Align the landing page with your brand colors, fonts, and logos.
    
*   **Enhanced User Experience:** A well-designed landing page encourages visitors to interact with your chatbot.
    
*   **Full Customization:** Easily update content, social links, layout, themes, and chat window styles without coding.
    
*   **Improved Engagement:** Custom headings, descriptions, and call-to-action placement help drive more interactions.
    
*   **Quick Updates:** Save and apply changes instantly, ensuring the landing page is always up to date.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

**How to Redirect to the screen:**

1.  Click on Bots from left menu
    
2.  Select any website bot.
    
3.  Click on "Chatbot Design" option from the expanded side panel.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR7o5RAl0plOxPpUuS2DH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b52af5-95cb-4e86-a4b3-53b10ac8a885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73925c5e&sv=2)

1.  User will be redirected to website chatbot screen by default.
    
2.  Select the Landing page Bot Tab.
    
3.  And by default user will be on the Content Tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fch7K9czk8gYbTUZMtjTv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59dc3563-9eac-439f-a4e5-7fd1d376a7aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c65c057&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#content-section)

Content Section


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enter your bot's landing page name in "Landing Page Name" box.
    
2.  Enter the heading text you want to display in "Landing Page Header" box.
    
3.  Enter the description text you want to display in "Landing Page Description" box.
    
4.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide logo and text.
    
5.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide chatbot's header.
    
6.  Upload profile logo for your chatbot page.
    
7.  Add any social media links and icons.
    
8.  And click on "Save Changes" to update all the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FiWM5keI3KePW5AN1AZbA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4e3c802-37bb-4f0d-a42f-bd64fc0699f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7775734a&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#theme)

Theme


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Switch the tab to Theme to change the theme .

1.  Select your chat window style from the given two options.
    
2.  Select a bot icon from the options or upload from your device.
    
3.  Select a landing page theme colour.
    
4.  Select a chat background colour.
    
5.  Select landing page background colour.
    
6.  Select a font style for your chatbot.
    
7.  Click on save changes to upload the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FACCNRPjgDSsFPYgpXqTE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db14b1193-d4f2-4578-8b58-4e7a05775a15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32ff300&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#layout)

Layout


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Here you can select the layout and positioning for your landing page
    
2.  Click on "Save Changes" to save your customizations.
    
3.  These are all the settings you can do to customize your website chatbot if still have queries you can contact us anytime.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fp2lmxwrp6buhq5pyVZZe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D875d2ce9-8b0c-46cb-ae4a-f5d6648979a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3180ab0&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot#need-assistance)

Need Assistance?

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b0c3c5c0c0dfc2c4f0d2dfc4c0d5ded7c5d9de9ed3dfdd)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousCustomize Website Chatbotchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot)
[NextChatbot Settingschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings)

# User Access | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **User Access** section allows you to manage who can access your chatbot. You can configure access based on devices, IP addresses, specific pages, and countries. Here’s how to set it up:

Here’s how you can configure it:

*   Go to the “Bots” section from the left sidebar.
    
*   Select any website bot
    
*   Select your bot and click on “Settings”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3B5ReW0tKSXREqjUWUjk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D535d89e6-c4b0-434e-94a1-0cde3bf0e17c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7059e934&sv=2)

*   Click on User access tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fs51e7f6MgulKcpgESwp5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D800a37bf-843f-4e63-8618-70b79de3d70d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a93a0e76&sv=2)

1.  **Device Selection**:
    
    *   Choose which devices can access the chatbot:
        
        *   Mobile-only
            
        *   Desktop-only
            
        *   All devices
            
        
    
2.  **Block IP Addresses**:
    
    *   Add IP addresses that you want to block from accessing the chatbot.
        
    *   You can enter multiple IP addresses by adding each one and pressing **Enter**.
        
    
3.  **Restrict Chatbot on Specific Pages**:
    
    *   Specify the URLs of pages where you do not want the chatbot to appear.
        
    *   Add multiple URLs by typing them in and pressing **Enter**.
        
    
4.  **Country Selection**:
    
    *   Select the countries where you want the chatbot to be accessible.
        
    *   Use the dropdown to choose one or multiple countries. The chatbot will only appear to users in the selected regions.
        
    
5.  **Save Changes**:
    
    *   Once you’ve configured all the settings, click **Save Changes** to apply your choices.
        
    

[PreviousTriggerschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/triggers)
[NextChat Windowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window)

Last updated 15 days ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Design | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#what-is-the-design-section)

What is the Design Section

The **Design section** in Website Chatbot Settings allows you to fully customize the visual appearance and layout of your chatbot and its landing page. You can adjust chat window styles, colors, fonts, icons, and landing page content to match your brand identity and create a cohesive experience for your website visitors.

Whether it’s choosing a chat window layout, updating your bot’s theme, or customizing the landing page header and description, the Design section ensures your chatbot looks professional, engaging, and aligned with your brand.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#benefits-of-the-design-section)

Benefits of the Design Section

*   **Brand Consistency:** Ensure your chatbot and landing page reflect your brand’s colors, fonts, and style.
    
*   **Enhanced User Experience:** A visually appealing chat window encourages users to interact with the bot.
    
*   **Flexible Customization:** Update chat window layout, theme, icons, and landing page content easily without coding.
    
*   **Improved Engagement:** Custom call-to-action text, chat bubble styling, and landing page content drive visitor interaction.
    
*   **Quick Updates:** Make changes to the bot’s look and landing page in real-time and save instantly.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

To Customize the Website and Landing Page Bot, Please visit these pages:

[Customize Website Chatbotchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot)
[Customize Landing Page Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-landing-page-bot)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#design-faqs)

Design FAQs

chevron-rightCan I customize the chat window layout without coding?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#can-i-customize-the-chat-window-layout-without-coding)

Yes, the Design section provides a visual editor that allows you to select chat window styles, positions, and layouts without any coding knowledge.

chevron-rightHow can I change the chatbot theme colors?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#how-can-i-change-the-chatbot-theme-colors)

You can update the chatbot window, chat background, and landing page theme colors directly in the Design section.

chevron-rightCan I upload a custom bot icon or logo?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#can-i-upload-a-custom-bot-icon-or-logo)

Yes, you can choose from preloaded bot icons or upload your own image to personalize your chatbot.

chevron-rightHow do I customize the landing page content?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#how-do-i-customize-the-landing-page-content)

In the Design section, you can update the landing page name, header, description, toggle visibility for logos or headers, and add social media links.

chevron-rightCan I change the chatbot font style?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#can-i-change-the-chatbot-font-style)

Yes, the Design section allows you to select a font style for the chat window and landing page text to match your branding.

chevron-rightDo I need to save changes manually?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design#do-i-need-to-save-changes-manually)

Yes, after making any customization, click on **Save Changes** to apply updates to the chat window and landing page.

# Chat Window | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#chat-window)

Chat Window

The **Chat Window** settings allow you to customize how your chatbot interface looks and behaves for end users. From live chat options and color themes to restart controls and advanced features, this section helps you create a seamless, branded, and user-friendly chat experience.

Use this page to:

*   Customize bot and agent display labels
    
*   Enable or disable live chat and WhatsApp transfers
    
*   Control chat restart, ratings, and placeholder text
    
*   Configure advanced options like ticketing, knowledge base, and AI streaming
    

All changes made here directly affect how users interact with your chatbot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#navigation)

Navigation:

*   Go to the “Bots” section from the left sidebar.
    
*   Select any website bot
    
*   Select your bot and click on “Settings”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3B5ReW0tKSXREqjUWUjk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D535d89e6-c4b0-434e-94a1-0cde3bf0e17c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7059e934&sv=2)

*   Click on Chat Window tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FremU6zxKxX8GRBDzKGeY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb59e2a8-c64e-4a34-952f-1025edb2eb70&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c58da28&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#section-details)

Section Details

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-1.-indicative-text-for-bot-message)

1\. Indicative Text for Bot Message

Define the label shown for bot messages in the chat window (e.g., _Bot_, _Assistant_, _Support_). This helps users clearly identify automated responses.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-2.-allow-users-to-request-live-chat)

2\. Allow Users to Request Live Chat

Enable this option to allow users to request a conversation with a human agent during the chat.

**Additional settings include:**

*   **Live/Agent Chat Display Name**: The name shown for human agents.
    
*   **Live Chat to Bot Transfer Option**: Controls how chats are transferred back to the bot.
    
*   **Live Chat Request Expiry Time**: Time (in seconds) after which a live chat request expires if not accepted.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-3.-live-chat-message-colors)

3\. Live Chat Message Colors

Customize the appearance of live chat messages:

*   **Primary Color**: Main message bubble color
    
*   **Secondary Color**: Supporting message or UI color
    
*   **Unavailable Color**: Displayed when live agents are unavailable
    

These options help match the chat UI with your brand identity.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-4.-enable-option-to-restart-chat)

4\. Enable Option to Restart Chat

Allow users to restart the conversation at any time.

*   **Restart Chat Menu Option Text**: Text shown for the restart option (e.g., _Restart Chat_, _Start Over_).
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnwOfLIbLyysIaC6xAE3t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De099f5a5-7adc-4d5f-b78c-48edf5cff81e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d1878fd&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-5.-enable-transfer-to-whatsapp)

5\. Enable Transfer to WhatsApp

Allow users to move the conversation from the website chat to WhatsApp.

*   **Transfer Chat to WhatsApp Option Text**: Text displayed for the WhatsApp transfer option.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-6.-enable-rate-the-chat-screen)

6\. Enable Rate the Chat Screen

Enable a rating screen at the end of the conversation to collect user feedback on chat experience.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fgtg7H3qmuwu2Xdlx1cut%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dead85458-1274-4d2e-ba47-e3d3fc6d3ad8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4e8ec07&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-7.-enable-custom-chat-reply-placeholder-text)

7\. Enable Custom Chat Reply Placeholder Text

Customize the placeholder text shown in the chat input field (e.g., _Type your message here…_).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-8.-enable-ticketing-management)

8\. Enable Ticketing Management

Allow users to raise support tickets directly from the chat window for follow-ups and issue tracking.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-9.-enable-knowledge-base)

9\. Enable Knowledge Base

Enable access to your knowledge base so users can view help articles or FAQs within the chat.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-10.-clear-chat-on-reload)

10\. Clear Chat on Reload

Automatically clears the chat history when the page is refreshed.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-11.-clear-chat-on-restart)

11\. Clear Chat on Restart

Clears the previous chat history when the user restarts the conversation.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#id-12.-real-time-ai-response-streaming)

12\. Real-time AI Response Streaming

Enable streaming responses so users can see AI replies appear in real time instead of waiting for the full message.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#save-changes)

Save Changes

Click **Save Changes** to apply all Chat Window customizations. Changes will reflect immediately on the live chatbot.

[PreviousUser Accesschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/user-access)
[NextTransfer Chat to WhatsApp Functionalitychevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window/transfer-chat-to-whatsapp-functionality)

Last updated 17 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Chat Window](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window#chat-window)

# Customize Website Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Website Chatbot Customization** feature allows you to design, style, and configure your chatbot to match your brand and website aesthetics. You can control how it appears, behaves, and interacts with your visitors, ensuring a consistent and engaging user experience.

**How to Redirect to the screen:**

1.  Click on Bots from left menu
    
2.  Select any website bot.
    
3.  Click on "Chatbot Design" option from the expanded side panel.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR7o5RAl0plOxPpUuS2DH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b52af5-95cb-4e86-a4b3-53b10ac8a885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73925c5e&sv=2)

1.  User will be redirected to website chatbot screen by default.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtnSLgwvk45gn5MkWMP1y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19a78e8a-6196-4261-b1af-29fa4d7ff92d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12748702&sv=2)

1.  Automatically user will be on the Content tab.
    
2.  To change the Theme and layout , user will need to switch the tabs.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-website-chatbot#theme)

Content

1.  Select the Content tab.
    
2.  Enter your bot's name in "Bot Name" box.
    
3.  Enter an inviting catch phrase that will make the user talk to bot in "Call to Action" box.
    
4.  Toggle ON/OFF auto hide call to action. If ON select time in seconds after which it will hide.
    
5.  Expand the more section.
    
6.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide CTA Chat Bubble.
    
7.  Select chat bubble background colour from the options.
    
8.  Select chat bubble text colour from the given options.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FoqWZFcn6UBgcC2B2eOna%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcca47966-dcaa-4ad4-827b-0e4a27ff3cfa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b67e389&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-website-chatbot#layout)

Theme

1.  Select your chat window style from the given two options.
    
2.  Select a bot icon from the options or upload from your device.
    
3.  Select a chatbot window theme colour.
    
4.  Select a chat background colour.
    
5.  Select a font style for your chatbot.
    
6.  Select Bot icon position.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FxMCDRymtUpGmqidJtpX2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9684117-c6bb-4ceb-8303-6efdeed9eca7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b92d778&sv=2)

1.  Add the Custom CSS for Advance Designs and add the custom CSS for launcher icon.
    

[pen-paintbrushAdding Custom CSS to Chat Windowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/adding-custom-css-to-chat-window)
[swatchbookCustomizing the Launcher Iconchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/customizing-the-launcher-icon)

1.  Click on save changes to upload the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwlvmwV7jlotBIP2p1QVi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9be243c6-d20d-48f4-9dec-2b11a8041a45&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4c6ab44&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-website-chatbot#layout-1)

Layout

1.  You can select chat window positioning on web.
    
2.  You can select chat window positioning on mobile.
    
3.  You can select chat window size.
    
4.  Click on "Save Changes" to save your customizations.
    

Here you can select the layout and positioning for your landing page

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fw9arDNOoo137w9Pcy66B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7d911c9-7cd1-4deb-a93b-33d6ee6207a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbcbb075&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-website-chatbot#need-assistance)

. We will respond back within 48 business hours.
