# FAQs | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#why-train-the-bot-with-faqs)

Why train the bot with FAQ's?

You can teach your chatbot by adding **FAQs (Frequently Asked Questions)**. Just write common questions your users might ask, and add clear answers. Group similar questions into categories to keep things organized. This helps your bot give faster and better answers. The more helpful questions you add, the smarter your bot becomes over time!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot)

**How to train your AI Chatbot?**

1.  Log into your BotPenguin, and choose the bot you wish to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "FAQs" tab to train on FAQs.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIqgJlC18ptSaTUix4Qz1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3427358-0b5a-4782-8924-17a2514dc412&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9c02a98&sv=2)

1.  Add the FAQs according to which you want to train your AI Chat Bot.
    
2.  There will be two Options , either Upload or Add Faqs.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#a.-uploading-faqs)

a. **Uploading FAQs:**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FC3LSXP2rddogVQqxEqyk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82b9a652-42c1-43bf-a473-27925cb91929&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15d54ec0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#what-this-feature-does)

What This Feature Does

*   Bulk upload FAQs using a CSV file
    
*   Automatically trains the AI chatbot on uploaded questions and answers
    
*   Saves time compared to adding FAQs one by one
    

Each row in the CSV represents **one FAQ (Question + Answer)**.

**Before You Upload (Important Guidelines)**

Please ensure the following before uploading your file:

1.  **Download the Sample CSV File** Use the provided sample file to understand the correct format.
    
2.  **Start Entering Data From the 2nd Row**
    
    *   The first row contains column headers
        
    *   All FAQ data must start from row 2 onwards
        
    
3.  **One FAQ Per Row**
    
    *   Each row should contain exactly one question and its answer
        
    
4.  **Ensure All FAQs Are Unique**
    
    *   Duplicate questions may lead to incorrect training or rejection
        
    
5.  **Maximum File Size: 20 MB**
    
    *   Files larger than 20 MB will not be uploaded
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFHHsRfMWPNOot1bm9jPp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc703a36f-8e09-47bf-8498-213a4351e05b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa242ad3&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#b.-add-faqs)

b. **Add FAQs:**

*   Click on Add FAQs button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnU0yyQDqKHYzdHSabYlG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3512c88a-7a11-46d4-9260-c9eb13b576df&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2af0d266&sv=2)

*   Add the Question and Answer
    
*   Then Click on save button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FlxmhBAFxMSd5TdgT4Mgb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98f148c4-5685-4d1d-a2b1-e096dd2cc2f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=871e5345&sv=2)

Congratulations! You have successfully created your first FAQ. continue to add more to make your bot smarter.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#faqs)

FAQ's

Here are some common questions asked regarding training with FAQ's:

chevron-rightWhere should I upload simple Q&A pairs?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#where-should-i-upload-simple-q-and-a-pairs)

Uploading simple Q/A pairs is best for the FAQ section. Just enter them in the category of your choice and they work!

chevron-rightCan I duplicate the FAQ categories across different bots, or do I need to recreate them manually?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#can-i-duplicate-the-faq-categories-across-different-bots-or-do-i-need-to-recreate-them-manually)

You will have to manually copy the categories across many bots.

chevron-rightIs there a character limit on the FAQ's?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#is-there-a-character-limit-on-the-faqs)

The question has a character limit of about 200 characters, while the answer can be effectively as long as you want.

chevron-rightAre there other ways to upload FAQ's?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#are-there-other-ways-to-upload-faqs)

Yes! You can upload a CSV file for the the questions. Follow the directions in any category by clicking on the "Upload FAQ's" button.

chevron-rightCan I upload duplicate FAQ's in multiple categories?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#can-i-upload-duplicate-faqs-in-multiple-categories)

No, the same FAQ in different categories us not possible, as BotPenguin will give an error when you try to do this.

chevron-rightWhy is the bot saying contradictory information?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#why-is-the-bot-saying-contradictory-information)

This is because the bot has been trained on sources that give the bot contradictory information regarding the same piece of data. Clear this contradiction to let the bot answer clearly.

chevron-rightHow long does it take for the bot to train on the FAQ's?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#how-long-does-it-take-for-the-bot-to-train-on-the-faqs)

The bot should train on the FAQ's almost instantly. Still, we recommend giving the bot 2 mins to finish training on the same.

chevron-rightDoes the bot learn from actual conversations in addition to FAQs?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs#does-the-bot-learn-from-actual-conversations-in-addition-to-faqs)

The bot can learn from the additional questions that are in the unanswered questions, and can be trained for the by answering them in the FAQ's.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a2d1d7d2d2cdd0d6e2c0cdd6d2c7ccc5d7cbcc8cc1cdcf)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousGoogle Sheetschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets)
[NextConversation Historychevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history)

Last updated 17 days ago

# Conversation History | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#interactive-guide)

**Interactive Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#what-is-the-unanswered-questions-feature)

What is the Unanswered Questions Feature?

The **Unanswered Questions** feature allows you to:

*   Identify queries that your AI chatbot was unable to answer.
    
*   Review and analyze questions over specific date ranges.
    
*   Train the chatbot on these questions by adding answers directly, enhancing its knowledge base.
    

This ensures that your chatbot becomes progressively smarter and more reliable over time.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#benefits-of-unanswered-questions)

Benefits of Unanswered Questions

*   🎯 **Identify Knowledge Gaps:** Quickly see where your chatbot needs improvement.
    
*   🟢 **Continuous Learning:** Add answers to unanswered questions to improve future responses.
    
*   ⚡ **Data-Driven Insights:** Analyze trends in questions your users ask.
    
*   🔧 **Easy Training:** Directly convert unanswered questions into FAQs.
    
*   📈 **Enhanced User Satisfaction:** Reduces repetitive unanswered queries and improves response accuracy.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#how-to-see-unanswered-questions-of-your-ai-chatbot)

**How to see unanswered questions of your AI Chatbot?**

1.  Log into your BotPenguin, and choose the bot you wish to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "Conversation History" option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnTrGIvIjSctchLvnZrJ7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D586a1a41-6506-4dc6-bab7-cdc83f52d87b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a876cc53&sv=2)

1.  A list of all the unanswered questions will be visible on the screen. You can choose the date ranges for which the questions are to be shown, or download the same using the export button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FcyUdjRazWscptD4zjsbP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D596b87e5-72eb-4e6a-a0b4-b8907e6d5a63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95396696&sv=2)

1.  Click on the icon on the right of the question to train the bot on it, directly from Unanswered Questions. Add the answer to the question, and then click on "Add FAQ" to add the FAQ
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fkuz3oDWYVsUSwvLt6kxk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d3b43e4-23e5-4ba6-9df9-945a92bf380c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4135814&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some FAQ's asked regarding Conversation history.

chevron-rightWhy are unanswered questions important for training?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#why-are-unanswered-questions-important-for-training)

They show what real users are asking but not getting answers to. Training on these helps your bot improve where it’s currently falling short.

chevron-rightWhat’s the best way to respond to these missed questions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#whats-the-best-way-to-respond-to-these-missed-questions)

Add clear answers to your FAQ section or directly into your training data. You can also create a new category for repeated missed topics.

chevron-rightHow often should I check for unanswered questions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#how-often-should-i-check-for-unanswered-questions)

Weekly reviews are ideal—this keeps your bot updated with user needs and ensures continued accuracy.

chevron-rightWhat if the unanswered question is too broad or vague?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#what-if-the-unanswered-question-is-too-broad-or-vague)

You can rephrase it into a more specific, helpful FAQ and train the bot accordingly. Or add follow-up prompts to guide users better.

chevron-rightCan I train the unanswered questions from the same tab?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history#can-i-train-the-unanswered-questions-from-the-same-tab)

Yes, unanswered questions can be trained from the same tab.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f1828481819e8385b1939e8581949f9684989fdf929e9c)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# Website | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#interactive-guide)

**Interactive Guide**

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#why-train-on-websites)

**Why train on Websites?**

Training bots on websites helps them understand your content better so they can answer user questions more accurately. It saves time by using your existing website data and ensures your chatbot gives responses that match your brand and information. This makes support faster, smarter, and more helpful for visitors.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot-on-website)

**How to train your AI Chatbot on Website?**

1.  Log into your BotPenguin, and choose the bot you wish to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "**Website**' tab to add the website.
    
2.  Click on Add your Website URL.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FxPDRSKGlEYD4Js9WlD70%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88c59855-e43f-449a-a4be-e2ee2a631cab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc6948c8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#training-options-available)

Training Options Available

You will see three training options:

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#a.-full-website-training-recommended)

a. Full Website Training (Recommended)

Train the bot using your entire website domain.

**Steps:**

1.  Select Full Website Training.
    
2.  Enter your Base Domain or Website URL (e.g., `https://yourwebsite.com`).
    
3.  (Optional) Add URLs or routes in Exclude URLs or Route if there are pages you don’t want the bot to learn from.
    
4.  Click Train.
    
5.  Expand the advance option to enable the toggle for training on images as well.
    

The system will crawl your website and import available content to train the AI model.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FfgNsZeq97tRHyXfVooL3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda050d87-ae9d-4f87-87bc-4ecc53bb551c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a461bbcc&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#id-2.-specific-urls)

2\. Specific URLs

Train the bot using selected pages instead of the full domain.

**Steps:**

1.  Select Specific URLs.
    
2.  Add or import the exact URLs you want to train the bot on.
    
3.  Click on add icon then the specific URL will be added.
    
4.  Click Train.
    
5.  Click on Upload file component to upload the files.
    
6.  Expand the advance option to enable the toggle for training on images as well.
    

Use this option when you only want the bot to learn from specific landing pages, help docs, or product pages.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrztbsvDlWUY43wnH5dTV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42c07f6e-f2d9-45a1-940c-74ef8b5e7d18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c36206a&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#id-3-json-feed)

3️⃣ JSON Feed

Train the bot using a structured JSON data feed.

**Steps:**

1.  Select **JSON Feed**.
    
2.  Add your structured feed URL.
    
3.  Click **Train**.
    

This option is best for structured content sources or dynamic databases.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#advanced-options)

⚙️ Advanced Options

Click on **Advance Options** to configure additional training settings (if required).

circle-info

You can also click on the "Advance option" to train the bot on images as well. Not that training on images takes significantly more time and cost than normal training.

Once done, click on the **"Train"** button. The website will start training.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F6ZA8ZtYbyf5uYIAy3le9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fdced8d-483f-4513-83f0-039be5ff7b54&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfda83f7&sv=2)

Congratulations! You have trained your bot on a website!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some common FAQ's regarding website training:

chevron-rightWhy is my bot not training from selected web pages?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#why-is-my-bot-not-training-from-selected-web-pages)

Make sure you have a valid URL, and give time for the website to train on.

chevron-rightHow to retrain your bot on a site?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#how-to-retrain-your-bot-on-a-site)

Click on the circular arrows to retrain or "Sync" your website.

chevron-rightWhy is the bot not answering information that is present on my site[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#why-is-the-bot-not-answering-information-that-is-present-on-my-site)

make sure the information is present in a clear format. Information that is in unique fonts may have trouble being trained on. Additionally, if information was in photos or images, then make sure to train the website on images as well, under the "Advance option".

chevron-rightMy site is freezing when I enter a URL[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#my-site-is-freezing-when-i-enter-a-url)

This is happening because the URL being entered is invalid. Kindly enter a valid URL. We are also working on this issue.

chevron-rightWhat is the proper method of training your on questions that are not being answered?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#what-is-the-proper-method-of-training-your-on-questions-that-are-not-being-answered)

Train these questions on the unanswered qusetions tab.

chevron-rightHow long does it take for the chatbot to crawl your website?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/website#how-long-does-it-take-for-the-chatbot-to-crawl-your-website)

Training time depends on your website, the number of pages trained, and the model that is being used. Use the latest GPT models, most websites can be trained within 2-3 mins, with larger websites and multiple pages training in bulk, allowing for quick training for multiple words simultaneously

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#d2a1a7a2a2bda0a692b0bda6a2b7bcb5a7bbbcfcb1bdbf)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousBest Practices for Training Your AIchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/best-practices-for-training-your-ai)
[NextFile Uploadchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload)

# Chatbot Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#interactive-guide-1)

Interactive Guide


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#what-are-website-chatbot-settings)

What are Website Chatbot Settings

Website Chatbot Settings on BotPenguin allow businesses to configure, customize, and manage all aspects of their chatbot on a website. From design and AI behavior to triggers, alerts, and user access, these settings ensure your chatbot operates efficiently, provides a consistent experience, and meets business goals.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#website-chatbot-settings-breakdown)

Website Chatbot Settings Breakdown

*   **Design:** Customize the look and feel of your chatbot to match your brand.
    
*   **General:** Configure basic chatbot behavior such as greetings, language, and fallback messages.
    
*   **Alerts:** Manage notifications for missed chats or other important events.
    
*   **Triggers:** Set rules to automatically initiate conversations or responses.
    
*   **User Access:** Control who can manage or interact with the chatbot backend.
    
*   **Chat Windows:** Customize the behavior and appearance of chat widgets on the website.
    
*   **AI Settings:** Manage AI responses, fallback handling, and knowledge base integration.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightCan I customize the chatbot design without coding?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#can-i-customize-the-chatbot-design-without-coding)

Yes, the Design section provides a visual editor to adjust colors, fonts, avatars, and widget positions without writing any code.

chevron-rightHow do I change the chatbot greeting or language?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#how-do-i-change-the-chatbot-greeting-or-language)

You can update the bot name, greeting message, and language in the General section of the settings.

chevron-rightHow do I get notifications for missed chats?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#how-do-i-get-notifications-for-missed-chats)

Alerts can be configured to send email or dashboard notifications whenever a chat is missed or unattended.

chevron-rightCan I set triggers for specific pages or user actions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#can-i-set-triggers-for-specific-pages-or-user-actions)

Yes, Triggers can be configured based on page visits, scroll depth, clicks, or exit intent to engage users automatically.

chevron-rightWho can manage the chatbot settings?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#who-can-manage-the-chatbot-settings)

User Access allows you to invite team members and assign roles with different permissions, ensuring secure and controlled management.

chevron-rightCan I preview chat window changes before publishing?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#can-i-preview-chat-window-changes-before-publishing)

Yes, the Chat Windows section provides a live preview so you can test the look and behavior before applying changes to your website.

chevron-rightWhat happens if the AI is unable to answer a question?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#what-happens-if-the-ai-is-unable-to-answer-a-question)

You can define fallback responses in AI Settings, which can either show a default message or escalate the conversation to a human agent.

chevron-rightWhat if I have set up everything correctly but still cannot move forward?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#what-if-i-have-set-up-everything-correctly-but-still-cannot-move-forward)

Please write to us at **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
**. Our team will respond within 48 business hours.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings#need-assistance)

Need Assistance?

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#dba8aeababb4a9af9bb9b4afabbeb5bcaeb2b5f5b8b4b6)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# Customize Website Chatbot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Website Chatbot Customization** feature allows you to design, style, and configure your chatbot to match your brand and website aesthetics. You can control how it appears, behaves, and interacts with your visitors, ensuring a consistent and engaging user experience.

**How to Redirect to the screen:**

1.  Click on Bots from left menu
    
2.  Select any website bot.
    
3.  Click on "Chatbot Design" option from the expanded side panel.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR7o5RAl0plOxPpUuS2DH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b52af5-95cb-4e86-a4b3-53b10ac8a885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73925c5e&sv=2)

1.  User will be redirected to website chatbot screen by default.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtnSLgwvk45gn5MkWMP1y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19a78e8a-6196-4261-b1af-29fa4d7ff92d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12748702&sv=2)

1.  Automatically user will be on the Content tab.
    
2.  To change the Theme and layout , user will need to switch the tabs.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot#theme)

Content

1.  Select the Content tab.
    
2.  Enter your bot's name in "Bot Name" box.
    
3.  Enter an inviting catch phrase that will make the user talk to bot in "Call to Action" box.
    
4.  Toggle ON/OFF auto hide call to action. If ON select time in seconds after which it will hide.
    
5.  Expand the more section.
    
6.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide CTA Chat Bubble.
    
7.  Select chat bubble background colour from the options.
    
8.  Select chat bubble text colour from the given options.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FoqWZFcn6UBgcC2B2eOna%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcca47966-dcaa-4ad4-827b-0e4a27ff3cfa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b67e389&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot#layout)

Theme

1.  Select your chat window style from the given two options.
    
2.  Select a bot icon from the options or upload from your device.
    
3.  Select a chatbot window theme colour.
    
4.  Select a chat background colour.
    
5.  Select a font style for your chatbot.
    
6.  Select Bot icon position.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FxMCDRymtUpGmqidJtpX2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9684117-c6bb-4ceb-8303-6efdeed9eca7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b92d778&sv=2)

1.  Add the Custom CSS for Advance Designs and add the custom CSS for launcher icon.
    

[pen-paintbrushAdding Custom CSS to Chat Windowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/adding-custom-css-to-chat-window)
[swatchbookCustomizing the Launcher Iconchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/customizing-the-launcher-icon)

1.  Click on save changes to upload the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwlvmwV7jlotBIP2p1QVi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9be243c6-d20d-48f4-9dec-2b11a8041a45&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4c6ab44&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot#layout-1)

Layout

1.  You can select chat window positioning on web.
    
2.  You can select chat window positioning on mobile.
    
3.  You can select chat window size.
    
4.  Click on "Save Changes" to save your customizations.
    

Here you can select the layout and positioning for your landing page

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fw9arDNOoo137w9Pcy66B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7d911c9-7cd1-4deb-a93b-33d6ee6207a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbcbb075&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget/customize-website-chatbot#need-assistance)

Need Assistance?

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5c2f292c2c332e281c3e33282c39323b293532723f3331)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# Alerts | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/alerts#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/alerts#alerts-settings)

Alerts Settings:

*   Go to the “Bots” section from the left sidebar.
    
*   Select any website bot
    
*   Select your bot and click on “Settings”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3B5ReW0tKSXREqjUWUjk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D535d89e6-c4b0-434e-94a1-0cde3bf0e17c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7059e934&sv=2)

*   Go to Alerts tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtKJxN4tq8DY15RCTlSCD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc34367f3-3b69-49e6-8e93-b5044e076b29&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=499fffd8&sv=2)

1.  **Email Subject Field**:
    
    *   Enter the subject line for the email notifications. This will be the title of the email you receive when a new lead interacts with the bot.
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FO66Zqdh53yLe61vnwFtE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e8925fa-5fb7-4da8-8c50-e091b332257e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0cfbdca&sv=2)
    
2.  **Email Notifications Toggle**:
    
    *   Use this toggle to enable or disable email notifications. When enabled, you will receive an email whenever a new lead interacts with the bot.
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FHL9wVDay3iNMWj394wWA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148d23eb-b2fc-4c68-986c-1f87f60a4c17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d092e5ec&sv=2)
    
3.  **Email Address Field**:
    
    *   Add the email addresses where you want to receive notifications.
        
    *   You can add multiple email addresses by typing each one and pressing **Enter**.
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fp1Y8e7J6jhX3if22lKxi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7655ec15-b2a5-440a-9759-8429412a90f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=337941ef&sv=2)
    
4.  **Lead Revisit Notifications Toggle**:
    
    *   Enable this toggle to receive notifications when a lead revisits and interacts with the bot.
        
    *   For example, if a lead interacts with the bot, leaves, and then returns later, you will receive a notification about their revisit.
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPdorikdlVTu5EyZpNuvT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc96f32e-859d-4fd4-8f81-ad0b3e8e8672&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e61d43e&sv=2)
    
5.  **Save Changes**:
    
    *   Click the **Save Changes** button to apply your settings. Your email notifications will now be active as per your configuration.
        
    
    ![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FgghNQqDvAZWMJVRcwuRw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D684af0de-c7c6-412f-87f3-96a5b52d34bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e687602&sv=2)
    

* * *

If you still have questions for our team, write to us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#4b383e3b3b24393f0b29243f3b2e252c3e222565282426)
. We’ll get back to you within 48 hours.

[PreviousGeneralchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general)
[NextTriggerschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/triggers)

Last updated 17 days ago

# 3rd party Integrations | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#streamline-your-workflow)

Streamline your workflow


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BotPenguin has 55+ Integration to automate your workflow for you. BotPenguin integration capabilities allow you to seamlessly transfer your lead, appointments, ticket, and task data to the 3rd party apps. You can integrate 3rd party apps with BotPenguin in two ways.

1.  Use available Native integrations
    
2.  Have the APIs ready! Create your custom integration with BotPenguin `My Integration` capabilities.
    

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#why-botpenguin-integrations)

Why BotPenguin Integrations?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BotPenguin bots work as a front-end app for your end customers, and it collects data in the form of the customer chat and other necessary data such as on which page they were, their indicative location (fetched from IP address), device, browser, etc. All this data is available on the BotPenguin dashboard. However, You may need the same data in any of the other apps that you might be using, such as

1.  CRMs
    
2.  Scheduling software
    
3.  Task/ticket management tools etc
    

**BotPenguin integrations enable you to use these integrations to send the metadata to your apps.**

![Drawing](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtvQJkK3KWtmcYOQuT8Ik%252Ffile.drawing.svg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D495b6b9e-5445-4bdd-b14c-4355239ce6cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=abdd9286&sv=2)

How BotPenguin works with 3rd party applications

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#how-to-integrate-3rd-party-apps-with-botpenguin)

How to integrate 3rd party apps with BotPenguin?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you have decided which app you want to send your data to, Here is how you can integrate it.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#botpenguin-integration-with-available-apps)

BotPenguin Integration with Available Apps

1.  Log in to the BotPenguin dashboard using the link [https://app.botpenguin.com/arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
    .
    
2.  Navigate your bot and find the `3rd Party Apps Integrations` option on the dashboard.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FER8JCHscqilMt7toNgMu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b459588-b1e1-4831-959d-a8a533cd8b50&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81399abd&sv=2)

1.  Once you find the list of all integrations available, search for the desired integrations.
    
2.  Once you find your integrations in the list, click on the connect button and follow the on-screen steps.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#couldnt-find-the-desired-app-build-your-custom-integration)

Couldn't find the desired App? Build your custom Integration!

If the app you are looking for is unavailable on the app list, You can build your integration. It is no code and is very simple to build. Below is the link to how

[Create your custom integration or My Integrationschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/create-your-custom-integration-or-my-integrations)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations#having-questions)

Having Questions?

If you have any questions, you can refer to the below link or contact us at [\[email protected\].envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b0c3c5c0c0dfc2c4f0d2dfc4c0d5ded7c5d9de9ed3dfdd)

[PreviousChatbot Templateschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates)
[NextChatGPTchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt)

# Other Sources | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#interactive-guide)

**Interactive Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#what-is-training-via-other-sources)

What is Training via Other Sources?

**Training your AI chatbot via external sources** allows you to provide additional knowledge beyond uploaded files or FAQs.

*   **Notion:** Connect your Notion workspace to enable the chatbot to retrieve content from pages, databases, or documentation.
    
*   **Dropbox:** Connect your Dropbox account to provide your bot access to stored files like PDFs, documents, and spreadsheets.
    

This integration ensures that your chatbot can reference multiple content repositories for accurate, context-aware answers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#benefits-of-using-other-sources)

Benefits of Using Other Sources

*   🎯 **Expanded Knowledge Base:** Utilize content from Notion and Dropbox for richer chatbot responses.
    
*   🟢 **Centralized Content Management:** Keep your information in familiar platforms while enabling the chatbot to access it.
    
*   ⚡ **Dynamic Updates:** Any changes in connected Notion pages or Dropbox files can automatically update your bot’s knowledge.
    
*   🔧 **Seamless Integration:** No coding required—simply connect accounts and start training.
    
*   📈 **Enhanced User Engagement:** Provides precise answers and reduces unanswered queries.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot)

**How to train your AI Chatbot?**

1.  To manage all your chatbots, you first need to visit the BotPenguin Dashboard: [https://app.botpenguin.com/homearrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)
    
2.  To manage your bot, select it from the left sidebar.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on **"Other sources"** tab.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#other-sources)

Other Sources

1.  You can connect your Notion Page and your chatbot will retrieve information from it.
    
2.  Similarly you can connect your Google Drive and your chatbot will retrieve information from it.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F5ifsYkV0FVeVdxD5iTex%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55b81d46-e2b9-454f-a424-765d5d380ad1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c6dfda0&sv=2)

Your AI-powered chatbot is now fully equipped to handle and answer all user queries seamlessly!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#id-5.-faqs)

5\. FAQs

chevron-rightCan I connect both Notion and Dropbox at the same time?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#can-i-connect-both-notion-and-dropbox-at-the-same-time)

Yes, you can connect multiple sources, and the chatbot will reference content from all connected platforms.

chevron-rightDo changes in Notion or Dropbox update the chatbot automatically?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#do-changes-in-notion-or-dropbox-update-the-chatbot-automatically)

Yes, once synced, updates in connected pages or files will reflect in the chatbot after the next sync.

chevron-rightIs authorization required for both platforms?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#is-authorization-required-for-both-platforms)

Yes, you need to authorize BotPenguin to access your Notion and Dropbox accounts.

chevron-rightCan I select specific pages or files to train the chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#can-i-select-specific-pages-or-files-to-train-the-chatbot)

Yes, you can choose which Notion pages, databases, or Dropbox folders/files should be used for training.

chevron-rightDoes this integration require coding knowledge?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#does-this-integration-require-coding-knowledge)

No, connecting and syncing content is completely code-free.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#d3a0a6a3a3bca1a793b1bca7a3b6bdb4a6babdfdb0bcbe)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousConversation Historychevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/conversation-history)
[NextCustomize your Bot widgetchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/customize-your-bot-widget)

Last updated 17 days ago

# Google Sheets | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#interactive-guide)

**Interactive Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#what-is-training-via-google-sheets)

What is Training via Google Sheets?

Training your AI chatbot via **Google Sheets** allows you to provide structured data stored in spreadsheets for accurate and dynamic responses.

By connecting Google Sheets:

*   Your chatbot can access live data from the spreadsheet.
    
*   Responses can be updated automatically as the spreadsheet changes.
    
*   Enables dynamic and personalized user interactions based on real-time data.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#benefits-of-google-sheets-training)

Benefits of Google Sheets Training

*   🎯 **Real-Time Data Sync:** Chatbot can fetch and respond using live spreadsheet data.
    
*   🟢 **Automated Knowledge Updates:** Changes in the sheet automatically reflect in chatbot responses.
    
*   ⚡ **Flexible Data Management:** Use Google Sheets as a backend for FAQs, orders, appointments, and more.
    
*   🔧 **Multi-Sheet Support:** Add multiple sheets to train the chatbot comprehensively.
    
*   📈 **Enhanced User Experience:** Provides accurate, context-aware, and timely responses.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#guidance-video)

**Guidance Video**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot-on-google-sheet)

**How to train your AI Chatbot on Google Sheet?**

1.  Log into your BotPenguin, and choose the bot you wish to train.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "**Google Sheet**' tab to train on sheets.
    
2.  Click on **“Connect your Google Sheet”** to add the sheet according to which you want to train your AI Chat Bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FsJuUYJATuCHwGRurulln%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9fec5b0-5bfb-4046-9b72-af520757ef77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f5089b3&sv=2)

circle-info

You may be redirected to the third party integrations page. Sign into your google account and then go back to the "Google Sheets" tab. Click on the "Connect your Google Sheet" again.

1.  Connect your google account and allow the permissions
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F4cnoSfP86kwnl23EdY95%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e9a2d89-3555-4c12-be2f-8b00e83977c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f1b99e1&sv=2)

1.  Botpenguin will ask you to allow some permissions in order to access the Google Sheets
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWT3HbP5fVFHgns6VjtQH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a026e0f-62bf-4d66-ae31-18ddcd2235ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4822d80&sv=2)

1.  Click on Allow button.
    
2.  Then your account will be connected .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCwl7bgco7eCipF6fIMKn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d714016-bf3c-47c5-b6c4-2adbf10d60f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30f07a4d&sv=2)

1.  Click on Add Google Sheet Button
    
2.  Add your Google Sheet URL and describe the content or purpose of this Google sheet.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWu4CTCPiMXRqIxcvYYeT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc09dd181-f376-4341-899c-664a2c75ae9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e795f7d0&sv=2)

1.  Click on **“Add Google Sheets”.**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdEXROLMTpRhI6PrV8vcx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D538488f4-a9d3-43b9-8305-734b4811b6b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19c8ab4e&sv=2)

Congratulations! You have just added a google sheet! The training for the current sheet should have started, and you can add more sheets using the "Sync Google Sheet" button on the top left corner.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some common FAQ's regarding Google Sheets:

chevron-rightWhat kind of Google Sheets are supported for training?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#what-kind-of-google-sheets-are-supported-for-training)

Only public or shared sheets with proper access permissions (viewer or editor) can be synced. Ensure your sheet isn't restricted or private.

chevron-rightMy Google Sheet has multiple tabs. Will the bot train on all of them?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#my-google-sheet-has-multiple-tabs.-will-the-bot-train-on-all-of-them)

Currently, the system typically trains on the **first tab** of the sheet. For multi-tab training, ensure relevant data is consolidated in a single tab.

chevron-rightWhat format should the sheet follow for best results?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#what-format-should-the-sheet-follow-for-best-results)

Use a two-column format: one for **Questions** and one for **Answers**. Avoid using formulas, merged cells, or complex formatting.

chevron-rightWhy was I redirected to another page while connecting Google Sheets?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#why-was-i-redirected-to-another-page-while-connecting-google-sheets)

That’s a normal part of the **OAuth authentication process** for Google account access. After signing in, return to the "Google Sheets" tab to complete the sync.

chevron-rightI clicked “Sync Google Sheet,” but nothing seems to happen. What should I do?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#i-clicked-sync-google-sheet-but-nothing-seems-to-happen.-what-should-i-do)

Refresh the page, ensure the sheet URL is correct and publicly accessible, and confirm you are logged into the correct Google account.

chevron-rightHow can I add more than one Google Sheet?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#how-can-i-add-more-than-one-google-sheet)

After syncing the first sheet, simply click the **"Sync Google Sheet"** button again (top-left corner) to repeat the process for additional sheets.

chevron-rightWill the bot automatically update if I make changes to the sheet later?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#will-the-bot-automatically-update-if-i-make-changes-to-the-sheet-later)

No, you need to **manually resync** the sheet after any edits to reflect the updates in your chatbot training.

chevron-rightCan I delete or disconnect a synced sheet later?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#can-i-delete-or-disconnect-a-synced-sheet-later)

Yes. Visit the connected sheets section and select the one you wish to remove or update. The training data will adjust accordingly.

chevron-rightI entered the correct sheet URL, but it's not syncing. What could be wrong?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#i-entered-the-correct-sheet-url-but-its-not-syncing.-what-could-be-wrong)

Double-check the sheet’s **sharing settings** and make sure it's not restricted. Also, confirm that you've completed the Google sign-in process correctly.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9deee8ededf2efe9ddfff2e9edf8f3fae8f4f3b3fef2f0)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousFile Uploadchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/file-upload)
[NextFAQschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/faqs)

Last updated 15 days ago

*   [Benefits of Google Sheets Training](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/google-sheets#benefits-of-google-sheets-training)

# Customize Landing Page Bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#what-is-the-landing-page-design-section)

What is the Landing Page Design Section

The **Landing Page Design section** in Website Chatbot Settings allows you to fully customize the visual appearance and content of your chatbot’s landing page. You can edit text, headings, descriptions, logos, social media links, layout, chat window style, theme colors, fonts, and background colors to ensure your chatbot’s landing page is visually appealing and aligned with your brand.

Whether it’s updating the landing page header, changing the chatbot icon, or selecting a layout, this section ensures your landing page creates a professional and engaging experience for website visitors.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#benefits-of-the-landing-page-design-section)

Benefits of the Landing Page Design Section

*   **Brand Consistency:** Align the landing page with your brand colors, fonts, and logos.
    
*   **Enhanced User Experience:** A well-designed landing page encourages visitors to interact with your chatbot.
    
*   **Full Customization:** Easily update content, social links, layout, themes, and chat window styles without coding.
    
*   **Improved Engagement:** Custom headings, descriptions, and call-to-action placement help drive more interactions.
    
*   **Quick Updates:** Save and apply changes instantly, ensuring the landing page is always up to date.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

**How to Redirect to the screen:**

1.  Click on Bots from left menu
    
2.  Select any website bot.
    
3.  Click on "Chatbot Design" option from the expanded side panel.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR7o5RAl0plOxPpUuS2DH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b52af5-95cb-4e86-a4b3-53b10ac8a885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73925c5e&sv=2)

1.  User will be redirected to website chatbot screen by default.
    
2.  Select the Landing page Bot Tab.
    
3.  And by default user will be on the Content Tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fch7K9czk8gYbTUZMtjTv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59dc3563-9eac-439f-a4e5-7fd1d376a7aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c65c057&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#content-section)

Content Section


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enter your bot's landing page name in "Landing Page Name" box.
    
2.  Enter the heading text you want to display in "Landing Page Header" box.
    
3.  Enter the description text you want to display in "Landing Page Description" box.
    
4.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide logo and text.
    
5.  Toggle ON/OFF to hide chatbot's header.
    
6.  Upload profile logo for your chatbot page.
    
7.  Add any social media links and icons.
    
8.  And click on "Save Changes" to update all the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FiWM5keI3KePW5AN1AZbA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4e3c802-37bb-4f0d-a42f-bd64fc0699f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7775734a&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#theme)

Theme


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Switch the tab to Theme to change the theme .

1.  Select your chat window style from the given two options.
    
2.  Select a bot icon from the options or upload from your device.
    
3.  Select a landing page theme colour.
    
4.  Select a chat background colour.
    
5.  Select landing page background colour.
    
6.  Select a font style for your chatbot.
    
7.  Click on save changes to upload the changes done.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FACCNRPjgDSsFPYgpXqTE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db14b1193-d4f2-4578-8b58-4e7a05775a15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32ff300&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#layout)

Layout


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Here you can select the layout and positioning for your landing page
    
2.  Click on "Save Changes" to save your customizations.
    
3.  These are all the settings you can do to customize your website chatbot if still have queries you can contact us anytime.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fp2lmxwrp6buhq5pyVZZe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D875d2ce9-8b0c-46cb-ae4a-f5d6648979a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3180ab0&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot#need-assistance)

Need Assistance?

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#30434540405f424470525f4440555e5745595e1e535f5d)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# General | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#configure-general-settings)

Configure General Settings

1.  Go to the “Bots” section from the left sidebar.
    
2.  Select any website bot
    
3.  Select your bot and click on “Settings”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3B5ReW0tKSXREqjUWUjk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D535d89e6-c4b0-434e-94a1-0cde3bf0e17c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7059e934&sv=2)

1.  Under the “General” tab, configure the following:
    

*   **Waiting Message** (e.g., Usual reply time: 2 to 3 Minutes).
    

This text will be displayed on the bot to inform the users regarding the waiting time.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMSiYGOXF7Q4m7dHMIzTQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05f72ba6-1618-4cb1-9cfe-4263d1abc444&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c79ce937&sv=2)

*   **Un-availability Message (if support bot is not available)**
    

This message is shown to users when the chatbot or live chat support is unavailable. It helps set clear expectations during offline hours.

*   **Waiting Message Title (for initiating live chat)**
    

This is the heading displayed above the waiting message while the system is connecting the user to an agent or processing the request.

*   **Un-availability Message Title (for initiating live chat)**
    

This is the title shown when the chatbot or support team is offline. It appears above the un-availability message for better visibility.

*   **Choose the “Language”.**
    

This setting defines the primary language in which the chatbot interface and default responses will operate.

*   **Time Zone**
    

This determines the time reference used for chatbot availability, working hours, and time-based automations.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#manage-chatbot-status-and-behavior)

Manage Chatbot Status & Behavior

*   Toggle “Chatbot Status” ON to make your bot active on the website.
    
*   **Send Incomplete Responses**
    

When enabled, the chatbot may send partial responses if the full response generation is interrupted due to timeout or technical issues.

*   **Invalidate Cache**
    

This option refreshes the chatbot’s cached data. Use it when recent changes are not reflecting on the live website.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#configure-chat-history-and-sounds)

Configure Chat History & Sounds

*   Select your preferred “Chat Window Message History” (e.g., Session-based).
    

Customize sound settings:

*   “Bot Pop-up Sound”
    
*   “Message Sound (For Team User)”
    
*   “Message Sound (For End User)”
    
*   “Bot Appearance Sound”
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#enable-data-capture)

Enable Data Capture

1.  Toggle ON:
    

*   **Capture IP & Device Information:** When enabled, the system collects visitor IP address and device details for analytics and support tracking purposes.
    
*   **Capture URL Source:** When enabled, the chatbot captures the URL or source page from which the user initiated the chat. This helps in tracking campaign performance and understanding visitor intent.
    
*   Enable Bot Whitelabel toggle to hide the Chat by BotPenguin tagline from the chatbot
    

This helps track visitor details for better analytics and follow-ups.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/general#save-changes)

Save Changes

1.  Scroll and click the “Save” button (if applicable) to apply your updates.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FP6vKcsqal0WBn5r0EQet%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd231cda-4287-4501-b651-ab5ee3c88ce0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5eef264&sv=2)

If you still have questions for our team, write to us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#57242227273825231735382327323930223e397934383a)
. We’ll get back to you within 48 hours.

[PreviousCustomize Landing Page Botchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/design/customize-landing-page-bot)
[NextAlertschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/alerts)

Last updated 17 days ago

# Chatbot Templates | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#what-are-pre-built-chatbot-templates)

What are Pre-Built Chatbot Templates?

**Pre-Built Chatbot Templates** are ready-to-use message structures designed to help you quickly create Chatbot.

These templates save time by providing predefined formats that can be customized with your content, media, and buttons. They can be used as-is or modified to match your business needs.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#benefits-of-pre-built-chatbot-templates)

Benefits of Pre-Built Chatbot Templates

*   🎯 **Quick Setup:** Launch campaigns faster by using pre-configured templates.
    
*   🟢 **Consistent Messaging:** Ensure uniform tone and formatting across all communications.
    
*   ⚡ **Flexible Customization:** Edit text, media, footers, and buttons to suit your audience.
    
*   🔧 **Draft & Edit:** Save templates as drafts to modify before submission.
    
*   📈 **Approval-Ready:** Pre-built templates are structured for WhatsApp compliance, reducing approval delays.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#how-to-use-pre-built-chatbot-templates)

How to Use Pre-Built Chatbot Templates

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#step-1-access-pre-built-templates)

Step 1: Access Pre-Built Templates

1.  Go to your bot dashboard.
    
2.  Click **Chatflow Templates**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2NIlZvOKo3LgYy2rCswC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d2e0d77-b496-4617-8f79-25e121deee92&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9396250c&sv=2)

1.  Browse the **template gallery** to choose a template closest to your campaign needs.
    
2.  Select the template to **customize** or create an entirely new template from scratch.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FgGbxrQYlWMqCdtWwEakf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cbbd014-1658-480b-a72a-ee6ef85027d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e79c157&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#step-2-preview-the-selected-template)

Step 2: Preview the Selected Template

1.  Hover on the template , then there will be eye icon.
    
2.  Click on eye icon to preview the Template.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Ftdrt56RZX9tCw7xpvKmp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73a0fe1e-0df3-4b8e-afc4-baf840f8d6b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4144e4c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-templates#step-3-using-the-selected-template)

Step 3: Using the Selected Template

1.  Hover on the Selected template.
    
2.  Click on Use Template Button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYa9zuWTXA311W155zbpn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df99ce845-90a0-4bd1-925b-d28a0b1bdb43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1cc41a3a&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOfSOkCBN66NY6auPAbP3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8cb372e-8e9e-4790-8b9a-8db936d6048d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc3b85e2&sv=2)

1.  Click on use now button to add the Template.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmXKZHT4BDMtjSxn6Tn2p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9ddfc8e-aff0-4c74-b5d8-9f52aa2e7062&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d19898ee&sv=2)

1.  Template added successfully and now you can edit the Template with the help of Components.
    

[comments-questionManage Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/manage-chatflow)

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3a494f4a4a55484e7a58554e4a5f545d4f535414595557)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.
