# Chatbot Persona | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#botpenguin-ai-persona)

BotPenguin AI Persona


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Persona refers to the personality of the Ai that is being used with the chatbot. Users have the option to configure the personality of the bot themselves, by following the instructions provided in the guidelines. By doing so, users can provide their customers with a more personalized, relatable and effective agent, allowing for better communication and experience.

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#setup-of-ai-agent)

Setup of AI Agent


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For usage of the AI Persona requires the integration of any AI platform into the Chatbot. Users have the option of ChatGPT, Claude, Gemini, and Deepseek, and the integration instructions for all are available in the "3rd Party Integrations Section".

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#reasons-to-setup-unique-personality)

Reasons to Setup Unique Personality:

*   **Boost customer engagement** by making interactions more natural, relatable, and human-like.
    
*   **Ensure brand consistency** by aligning the chatbot’s tone and style with your business identity.
    
*   **Increase conversation effectiveness** by guiding users seamlessly toward desired outcomes.
    
*   **Deliver personalized experiences at scale** by adapting responses based on user behavior and context.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#setup-of-ai-persona)

Setup of AI Persona

1.  Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    
2.  Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Configure AI Personality", and turn the toggle off.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FczQhxGz9QCyjymNrTEnE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D651ffa90-f6f8-40fc-900f-595e20b45c5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=141ebb20&sv=2)

Turn the "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed"

1.  To create a new persona, click on "Create Persona", or hover over the general persona and click con the settings icon that will show up.
    
2.  The user has the option to configure the AI's personality based on the following sections:
    
    1.  Persona Details
        
    2.  Communication Style
        
    3.  Chat Scenarios
        
    4.  Custom Instructions
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FDNqfUiwzpxViy5oQyMUD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45832362-d84b-4138-91bf-2b5438cc7d71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e231c1ea&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#settings-in-ai-persona)

Settings in AI Persona:

1.  Persona Details:
    
    1.  Persona Title: Title of the persona to be shown on the title card(similar to General)
        
    2.  Persona Description: Description of the Persona
        
    3.  Upload Photo: Photo shown on Persona card.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FX2P81Al5xdOTkN8xNBuT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd83a48e-ef91-4dcc-ab67-fae683faaf9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=816da3b3&sv=2)

1.  Communication Style:
    
    1.  Answer Length: Select the length of the answers that you want.
        
    2.  Answer Perspective (1st person, 3rd person, etc.)
        
    3.  Tone: Can be configured to formal, joyful, sincere, etc.
        
    4.  Language: Can detect the users language and answer that, or can be configured to a particular language.
        
    5.  Answer Formatting: Can be in paragraph, bullet points or numbered points.
        
    6.  Included Sources for Response: Toggle that allows us to include the source of the answer.
        
    7.  Personalize Replies with Chat History: Remembers the context of the conversation and answers in relation to that history.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F5MWdIGxq02HbL9wcPCRG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd4cd479-ca84-4af3-8517-b4184e69bfe7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afa667ee&sv=2)

1.  Chat Scenarios:
    
    1.  Allows users to configure particular scenarios, and the responses or flows to redirect for the same.
        
    2.  For more details, refer to the details below:
        
    

[Chatbot Personachevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fi7NCLZ39NznMLrW8pWNO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56840516-449a-4b3f-8993-a38eec9a1ab5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7eb64492&sv=2)

1.  Custom Instructions:
    
    1.  Allows users to give custom instructions to their chatbot, and it will follow the same.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FicXk9BiJFfDfUQaGflTf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83c9fa48-1c56-449c-934a-fa85d3a2b715&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=625824c&sv=2)

circle-info

Note : You can decide how many queries/answers to be handled via AI. After that you can continue your chat flow. Available in Customize Bot Message.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FhLBsZAr7x6iVPCuA6Giu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ff2ca63-1c5a-46a3-ad84-b5cfecbfb68e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6037d564&sv=2)

And you're done! Whenever the AI component is invoked, your custom-trained model will provide responses based on the settings and training you've configured, enhancing your chatbot's conversational abilities.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some common questions asked for setting the AI Personalities:

chevron-rightWhy is My AI component returning the exact same line as input?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#why-is-my-ai-component-returning-the-exact-same-line-as-input)

Successful integration of any AI Platform key is necessary for the component to work.

chevron-rightHow to make my files to be included in the response.[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#how-to-make-my-files-to-be-included-in-the-response)

Click on the "Include source files in answer" in the Communication Style section of the persona to configure the same.

chevron-rightAI is not answering in the language that is entered. What should I do?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#ai-is-not-answering-in-the-language-that-is-entered.-what-should-i-do)

Make sure that the language is set to "Detect Users' Language & Respond In The Same". If it is for a particular language, the bot might have difficulty answering in the users language.

chevron-rightHow to use Custom Instructions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/chatbot-persona#how-to-use-custom-instructions)

Enter the commands that you want to be noted all the time. These can be related to display, tone, answers, etc.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a4d7d1d4d4cbd6d0e4c6cbd0d4c1cac3d1cdca8ac7cbc9)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousConfiguring Chatbot Scenarioschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios)
[NextAI Chat Summarychevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary)

# AI settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings#botpenguin-ai)

BotPenguin AI

BotPenguin utilizes a combination of ChatGPT, proprietary technology, and specialized training to create custom AI models tailored to your business's unique knowledge and customer service needs.

You can feed data to your custom AI model through various sources, including website URLs, content files, and FAQs. This enables BotPenguin to develop AI solutions that deliver exceptional service and support to your customers by leveraging both publicly available information and your business-specific data.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings#setup-chatgpt-and-ai-settings)

Setup ChatGPT and AI Settings

To integrate ChatGPT into your BotPenguin chatbot and customize its behavior, follow these steps:

**Step 1: Create Your Bots**

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

**Step 2: Chatbot Settings**

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

**Step 3: Configure Bot's Personality**

*   Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up:
    
*   Go to Configure Bot's personality
    
*   Toggle off "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed option" to create your own AI persona
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYVlnuOGyL6qd6Y2532ue%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b7554be-3015-4843-92e5-478712e5bda4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78ea38e0&sv=2)

*   Click on settings icon to change the existing persona or click on **"use persona"** to use the existing one .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmmMqxalxGsYmDqyc88oU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D628b71d5-e5eb-4448-9eb2-72ccae878422&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32c3dc32&sv=2)

*   Click on Create persona button to create a new persona
    

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252F0B1YAMnq64N6qgvVff7z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea820ef-33bf-454d-8c3a-d98aa6d5a37c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da9b7828&sv=2)

*   In these settings, you can define the persona details to:
    
    *   **Configure Bot's Personality**
        
    *   **Answer Length**
        
    *   **Answer Perspective (1st person, 3rd person, etc.)**
        
    *   **Tone**
        
    *   **Language**
        
    *   **Answer Formatting**
        
    *   **Included Sources for Response**
        
    *   **Custom Prompt Instructions**
        
    *   **Manage Unusual Chat Scenarios**
        
    *   **Message for When Bot Can't Answer**
        
    *   **Message for Responding to Inappropriate Language Usage**
        
    

Persona Details

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FHgX8z0KhVWUM9IM9oZVg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4211c2cc-a205-4dd8-b22f-5a9d12c6583c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c510746&sv=2)

*   In Persona Details enter the persona title, persona description and upload a cover photo for your bot's persona.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOBUmVEwsm8SBzstZMept%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2d78f22-6bdb-41e4-a63d-3a8766772a2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4286c154&sv=2)

*   In Communication Style, enter answer length, answer as (1st person , 2nd person etc), tone of bot, language used and answer formating. You can also toggle ON/OFF sources and personalize replies with chat history.
    
*   If "include sources for response" is ON it will share the source name of the knowledge base.
    

**Chat Scenerios**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F64lR3IiXmfOGhLXaLUN2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d784a0-98bb-4092-8808-2ad6b1563adc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7246a797&sv=2)

*   You can add a chat scenerio by clicking on "Add Action".
    
*   In Chat Scenarios, select or add an action which gets triggered based on the user's response.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FgvPr2ccHHX2l3OgqMOqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c919357-761b-4d53-985a-cac945d717ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65dd37b8&sv=2)

*   Here you can add a keyword according to which LLM model will identify the chat intent and will give message or flow set by you.
    
*   You can add the chat Intent and message.
    

**Custom Instructions:**

*   In Custom Instructions, add a custom prompt which best defines your bot persona and based on that it will act. Example: "Act as a salesman and use formal tone and be polite and friendly"
    
*   And finally click on "Update" to save the changes.
    
*   You can click on "Use Persona" to use it in you chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdmhfrxKWLhxnOPj6Nlgq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aca1a95-3e0d-4323-8205-60d4b3cf71b9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb9f289e&sv=2)

**Persona in Use**

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FeFcSnMU78LLXa8mbU3Cs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5171d242-b623-44d0-b8cf-81e8bce2eb91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea672433&sv=2)

*   Finally the AI model in your chatflow will work based on the persona set by you.
    

Note : You can decide how many queries/answers to be handled via AI. After that you can continue your chat flow. Available in Customize Bot Message.

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FHToxSrHGwf1yRpb5H1Jx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94419ec1-a898-4ab2-9213-679020d0f0db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5e214a0&sv=2)

**Step 4: Configure ChatGPT Component**

*   Integrate ChatGPT model with your bot for better outputs.
    
*   You can invoke the ChatGPT component at multiple points in the chatflow as needed.
    
*   Select a GPT model you want to use after integrating with ChatGPT.
    

circle-info

Initially it will be set on GPT-3.5 Turbo

And you're done! Whenever the ChatGPT component is invoked, your custom-trained model will provide responses based on the settings and training you've configured, enhancing your chatbot's conversational abilities.

[PreviousTransfer Chat to WhatsApp Functionalitychevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/chat-window/transfer-chat-to-whatsapp-functionality)
[NextConfiguring Chatbot Scenarioschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios)

Last updated 17 days ago

# Configuring Chatbot Scenarios | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The inputs of users are varying, but certain inputs, such as those which the chatbot cannot provide an answer to, or those that may be offensive, can be configured to give a pre-defined response. This is done through the use of AI, which analyses the input to understand its intent, and responds back with the correct pre-defined response. Additionally, for better organization, you can have different flows. Utilizing the power of artificial intelligence, we can use flow redirection to analyze the users input, and then redirect them to the appropriate flow at any time.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios#steps-for-setup-of-dynamic-chatflow-configuration)

Steps for Setup of Dynamic Chatflow Configuration:

1.  **Create Your Bots**
    

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

1.  **Chatbot Settings**
    

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  **Configure Bot's Personality**
    

*   Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up:
    
*   Go to Configure Bot's personality
    
*   Toggle off "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed option" to create your own AI persona
    

1.  Click on the toggle to **disable** the “Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed”, as we need to customize the responses of our chatbot to certain intents. Then, go to “**Create Persona**”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FEnPBJhXpgL29GTpcuwp0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3a32ef7-1d27-4523-975a-dbcf2c04e613&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37774cda&sv=2)

1.  Upon reaching the main screen here, go to “**Chat Scenarios**”.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFi5GE6YY5cHLl9bDsIX7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fbe8e76-5e17-401c-8369-9a5058c55615&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba457cd0&sv=2)

circle-info

If you are configuring the bot for the first time, then the above fields (Persona Details, Communication Style) also need to be filled for the redirection to work.

1.  Click on the “**Add-Action button**” to proceed to the configuration of the chatbot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIBneq4NtNd4AiSWtbDW0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f428c55-33a4-4305-8ba2-12f597a5e846&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=61b004de&sv=2)

1.  Complete the form with the relevant details for the bot. The fields to fill are as follows:
    
    1.  **Name**: Specify the name of the chat. This name will be the primary description of the trigger. E.g.: “Flowers” for redirection to flowers chat
        
    2.  **Trigger**: Define the action to be executed when the specified condition is met. Options include triggering a specific message or an entire chat flow.
        
        1.  **Message**: Enter the message to be displayed in the chat.
            
        2.  **Flow**: Select the chat flow to be triggered.
            
        
    3.  Based on the previous Trigger input:
        
        1.  **Message**: Enter the message that is to be displayed when triggered. Eg. If the message is offensive, the response message can be "I am not quite used to this language".
            
        2.  **Flow**: Select the flow onto which the chat should be redirected to.
            
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrwixSwDzxZRv3ACnOhvU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0277fae4-cb39-4353-ad82-62b71d4bf519&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd92805&sv=2)

1.  Click on “**Add Intent**” to finish setup.
    

circle-info

Remember to toggle on the button to enable the message/flow redirection.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZMtBHUlZVH2FckJVGHnJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0cd1380-795d-4765-8aa2-04efffd676c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb504a11&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios#still-not-working-lets-troubleshoot)

Still Not Working? Let's Troubleshoot

If the chat is not responding as expected, consider the following troubleshooting steps:

1.  **Verify Triggers and Conditions**: Ensure that the trigger conditions are correctly set and aligned with the intended message types or user inputs.
    
2.  **Check Message and Flow Settings**: Confirm that the correct message or chat flow is selected and configured properly.
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#42313732322d303602202d3632272c25372b2c6c212d2f)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousAI settingschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/chatbot-settings/ai-settings)
[NextAI Settingschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings)

Last updated 15 days ago

# Basic Configuration | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#basic-configuration)

Basic Configuration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Basic Configuration** section allows you to set up the core AI capabilities of your website chatbot. This includes integrating an LLM provider, managing AI message usage, and enabling third-party app integrations required for advanced automation.

This setup is essential for activating AI-powered conversations and connecting your chatbot with external tools.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#accessing-basic-configuration)

Accessing Basic Configuration

1.  **Create Your Bots**
    

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

1.  **Chatbot Settings**
    

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  Open the **Basic Configuration** section.
    

From here, you can configure the foundational AI and integration settings for your chatbot.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FM9hrY70nKZYgxRjizmNr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b045397-7a42-4628-8a4a-7686481f4a22&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac609a40&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#integrate-llm-provider)

Integrate LLM Provider

To enable AI-generated responses, you must first integrate a **Large Language Model (LLM) Provider**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#steps-to-integrate-an-llm-provider)

Steps to Integrate an LLM Provider

1.  Under Basic Configuration, click Integrate LLM Provider.
    
2.  You will be redirected to the Third-party Apps Integration page.
    
3.  Browse or search for the supported ChatGPT.
    
4.  Click Connect.
    
5.  Enter the required API credentials and complete authorization.
    

Once connected, the LLM provider will power your chatbot’s AI responses.

> ⚠️ LLM integration is mandatory for AI-based chatbot behavior.

[BotPenguin Integrationschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FSumx7Zg6DOnU75TwxdnK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabec25c1-2f18-4d11-8ae8-ce2e6a8710c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e917a82a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#third-party-apps-integration-llm-and-tools)

Third-party Apps Integration (LLM & Tools)

The **Third-party Apps Integration** page lists all supported external applications, CRMs, scheduling tools, payment gateways, and AI providers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#what-you-can-do-here)

What You Can Do Here

*   Connect AI/LLM providers
    
*   Integrate CRMs to capture and sync leads
    
*   Enable appointment scheduling tools
    
*   Add payment gateways for transactions
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#how-to-connect-an-app)

How to Connect an App

1.  Use the **Search** field to find the app you want.
    
2.  Click **Connect** next to the app name.
    
3.  Complete the authentication steps.
    
4.  Once successful, the app status will update from **Not Connected** to **Connected**.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#integration-status)

Integration Status

*   **Not Connected** – App is available but not yet linked.
    
*   **Connected** – App is successfully integrated and ready to use in chatflows.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#purchase-ai-messages-add-on)

Purchase AI Messages Add-on

AI responses consume AI message credits. If your current plan limit is reached, you can purchase additional AI messages.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#how-to-purchase-ai-messages)

How to Purchase AI Messages

1.  In **Basic Configuration**, click **Purchase AI Messages Add-on**.
    
2.  Choose the required AI message pack.
    
3.  Complete the payment process.
    
4.  AI messages will be added to your account instantly.
    

This ensures uninterrupted AI conversations with your users.

[business-timeBuying Add-Onschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fe77XwOIL0VggwORSsLaz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc19b0ab1-ce80-4a06-9a47-6f02a3eb8c0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be866575&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#how-basic-configuration-works-together)

How Basic Configuration Works Together

Once Basic Configuration is completed:

*   The **LLM provider** powers intelligent, real-time AI responses
    
*   **Third-party integrations** enable automation and data syncing
    
*   **AI message add-ons** ensure scalability for high conversation volumes
    

Together, these settings form the foundation for advanced chatbot behavior.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#important-notes)

Important Notes

> ⚠️ AI responses will not work without an active LLM provider. ⚠️ Ensure API credentials are valid during integration. ⚠️ AI message usage depends on your plan and add-ons.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#what-to-do-next)

What to Do Next

After completing Basic Configuration, you can:

*   Design AI-powered chatflows
    
*   Configure chatbot personality
    
*   Use integrations inside flows (CRM, scheduling, payments)
    
*   Monitor AI usage and performance
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/basic-configuration#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues while integrating an LLM provider or third-party apps, contact us at: 📧 [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#23505653534c515763414c5753464d44564a4d0d404c4e)

Our team will respond within **48 business hours**.

[PreviousAI Settingschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings)
[NextConfiguring Chatbot Scenarioschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/configuring-chatbot-scenarios)

# AI Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings#botpenguin-ai)

BotPenguin AI

BotPenguin utilizes a combination of ChatGPT, proprietary technology, and specialized training to create custom AI models tailored to your business's unique knowledge and customer service needs.

You can feed data to your custom AI model through various sources, including website URLs, content files, and FAQs. This enables BotPenguin to develop AI solutions that deliver exceptional service and support to your customers by leveraging both publicly available information and your business-specific data.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings#setup-chatgpt-and-ai-settings)

Setup ChatGPT and AI Settings

To integrate ChatGPT into your BotPenguin chatbot and customize its behavior, follow these steps:

**Step 1: Create Your Bots**

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

**Step 2: Chatbot Settings**

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

**Step 3: Configure Bot's Personality**

*   Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up:
    
*   Go to Configure Bot's personality
    
*   Toggle off "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed option" to create your own AI persona
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYVlnuOGyL6qd6Y2532ue%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b7554be-3015-4843-92e5-478712e5bda4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78ea38e0&sv=2)

*   Click on settings icon to change the existing persona or click on **"use persona"** to use the existing one .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmmMqxalxGsYmDqyc88oU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D628b71d5-e5eb-4448-9eb2-72ccae878422&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32c3dc32&sv=2)

*   Click on Create persona button to create a new persona
    

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252F0B1YAMnq64N6qgvVff7z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea820ef-33bf-454d-8c3a-d98aa6d5a37c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da9b7828&sv=2)

*   In these settings, you can define the persona details to:
    
    *   **Configure Bot's Personality**
        
    *   **Answer Length**
        
    *   **Answer Perspective (1st person, 3rd person, etc.)**
        
    *   **Tone**
        
    *   **Language**
        
    *   **Answer Formatting**
        
    *   **Included Sources for Response**
        
    *   **Custom Prompt Instructions**
        
    *   **Manage Unusual Chat Scenarios**
        
    *   **Message for When Bot Can't Answer**
        
    *   **Message for Responding to Inappropriate Language Usage**
        
    

Persona Details

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FHgX8z0KhVWUM9IM9oZVg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4211c2cc-a205-4dd8-b22f-5a9d12c6583c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c510746&sv=2)

*   In Persona Details enter the persona title, persona description and upload a cover photo for your bot's persona.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOBUmVEwsm8SBzstZMept%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2d78f22-6bdb-41e4-a63d-3a8766772a2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4286c154&sv=2)

*   In Communication Style, enter answer length, answer as (1st person , 2nd person etc), tone of bot, language used and answer formating. You can also toggle ON/OFF sources and personalize replies with chat history.
    
*   If "include sources for response" is ON it will share the source name of the knowledge base.
    

**Chat Scenerios**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F64lR3IiXmfOGhLXaLUN2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d784a0-98bb-4092-8808-2ad6b1563adc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7246a797&sv=2)

*   You can add a chat scenerio by clicking on "Add Action".
    
*   In Chat Scenarios, select or add an action which gets triggered based on the user's response.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FgvPr2ccHHX2l3OgqMOqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c919357-761b-4d53-985a-cac945d717ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65dd37b8&sv=2)

*   Here you can add a keyword according to which LLM model will identify the chat intent and will give message or flow set by you.
    
*   You can add the chat Intent and message.
    

**Custom Instructions:**

*   In Custom Instructions, add a custom prompt which best defines your bot persona and based on that it will act. Example: "Act as a salesman and use formal tone and be polite and friendly"
    
*   And finally click on "Update" to save the changes.
    
*   You can click on "Use Persona" to use it in you chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdmhfrxKWLhxnOPj6Nlgq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aca1a95-3e0d-4323-8205-60d4b3cf71b9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb9f289e&sv=2)

**Persona in Use**

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FeFcSnMU78LLXa8mbU3Cs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5171d242-b623-44d0-b8cf-81e8bce2eb91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea672433&sv=2)

*   Finally the AI model in your chatflow will work based on the persona set by you.
    

Note : You can decide how many queries/answers to be handled via AI. After that you can continue your chat flow. Available in Customize Bot Message.

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FHToxSrHGwf1yRpb5H1Jx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94419ec1-a898-4ab2-9213-679020d0f0db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5e214a0&sv=2)

**Step 4: Configure ChatGPT Component**

*   Integrate ChatGPT model with your bot for better outputs.
    
*   You can invoke the ChatGPT component at multiple points in the chatflow as needed.
    
*   Select a GPT model you want to use after integrating with ChatGPT.
    

circle-info

Initially it will be set on GPT-3.5 Turbo

And you're done! Whenever the ChatGPT component is invoked, your custom-trained model will provide responses based on the settings and training you've configured, enhancing your chatbot's conversational abilities.

# How to get the GPT Assistant key and connect it with the bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#what-is-a-gpt-assistant)

What is a GPT Assistant?

A **GPT Assistant** is an AI-powered virtual assistant built using OpenAI’s GPT models that can understand natural language and generate human-like responses. It is commonly used to automate conversations, answer questions, provide support, generate content, and assist users across channels like websites, apps, and messaging platforms (e.g., WhatsApp).

In platforms like BotPenguin, a GPT Assistant can be connected to handle customer queries, FAQs, lead qualification, and conversational workflows intelligently.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#pros-of-using-a-gpt-assistant)

✅ Pros of Using a GPT Assistant

*   **24/7 Availability:** Responds to users instantly at any time without human intervention.
    
*   **Natural Conversations:** Understands context and provides human-like, conversational replies.
    
*   **Scalable Support:** Handles multiple conversations simultaneously without performance issues.
    
*   **Reduced Support Costs:** Minimizes dependency on human agents for repetitive queries.
    
*   **Customizable Responses:** Can be trained or prompted to follow your brand tone and business rules.
    
*   **Multi-Use Capabilities:** Useful for support, sales, onboarding, FAQs, and content generation.
    
*   **Continuous Improvement:** Gets smarter over time with better prompts and structured inputs.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-api-key)

How to Get the GPT Assistant API Key

Follow these steps to generate your GPT (OpenAI) API key:

**Step 1: Sign in to OpenAI**

Go to the OpenAI platform and log in with your account.

**Step 2: Open API Keys Page**

After logging in, navigate to **View API Keys** from your account dashboard.

**Step 3: Create a New API Key**

Click on **Create new secret key** and copy the generated key.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FesOyCb4MBgFeJ1Q7qJfT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70a29dcc-0a00-48ac-8b30-cac6290f7b5b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e4dead1&sv=2)

**Step 4: Save the Key Securely**

Store the API key safely. For security reasons, you won’t be able to view it again.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FXbJXNa1xiIYhhKwiYSTa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D351793ba-03b6-4e40-b252-26d6ec3d18ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb2c36ec&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FArQ7nV8cQyXzmNblEpiI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6217e71-84ae-4839-93a0-bc19f5ce1dc9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d87894cf&sv=2)

**Step 5: Add the Key to Your Platform**

*   Select your Bot
    
*   Go to Third party Integrations
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fydlnu9KKiw4avGKLXRg2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fa9bcb3-e1fc-4bac-9882-8b0929eced7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e110af39&sv=2)

*   Search the ChatGPT and click on Connect Button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FqQbEnAYJqr6teuIeT6jU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fd28d5d-0fc5-4b40-92e0-c864e7e70cff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4dc89174&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8eno2bsSr9NqJ0iPomq3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33c6da51-08cf-4056-a694-cc40830daad9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=920b4111&sv=2)

*   Paste the copied API key , select the model and select the knowlede mix.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWmFJZXXWsilgrLC8m1KF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a1f230f-05a0-4c71-b687-b5e7fbe65cb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=206726bc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#how-to-connect-gpt-assistant-with-your-bot)

How to Connect GPT Assistant with Your Bot

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#step-1-create-a-gpt-assistant)

Step 1: Create a GPT Assistant

1.  Go to your **Settings** → **AI Assistants Configuration** → **Basic Configuration**.
    
2.  Under **AI Service Provider**, select **Integrate with ChatGPT**.
    
3.  In **Choose Model**, select **Assistants Beta**.
    
4.  Paste the **GPT Assistant Key** you copied earlier.
    
5.  Click **Update** to save the changes.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fck07VEBBgHR9KAaQhctz%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-06%2520at%25205.12.31%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3abb39d2-8163-4241-8fd8-d452766f1454&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48da69c8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#step-2-setup-of-ai-assistant)

Step 2: Setup of AI Assistant

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnYo7HCXOfMIgrtS5FS5r%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-06%2520at%25205.13.33%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4af2dbb-fbc1-4cd2-8fd7-637cc8e4d859&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=210a3890&sv=2)

1.  Click **Add Assistant**.
    
2.  Enter an **Assistant Name**.
    
3.  Select the **Model** (e.g., GPT-4o).
    
4.  Set **Temperature** and **Top-P** as needed.
    
5.  Add your **Custom Prompt** (instructions that define how the assistant should behave).
    
6.  Click **Add Assistant** or **Update Assistant**.
    
7.  Enable the assistant using the **Status toggle**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FndMJuWxHjfFEOW0jqGCR%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-06%2520at%25205.13.47%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaa7f385-c542-40d2-9cc4-768e0d8ab824&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca487f8&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#step-4-edit-the-assistant)

Step 4: Edit The Assistant

1.  From the list select any assistant that you would like to edit by clicking on edit icon.
    
2.  Update the details.
    
3.  Click on the Update Assistant.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOfWejJrnm9sA8CcD3fLv%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-06%2520at%25205.14.53%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7696e769-9a34-4a40-87ae-82ad02198b51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d9c848b3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/how-to-get-the-gpt-assistant-key-and-connect-it-with-the-bot#test-the-bot)

Test the Bot

*   Open your chatbot and send a test message.
    
*   The bot will now respond using the configured **GPT Assistant logic and instructions**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZIH21Ui9DFFnEvtZnwE6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafd55b74-e6f1-44df-bf50-13429c15771c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfa32b95&sv=2)

# ChatGPT | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#what-is-chatgpt-integration)

What is ChatGPT Integration?

The ChatGPT Integration enables your bot to leverage OpenAI’s advanced natural language capabilities directly inside BotPenguin. By connecting your OpenAI API key, you unlock contextual responses, powerful reasoning, and more human-like conversational flows.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#benefits-of-chatgpt-integration)

Benefits of ChatGPT Integration

*   ⚡ Enhances conversational intelligence for more dynamic user interactions.
    
*   🤖 Provides contextual and human-like responses with minimal training overhead.
    
*   🎯 Reduces manual scripting efforts by generating responses on the fly.
    
*   🚀 Boosts customer satisfaction with smart, fast, and accurate answers.
    
*   🛠️ Integrates seamlessly with your existing chatflows and automation logic.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

Integrate ChatGPT

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#xvw43v6b0iop)

Steps to Integrate BotPenguin with ChatGPT

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#xvw43v6b0iop-1)

Step 1 of 5: Log in to your BotPenguin Account and Select ChatGPT Integration

1.  Login to your BotPenguin account. Then, select and click the Bot you want to integrate with ChatGPT. Click on the **"Third Party Apps Integration"**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR02Gy8CIXoED5HpPI3SI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6792b14b-6e38-4435-adbb-4f03988fae77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=826f5b41&sv=2)

1.  A list of all native integrations for BotPenguin will be available in this window. Find ChatGPT by
    
2.  Either by scrolling down the list, or
    
3.  By typing **‘**ChatGPT**’** in the Search Box with the placeholder **“Search Here”.**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F4qTAIGGAceh8HGT0vtYB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe8a615b-47c2-4fcd-a81c-270eedbab417&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70dda506&sv=2)

1.  Click On The **‘Connect’** button as shown.
    
2.  An Integration Details page will show up. Continue by clicking on the "Connect" button.
    
3.  Enter all the details shown on the subsequent page to connect ChatGPT to your chatbot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCAJUQKMJvUiJlnpjfrVP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da16d34c6-86d6-4a1a-8753-4a84c815f7c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4ca7737&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#nzrqyz7o2otx)

Step 2 of 5: Find your Authorization Key/Token in App Account

1.  To get the API Token, log-in, or create the Open AI account, and on the main dashboard.
    

1.  Click on the "API Platform" on the left hand side, followed by the "API login"
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCEod1v4U2MShDxlyFvAU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94439918-e4c4-4605-a874-749eb5f6f971&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa1a997f&sv=2)

Click on "API Platform"

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FbFjT5tFyEjEr1IZaTQ04%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e0e3eb7-5e64-44cc-9daf-4a15b21bbe6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=212948c4&sv=2)

Click on "API Log In"

1.  You will be directed to the "platform.openai.com/docs/overview" page, where search for "API Keys" in the search bar and select the option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIDyALcVFfaFAqbg8oF1y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6a8db00-5e14-4bef-9b11-6e42aa1263ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76ad65b0&sv=2)

1.  The page that opens will contain options to create new API keys. Click on the "**Create new secret key**" button in the center.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFk1iAJhUp8XA7JmkxDEM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72befef7-3bec-403c-9397-c6a2535d2f57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b57a0cfb&sv=2)

1.  Enter the required details on the opened form. Choose the service account. The details include:
    
    1.  Service Key Name(Optional): The name of the API key.
        
    2.  The Project for which the key will be used.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRrXqIqVRlBSdf7cQg0Lv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ac5c920-a60f-4c4f-b53e-a67bbb85b002&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d5b6092&sv=2)

circle-info

To add the names of projects, go to "Project->General" on the left hand side, right above the API Keys tab, and enter the name of the new project.

1.  After entering the relevant details and clicking "Create secret key", the secret key will be created. **Save the key in a secure method**, as you won't be able to view it again.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FezeZzHK5gLn2OjewwICV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D245892fe-e061-4c64-a9ee-cc6418d288e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=626e7eed&sv=2)

1.  Click on "**Done**", and the following will be displayed:
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJRYmZKoctpC7uolKmJrl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00e6929f-57a3-48b8-bbf9-84e71a3e9c64&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d03edf19&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

Remember to add credits to the API token, as without the token, the API key will remain inactive and will give error if used.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#id-2xyz17m6s45r)

Step 3 of 5: Adding Credits to ChatGPT:

1.  To add credits to your ChatGPT token, open the left hand sidebar. You will see a billings tab. Proceed to click on the "Billing" Tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMa9GxRDzR4O55R5uRBsj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ac9aba3-9537-4aad-9776-313a57b4ee15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29e90f0d&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Add Payment details" and input of details.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FqXAKMi7k25KlOxHwKnj9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0022738b-aa62-4b96-966a-42a187150a77&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a95312&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

The OpenAI platform only accepts credit cards as viable payment options.

1.  Once all the details have been added, click on continue to save the details. Now, all your keys will have credits, and will be viable keys.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#id-2xyz17m6s45r-1)

Step 4 of 5: Enter the API key in BotPenguin to Connect with ChatGPT

1.  Enter the secret key, and press **Authenticate,** to complete the integration of BotPenguin with ChatGPT.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FDTa9DOGbaskNfd5ld6Fw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde8d9297-fcaa-49fd-9645-e341655cc9f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15fb8b93&sv=2)

1.  Also select which model of ChatGPT you want to have integrated with the bot. The o options for the same are:
    
    1.  GPT 3.5
        
    2.  GPT 4
        
    3.  GPT 4 Turbo
        
    4.  GPT 4o
        
    5.  Assistants Beta\*
        
    
2.  Lastly, choose the from where you want the bot to gain its training/information from:
    
    1.  General: Work just like a general ChatGPT
        
    2.  Knowledge Base: Work only with the knowledge it was trained for.
        
    3.  Knowledge Base With General GPT: Work with a combination of both.
        
    
3.  Click on connect. If configured properly, ChatGPT should properly connect to the bot.
    
4.  Also, your ChatGPT integration will reflect the message **Installed** in the Integration List.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FyaTltDQI4rsyBKWA4eH3%252FScreenshot%2520%28111%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4fb6c5f-8001-4e40-b02a-34b4e76aef49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=479bf6aa&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#x3dzdlz6r1mf)

Step 5 of 5: Test your Integration Setup with Data

Once you have established a connection between **BotPenguin** and **ChatGPT**, you are ready for your first NLP-enabled customer interaction. You can test your integration setup by creating a dummy lead on the bot.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#kv3gzu3jags5)

FAQ's

chevron-rightWhy am I getting blank or incomplete responses from ChatGPT?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#why-am-i-getting-blank-or-incomplete-responses-from-chatgpt)

This typically happens when incorrect API credentials are entered or when the OpenAI project lacks credits. Verify the API token and key, confirm the integration URL is correct, and ensure your OpenAI project has active billing and available credits.

chevron-rightWhy is my ChatGPT integration showing an error even after entering the API key?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#why-is-my-chatgpt-integration-showing-an-error-even-after-entering-the-api-key)

Errors commonly occur when the API key is associated with an inactive project or the key lacks required permissions. Confirm the project is active, payment details are added, and the generated secret key was copied and pasted in full without extra whitespace.

chevron-rightDo I need a paid plan to integrate ChatGPT with BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#do-i-need-a-paid-plan-to-integrate-chatgpt-with-botpenguin)

Yes. BotPenguin requires an active paid subscription for ChatGPT integration, and the OpenAI account used for the API key must also have a paid plan with billing enabled.

chevron-rightWhy is my bot giving irrelevant or low-quality replies?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#why-is-my-bot-giving-irrelevant-or-low-quality-replies)

Low-quality responses typically indicate inadequate or poorly structured training data. Review the bot’s Knowledge Base content, refine prompts and context in your chatflow, and select the appropriate model mode (General, Knowledge Base, or Hybrid).

chevron-rightWhy is ChatGPT not appearing inside the chatflow after integration?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#why-is-chatgpt-not-appearing-inside-the-chatflow-after-integration)

The ChatGPT component becomes available only after successful authentication. Revisit the Integration page, confirm the status shows Installed, and validate that the API key was authenticated successfully.

chevron-rightWhat should I do if my API key is lost?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#what-should-i-do-if-my-api-key-is-lost)

OpenAI does not allow re-displaying secret keys for security reasons. Generate a new secret key in the OpenAI dashboard and update the key within the BotPenguin configuration.

chevron-rightWhich ChatGPT models can I use inside BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#which-chatgpt-models-can-i-use-inside-botpenguin)

BotPenguin supports models based on your OpenAI subscription and permissions, including GPT-3.5, GPT-4, GPT-4 Turbo, GPT-4o, GPT-5, and Assistants Beta where applicable.

chevron-rightWhy is my API key not being accepted on BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#why-is-my-api-key-not-being-accepted-on-botpenguin)

Confirm that the key belongs to the correct OpenAI project, has not been revoked or expired, and was copied exactly (no missing characters or additional whitespace). Also verify there are no organization-level restrictions on the key.

chevron-rightCan I use ChatGPT only with a Knowledge Base?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#can-i-use-chatgpt-only-with-a-knowledge-base)

Yes. You can configure ChatGPT to operate in one of three modes:

*   **General** — standard ChatGPT behavior.
    
*   **Knowledge Base** — responses restricted to your uploaded data.
    
*   **Knowledge Base + General** — hybrid mode combining your data with general model capabilities.
    

chevron-rightWhat should I do if none of the troubleshooting steps help?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#what-should-i-do-if-none-of-the-troubleshooting-steps-help)

If you have tried all the troubleshooting steps and are still experiencing issues, please contact BotPenguin support for further assistance. Provide detailed information about the problem and any error messages you have encountered to help us resolve your issue more efficiently.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/chatgpt#kv3gzu3jags5-1)

Still Not Working, Let’s Troubleshoot!

If you are getting blank responses or undesired responses :

*   **Wrong Authorization Details**\- You will be required to check and see if all the authorization credentials, such as API Token, API key, and/or URL, have been entered correctly.
    
*   **Free plan**\- You are not subscribed to the paid plan on BotPenguin or ChatGPT, as integration works only in the paid plan.
    
*   Training Data- The training data you provided was ineffective or inept.
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#cfbcbabfbfa0bdbb8fada0bbbfaaa1a8baa6a1e1aca0a2)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# AI Chat Summary | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#ai-what-is-chat-summary)

AI What is Chat Summary?

AI Chat Summary allows you to automatically generate short AI-powered summaries of conversations between users and your bots, AI agents or live agents. These summaries highlight the user’s intent, key questions, and final outcomes, helping teams quickly understand conversations without reading the full chat.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#benefits-of-configuring-ai-chat-summary)

Benefits of Configuring AI Chat Summary

*   ⚡ Saves time by eliminating the need to read full conversations.
    
*   🧠 Helps agents quickly understand user intent and context.
    
*   📊 Improves reporting and follow-up efficiency.
    
*   💬 Ensures consistent conversation summaries across the team.
    
*   💰 Optimizes AI credit usage with interaction-based restrictions.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#how-to-use-configure-chat-summary)

How to Use Configure Chat Summary

1.  Go to the **“Bots”** section from the left sidebar.
    
2.  Select the bot for which you want to enable chat summary.
    
3.  Navigate to **“AI Settings”**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  Open **“Configure Chat Summary”**.
    
2.  Turn on the **“AI Chat Summary”** toggle.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FAYtHlV9p7Cd1kTaa9vzb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e58ac25-bae1-4fd7-9a11-87b8f45c1404&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdb88bf5&sv=2)

circle-info

Each summary generation uses **one AI message credit** from the configured LLM key. If no key is added, it will use the free credits provided by our platform to every user. Once enabled, the remaining configuration options will become available.

1.  Select your preferred language from **“Preferred Summary Language.”** For example, if **English** is selected, the summary will be generated in English.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2Y4Xt3zR7k6LVEOiPXqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10d493b1-d8da-4935-b078-c8cfee2339dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47d6b439&sv=2)

1.  Enable the toggle if you would like to **“Generate only if user interacted”** .
    

**ON:** The system will generate a chat summary only if the user has sent at least one message in the conversation.

**OFF:** The system will generate a chat summary for all chats, even if the user did not send any message.

1.  Enable **“Restrict based on number of messages”** and enter the minimum interaction count.
    
2.  Add your custom instructions in the **“Custom Prompt”** field to define how summaries should be generated.
    

circle-check

To learn best practices, go to this link : [Setting Up Your AI Agent: Guidelines and Best Practices](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/setting-up-your-ai-agent/setting-up-your-ai-agent-guidelines-and-best-practices)

1.  Click **“Save”** to apply the settings.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FjlqsfMqwZW4Eq8fFHNGE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8191d3f-7168-4f65-b2f0-a84b73cfcaa8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcfd8917&sv=2)

1.  After saving the changes, the **AI Summary component** will appear in the **Inbox** section.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVXwEdqsBXGofZn9apRUV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daceb8915-bf3b-4a97-a215-7e15d1d61536&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e237589a&sv=2)

1.  Clicking the **AI Summary icon** opens a popup with options to:
    
    1.  Generate the AI summary
        
    2.  Go to the chat
        
    
2.  Clicking **“Generate”** will create a summary for that specific conversation.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FaSMYhC19xu4hzPtUMaiC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c193f38-bea1-49ec-9de0-6ee019684290&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a08d3537&sv=2)

1.  The AI summary will be generated once the chat is completed.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0OhirRCW44lviXHZoZ5B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa4bed84-eb13-442c-912b-9090bd72518a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e4be4d8&sv=2)

1.  You can also generate the summary from the chat itself by clicking on the **"Generate"** button.
    

circle-info

**The AI Summary icon will only be visible if:**

*   The **AI Assistance** toggle is enabled in the user’s plan, **and**
    
*   **AI Chat Summary** is enabled for the specific bot or agent.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtYVx9Ux8y9zWqwSxesfy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De875c74d-8b71-4321-a52f-2869dc26f92a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4215550d&sv=2)

* * *

🎉 Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section! You're one step closer to mastering BotPenguin.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-right**Does generating a chat summary consume credits?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#does-generating-a-chat-summary-consume-credits)

Yes. Each time a summary is generated, one AI credit is consumed from your available AI messages or API key credits.

chevron-right**When is the AI summary generated automatically?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#when-is-the-ai-summary-generated-automatically)

The summary is generated automatically once the chat is completed, based on the configuration you have set, such as interaction limits or user participation.

chevron-right**Can I control when summaries are generated?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#can-i-control-when-summaries-are-generated)

Yes. You can enable options like “Generate only if user interacted” or set a minimum number of messages using the “Restrict based on number of messages” setting.

chevron-right**Where can I view the AI chat summary?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#where-can-i-view-the-ai-chat-summary)

You can view the summary in the Inbox by clicking the AI Summary icon. It opens a popup where you can generate or review the summary for that conversation.

chevron-right**If I enable the Chat Summary for one specific bot, will it be automatically enabled for the other bots as well?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#if-i-enable-the-chat-summary-for-one-specific-bot-will-it-be-automatically-enabled-for-the-other-bot)

No, the Chat Summary feature is bot-specific and must be enabled separately for each bot.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

Last updated 15 days ago
