# Integrate BotPenguin with WooCommerce | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#what-is-woocommerce-integration)

What is WooCommerce Integration?

WooCommerce Integration allows your BotPenguin WhatsApp bot to seamlessly connect with your WooCommerce store. By enabling this integration, you can send automated WhatsApp notifications for order updates, abandoned carts, returns, and more — ensuring customers stay informed at every stage of their shopping journey.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#benefits-of-woocommerce-integration)

Benefits of WooCommerce Integration

*   🎯 Automates customer updates for orders, returns, and carts.
    
*   🟢 Improves customer engagement and boosts conversions.
    
*   🎯 Helps recover lost sales through abandoned cart reminders.
    
*   🟢 Reduces manual effort in sending follow-up messages.
    
*   🎯 Ensures a smooth post-purchase experience with instant updates.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#prerequisites)

Prerequisites:

The following prerequisites need to be met when you are integrating WooCommerce with WhatsApp bot.

*   Having a WhatsApp Chatbot
    
*   Having a WooCommerce Web Store
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#step-1-of-4-login-to-your-botpenguin-account-and-select-application-to-integrate)

Step 1 of 4: Login to your BotPenguin Account and Select Application to Integrate:

1.  Login to your BotPenguin account. Now, select and click the WhatsApp chatbot you want to integrate with WooCommerce. Click on the “**Third-party Apps Integration”.**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FpYZpPGkWBIROAACitbEC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ec87db2-f0e5-4a42-9ecc-8e2ff35232b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ee489b1&sv=2)

1.  Go to WooCommerce integration either by:
    
    1.  Searching for WooCommerce on the search bar available, or
        
    2.  Scrolling down to WooCommerce.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fvgm2Ccebif1wOGlWwkiv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9049b89-ca46-496a-a753-12906735b542&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c19418f&sv=2)

1.  As shown below, a page requiring for the input of your WooCommerce Shop URL, and the WooCommerce API Plugin Key.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2jDLis6DPfs20MgWG4i8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01cd3135-c514-4f23-a133-487f96f1f6c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3500beeb&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#step-2-of-4-add-woocommerce-shop-url-and-whatsapp-api-key)

Step 2 of 4: Add WooCommerce Shop URL and WhatsApp API Key

**WooCommerce Shop URL:**

*   Go to your WooCommerce store.
    
*   Copy the **base URL** of your shop.
    
*   Paste it into the **WooCommerce Shop URL** box in BotPenguin.
    

**WhatsApp API Key:**

*   Go to your selected **WhatsApp bot settings** inside BotPenguin.
    
*   Click on the **API Key** tab.
    
*   Copy the **API key** shown there.
    
*   Paste it into the **API Key** field in the WooCommerce integration page.
    

Once both fields are filled, click **“Save”** to establish the connection.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#id-2xyz17m6s45r)

Step 3 of 4: Edit the integration configurations in BotPenguin

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FccvxLv4DvigvS0HotDhO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0289aa4e-ae79-4b8f-807d-8802fab0213c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7c3d230&sv=2)

A variety of actions are available for automation of messages after going to the “**Automated Messages**” tab, such as:

* * *

1.  **Abandoned Recovery Message**
    

Customers often leave items in their carts without completing a purchase. This feature allows you to send **automated follow-up messages** to encourage them to return and complete their orders.

This is done through the manual toggling of the button, following which user is prompted select a template of the message that needs to be sent. If some variables are included in the template, the input of those values are also necessary, along with fallback values, and additional header media(additional image, video, or document that can be attached to the message for better engagement.)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8oLJTKNAXW4KRNwzYKCY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb019091-fffb-4ceb-91d5-f1f80c3a3bfe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=129ec589&sv=2)

1.  **Order Completed**
    

Once a customer successfully places an order, this feature sends an **order confirmation message** instantly. It reassures the customer that their purchase has been processed.

This is done through the manual toggling of the button, following which user is prompted select a template of the message that needs to be sent. If some variables are included in the template, the input of those values are also necessary, along with fallback values, and additional header media(additional image, video, or document)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FqRP3W4opbtIPjC4d5eHi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b3aa46d-d6ee-4139-94f7-e230dda47240&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3fd38c96&sv=2)

1.  **Order Fulfillment**
    

When an order is shipped, BotPenguin can automatically notify customers with a **shipment confirmation message**.

This is done through the manual toggling of the button, following which user is prompted select a template of the message that needs to be sent. If some variables are included in the template, the input of those values are also necessary, along with fallback values, and additional header media(additional image, video, or document)

* * *

1.  **Return/Exchange Request**
    

Managing return or exchange requests manually can be time-consuming. This feature sends an **automated acknowledgment message** when a customer requests a refund or exchange.

This is done through the manual toggling of the button, following which user is prompted select a template of the message that needs to be sent. If some variables are included in the template, the input of those values are also necessary, along with fallback values, and additional header media.

* * *

**5\. Cart Template Message**

For customers who place orders directly from a product catalog, this feature sends an instant confirmation message. It helps in verifying bulk orders and catalog-based purchases, ensuring that the customer receives a summary of their selected products before checkout.

For the correct implementation of this feature, the given code snippet must be pasted in your website's footer or header before the closing </body> tag. Additionally, the content of the message can be selected through template‘s in the “**Select Template**” section. If some variables are included in the template, the input of those values are also necessary, along with fallback values, and additional header media.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJXtCKPG9LEzUxYNr5VMu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47498df9-917c-4d5f-86f7-7a55fcfd61c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4b159fd&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#step-4-of-4-test-your-integration-setup-with-data)

Step 4 of 4: Test your Integration Setup with Data:

Once you have established a connection between **BotPenguin** and **the WooCommerce website, you are ready** for your first test lead. You can test your integration setup by creating a dummy lead on the bot. This lead should appear in your BotPenguin dashboard as well as in the WhatsApp chatbot sent messages.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightDo I need coding knowledge to integrate WooCommerce with BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-integrate-woocommerce-with-botpenguin)

No, the integration is completely no-code. You only need to copy and paste your WooCommerce API keys into BotPenguin.

chevron-rightWhere can I find my WooCommerce Consumer Key and Secret?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#where-can-i-find-my-woocommerce-consumer-key-and-secret)

You can generate them by navigating to \*\*WooCommerce → Settings → Advanced → REST API\*\* in your WordPress admin dashboard.

chevron-rightCan the chatbot share real-time order updates?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#can-the-chatbot-share-real-time-order-updates)

Yes, once connected, your chatbot can fetch order details and update customers in real time.

chevron-rightIs the WooCommerce integration secure?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#is-the-woocommerce-integration-secure)

Yes, the integration uses secure API authentication with Consumer Key and Secret. BotPenguin does not store sensitive customer data.

chevron-rightCan I connect multiple WooCommerce stores?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#can-i-connect-multiple-woocommerce-stores)

Currently, you can integrate one WooCommerce store per BotPenguin account. For multiple stores, use separate BotPenguin accounts.

chevron-rightWhat happens if my API keys expire?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#what-happens-if-my-api-keys-expire)

You’ll need to regenerate new keys in your WooCommerce dashboard and update them in BotPenguin’s integration settings.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-woocommerce#still-not-working-lets-troubleshoot)

**Still Not Working, Let’s Troubleshoot!**

If you are not getting dummy lead, it may be due to the multiple reasons:

*   Wrong Authorization Details added- You will be required to check and see if all the authorization credentials such as API Token, API key, and/or URL has been entered correctly.
    
*   Free plan- You are not subscribed to the paid plan on BotPenguin as integration works only in paid plan.
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f5868085859a8781b5979a8185909b92809c9bdb969a98)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# Integrate BotPenguin with Close CRM | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#x8blz4n9yuhv)

Step 1 of 5: Login to BotPenguin Account and Select Application to Integrate

a. Login to your BotPenguin account. Now, select and click the Bot you want to integrate with Close CRM. Click on the **‘Integrate tab.’**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FBO4ZVfzFVkKJF6wD4zww%252F0%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=948f3c82&sv=2)

b. The Integrate Window Will Open up. Select the **‘All Integrations’** Tab.

c. A list of all native integrations for BotPenguin will be available in this window.

d. Now find Close CRM by:-

*   Either by scrolling down the list or,
    
*   by typing **‘Close’** in the Search Box with the placeholder “Search Integration By Name”
    

e. Now Click On The **‘Connect’** Button As Shown

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLKuMQZg3M7awtjzl94C1%252F1%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2dd5a8a&sv=2)

f. An Interface, as shown below, will open up. Here, you will be asked to enter APi Token that you will get by logging into your Close account.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FTE4ehCa9vvdZjiAwtxcw%252F2%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5aeb17a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#cqibpdrqwf7c)

Step 2 of 5: Find your Authorization Key/Token in App Account

a. To get the API key, login to your Close CRM account. On the left side of the dashboard, scroll down and go to Settings>API Keys.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F22m7TkpQDiX8LyYq396A%252F3%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=adb43de&sv=2)

b. Note your APi Key if listed else you may click **‘New API Key’** to create one.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FX9RLYXFu9OxsXSvbdrCB%252F4%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40b3419c&sv=2)

c. Enter the API Key Name/Label and click **‘Create API Key’.**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnrtxqSzXV6r7wVVbwaP5%252F5%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d679b1a&sv=2)

d. Your new API Key will be generated and listed on the dashboard under API Keys name. Copy the API Key

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtqHkEX4vCxGlxD9N4Vwo%252F6%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45437742&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FvvjRN5BkD25BwMQ2CCKN%252F7%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f7f21d8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#wsidcausdjp2)

Step 3 of 5: Enter Authorization Details and establish connection with your App

a. Enter Close CRM APi key, and click the ‘Connect’ Button to complete integration of BotPenguin.

b. If you have entered all the details correctly, you will see a notification that says, “**Integrated Successfully.”**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fb3DauoRJruFEGGhhrG5Q%252F8%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7155327&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#id-66fx78md5116)

Step 4 of 5: Set up Mapping Parameters

a. Now, as connection of the BotPenguin and Close CRM is established, you need to map **parameters (fields) of Close CRM** to the user response of the BotPenguin question. You can use the **+Add Parameters** button to add more fields.

For example, you select a question from All bot questions/components: Please provide your name? Then, you map it with the parameter -Name.

As a result, this mapping will enable integration to send the user's response from BotPenguin to the Close CRM’s **Name** field in the leads. Similarly, in order for integration to work properly, you will require to map all other questions/ components of your Bot to Close CRM fields.

circle-info

The queries/questions options will be auto fetched from your bot chat flow, So, make sure you configure your chat flow first.

b. Select the **‘Lead ID’**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FWqUWnPNgrqbfmiyux6Lg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1362d037-bfe7-423a-b38a-84b3885815e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=834d69f2&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F6Tz5eQoMjiqyI8VPZCcA%252F10%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c73b933&sv=2)

c. If you have entered all the details correctly, you will see a notification that says, “**Mapping successfully.”**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FD3eFAGqmwWSi3fTXQT9g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a09cbca-636a-4e2b-b7d0-a14ab8f174f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6e01f42&sv=2)

d. Also, your Close integration will show the message **Installed** in the Integration List.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FkOZXkvOT28tLpB3q3UK2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e69070f-e1bf-49a4-8945-3ac7e7174734&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97eebe8d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#id-40sv8rw33b09)

Step 5 of 5: Test your Integration Set up with Data

Once you have established a connection between **BotPenguin** and **Close CRM**, and the mapping is complete, you are ready to go for your first test lead. You can test your integration setup by creating a dummy lead on the bot. This lead should appear in your BotPenguin dashboard as well as in the Close CRM that you have integrated.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-close-crm#rafo1o36o0k)

Still Not Working, Let’s Troubleshoot!

If you are not getting dummy lead from your Bot to Close CRM, it may be due to the multiple reasons:

*   Wrong Authorization Details added- You will be required to check and see if all the authorization credentials such as API Token, API key, and/or URL has been entered correctly.
    
*   Wrong Mapping Set up - Your mapping with BotPenguin Question and CRM parameter is either incorrect or you haven’t added any mandatory parameter.
    
*   Free plan- You are not subscribed to the paid plan on BotPenguin as integration works only in paid plan.
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#aad9dfdadac5d8deeac8c5dedacfc4cddfc3c484c9c5c7)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[NextIntegrate BotPenguin with CalendarHero CRMchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-calendarhero-crm)

# Prerequisites for WhatsApp Bots | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

In order to create the WhatsApp bot using the WhatsApp cloud API, the following things are required.

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-bot-creation-with-manual-onboarding/prerequisites-for-whatsapp-bots#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you start creating the WhatsApp bot, Make sure that you have

*   A phone number that is
    
    *   Active & capable of receiving SMS.
        
    *   Not registered on WhatsApp or WA Business App.
        
    
*   Registered legal business
    
*   An active website with a valid privacy policy
    
*   Business use case compliant with [WhatsApparrow-up-right](https://www.whatsapp.com/legal/commerce-policy)
     and [Meta commerce policyarrow-up-right](https://www.facebook.com/policies_center/commerce/)
    .
    
*   A valid payment method (Debit or Credit card) capable of making international payments to Meta for conversation charges.
    
*   GSTIN Number, Only if the business is registered in India.
    

If you have all of the above checked, You are good to start with WhatsApp Cloud API Bot.

circle-exclamation

Please note that a single mobile number can only be utilized on one of the WhatsApp services at a given time, namely WhatsApp, WA Business, or WhatsApp Business API. If you wish to use your existing number, you are required to remove your account from one service before using it on another.

[PreviousWhatsApp Bot Creation with Manual Onboardingchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-bot-creation-with-manual-onboarding)
[NextCreate a Meta Appchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-bot-creation-with-manual-onboarding/create-a-meta-app)

# General Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **General** section allows you to configure core interaction settings for your Whatsapp chatbot.

Access the general settings:

1.  Go to your selected whatsapp bot.
    
2.  Click on Settings.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPsvhlmMl79MJyabS2NDW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b48c432-02aa-4802-9f5c-09f9269e0654&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ca86570&sv=2)

Below are the fields and their functionalities:

1.  **Session Timeout** Define the time limit after which the chat session will automatically end if the user does not respond to the bot's messages.
    

1.  **Restart Chat Keywords** Specify keywords to restart the chat. For example, entering "restart" will trigger a new chat session. Multiple keywords can be added.
    
2.  **Live Chat Expiry** Set a time limit for live chat requests. If no agent accepts the request within this time, the live chat request will expire.
    
3.  **Live Chat Request Keywords** Add keywords to initiate a live chat request. For instance, typing "live agent" will request live agent support.
    
4.  **Unavailability Message** Customize the message shown when live chat support is unavailable. Example: "Live chat is currently unavailable. Sorry for the inconvenience."
    

1.  **Completion Message** Provide a message that appears when a chat session concludes. This can include instructions for restarting or requesting live chat again.
    
2.  **User Inactivity Message** Configure a message to prompt the user when there is no activity. Example: "It seems you haven't responded. Please reply to continue."
    

[PreviousWhatApp Chatbot Settingschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings)
[NextTriggers Settingschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings)

# AI Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings#botpenguin-ai)

BotPenguin AI

BotPenguin utilizes a combination of ChatGPT, proprietary technology, and specialized training to create custom AI models tailored to your business's unique knowledge and customer service needs.

You can feed data to your custom AI model through various sources, including website URLs, content files, and FAQs. This enables BotPenguin to develop AI solutions that deliver exceptional service and support to your customers by leveraging both publicly available information and your business-specific data.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings#setup-chatgpt-and-ai-settings)

Setup ChatGPT and AI Settings

To integrate ChatGPT into your BotPenguin chatbot and customize its behavior, follow these steps:

**Step 1: Create Your Bots**

*   Begin by creating your chatbots. Once you've completed this step, proceed to the next.
    

**Step 2: Chatbot Settings**

*   Navigate to the "AI settings" .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

**Step 3: Configure Bot's Personality**

*   Access "AI Settings" based on the type of chatbot you're setting up:
    
*   Go to Configure Bot's personality
    
*   Toggle off "Let AI Manage bot's personality as needed option" to create your own AI persona
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYVlnuOGyL6qd6Y2532ue%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b7554be-3015-4843-92e5-478712e5bda4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78ea38e0&sv=2)

*   Click on settings icon to change the existing persona or click on **"use persona"** to use the existing one .
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmmMqxalxGsYmDqyc88oU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D628b71d5-e5eb-4448-9eb2-72ccae878422&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32c3dc32&sv=2)

*   Click on Create persona button to create a new persona
    

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252F0B1YAMnq64N6qgvVff7z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ea820ef-33bf-454d-8c3a-d98aa6d5a37c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da9b7828&sv=2)

*   In these settings, you can define the persona details to:
    
    *   **Configure Bot's Personality**
        
    *   **Answer Length**
        
    *   **Answer Perspective (1st person, 3rd person, etc.)**
        
    *   **Tone**
        
    *   **Language**
        
    *   **Answer Formatting**
        
    *   **Included Sources for Response**
        
    *   **Custom Prompt Instructions**
        
    *   **Manage Unusual Chat Scenarios**
        
    *   **Message for When Bot Can't Answer**
        
    *   **Message for Responding to Inappropriate Language Usage**
        
    

Persona Details

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FHgX8z0KhVWUM9IM9oZVg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4211c2cc-a205-4dd8-b22f-5a9d12c6583c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c510746&sv=2)

*   In Persona Details enter the persona title, persona description and upload a cover photo for your bot's persona.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOBUmVEwsm8SBzstZMept%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2d78f22-6bdb-41e4-a63d-3a8766772a2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4286c154&sv=2)

*   In Communication Style, enter answer length, answer as (1st person , 2nd person etc), tone of bot, language used and answer formating. You can also toggle ON/OFF sources and personalize replies with chat history.
    
*   If "include sources for response" is ON it will share the source name of the knowledge base.
    

**Chat Scenerios**

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F64lR3IiXmfOGhLXaLUN2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d784a0-98bb-4092-8808-2ad6b1563adc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7246a797&sv=2)

*   You can add a chat scenerio by clicking on "Add Action".
    
*   In Chat Scenarios, select or add an action which gets triggered based on the user's response.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FgvPr2ccHHX2l3OgqMOqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c919357-761b-4d53-985a-cac945d717ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65dd37b8&sv=2)

*   Here you can add a keyword according to which LLM model will identify the chat intent and will give message or flow set by you.
    
*   You can add the chat Intent and message.
    

**Custom Instructions:**

*   In Custom Instructions, add a custom prompt which best defines your bot persona and based on that it will act. Example: "Act as a salesman and use formal tone and be polite and friendly"
    
*   And finally click on "Update" to save the changes.
    
*   You can click on "Use Persona" to use it in you chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdmhfrxKWLhxnOPj6Nlgq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aca1a95-3e0d-4323-8205-60d4b3cf71b9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb9f289e&sv=2)

**Persona in Use**

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FeFcSnMU78LLXa8mbU3Cs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5171d242-b623-44d0-b8cf-81e8bce2eb91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea672433&sv=2)

*   Finally the AI model in your chatflow will work based on the persona set by you.
    

Note : You can decide how many queries/answers to be handled via AI. After that you can continue your chat flow. Available in Customize Bot Message.

![](https://partners.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1613146696-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZpVksvLNWoWVCzCZ4a1O%252Fuploads%252FHToxSrHGwf1yRpb5H1Jx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94419ec1-a898-4ab2-9213-679020d0f0db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5e214a0&sv=2)

**Step 4: Configure ChatGPT Component**

*   Integrate ChatGPT model with your bot for better outputs.
    
*   You can invoke the ChatGPT component at multiple points in the chatflow as needed.
    
*   Select a GPT model you want to use after integrating with ChatGPT.
    

circle-info

Initially it will be set on GPT-3.5 Turbo

And you're done! Whenever the ChatGPT component is invoked, your custom-trained model will provide responses based on the settings and training you've configured, enhancing your chatbot's conversational abilities.

# Triggers Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#what-are-whatsapp-triggers)

What are WhatsApp Triggers:

WhatsApp Triggers on BotPenguin are predefined words or phrases that initiate specific actions within a bot conversation. They serve as powerful entry points for restarting conversations, initiating live chats, managing subscriptions and unsubscriptions, and launching specific bot flows. These triggers are also used to define **Ice Breakers** (starter messages users can tap) and **Command Prompts** (typed phrases that trigger specific workflows or bot behaviors). By simply messaging the bot with a trigger word, users can seamlessly navigate to desired actions, making the chatbot more interactive, intuitive, and automation-friendly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#section-a-how-to-use-whatsapp-triggers)

Section A: How to use WhatsApp Triggers:

1.  Sign into you BotPenguin account and select the WhatsApp chatbot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FlABxSCtOoOKjan6zBDZ9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dded63c11-09e0-419e-a930-fecad40acf9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca6e7049&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Settings", and go over to the "Triggers" tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVZjg43tBWkmodwadF4Ww%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d70bf60-af0b-4631-b15b-e76bf2c1c564&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=325a20e9&sv=2)

1.  You will be presented with 4 cards, each designed for different purposes:
    
    1.  Bot Triggers
        
    2.  Chat Flow Triggers
        
    3.  Chatbot Ice Breaker
        
    4.  Chatbot Commands
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#section-b-using-bot-triggers)

Section B: Using Bot Triggers:

You can define the specific words or phrases that act as commands to control key chat actions. These include:

*   **Restart Chatflow Triggers**: Set keywords (e.g., “restart”, “begin again”) that reset the conversation and take the user back to the bot’s starting point.
    
*   **Live Chat Triggers**: Assign words (e.g., “agent”, “help”) that instantly connect the user to a human agent for real-time support.
    
*   **Subscribe/Unsubscribe Triggers**: Configure terms (e.g., “start”, “stop”) to automate user opt-ins and opt-outs from marketing flows or broadcasts.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRZwaI1SC9qJSOTiUl6pe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D859f51f2-03f2-4cf0-81e5-0db1b9b66731&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5799d7d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#section-c-using-chat-flow-triggers)

Section C: Using Chat Flow Triggers:

Configure keywords to automatically initiate specific chatflows based on user messages. Two flexible matching options are available:

*   **Exact Match**: The chatflow is triggered only when the user's message exactly matches the configured keyword (e.g., user types just “pricing”).
    
*   **Contains Match**: The chatflow is triggered if the keyword appears anywhere in the user’s message (e.g., “Can you share pricing details?” triggers the “pricing” flow).
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FY1ffaSz6StfkDUBEvMWL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfba6c645-3313-423c-84be-12ad3884d9cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dafba11&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#section-d-using-chatbot-ice-breaker)

Section D: Using Chatbot Ice Breaker:

Ice Breakers are ready-made message options that show up when someone opens your WhatsApp chatbot for the first time. When a user taps on one, it can start a specific chatbot flow in BotPenguin.

*   Enter the prompt of the Ice Breaker.
    
*   Select the chatflow to be started when the above Ice Breaker is chosen.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F9kTVdDJr91FvhHkOYp3j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0bf7868-b587-4179-b43c-6faaf4cb5eda&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57db240c&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#section-e-using-chatbot-commands)

Section E: Using Chatbot Commands:

Commands let users type a `/` followed by a keyword in the WhatsApp chat to trigger specific bot actions. These commands help users quickly restart a chat, start a live chat, subscribe or unsubscribe, or even trigger a chatflow. They make the chatbot experience faster, smarter, and more interactive—especially for repeat users.

**How to set up Commands:**

*   **Enter a Command Name:** This is the word the user will type after `/` (e.g., `/help`).
    
*   **Add a Description:** Give a short explanation of what the command does.
    
*   **Select the Trigger Action:** Choose what action the command should perform—restart chat, start live chat, subscribe/unsubscribe, or run a chatflow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLjwcEP8RObkl66ABnx6t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D211f0ecc-c2e5-43ba-8f0f-75917fd0e3f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd721437&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#faqs)

FAQ's

chevron-rightCan I assign the same command to multiple actions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#can-i-assign-the-same-command-to-multiple-actions)

No, each command can trigger only one action. You’ll need to create separate commands for different functions.

chevron-rightWill users see a list of available Ice Breakers in the chat?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#will-users-see-a-list-of-available-ice-breakers-in-the-chat)

Yes the users will see a list of all available ice breakers as soon as they open the chat.

chevron-rightCan commands be used in groups or only individual chats?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#can-commands-be-used-in-groups-or-only-individual-chats)

Commands are designed for 1:1 user-to-bot interactions and work best in individual WhatsApp sessions for automation and engagement.

chevron-rightWhat happens if a user types a wrong command?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatapp-chatbot-settings/triggers-settings#what-happens-if-a-user-types-a-wrong-command)

If the typed command doesn’t match any configured action, the bot will treat it as a normal message. It won’t trigger anything unless handled in a fallback or default flow.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#98ebede8e8f7eaecd8faf7ece8fdf6ffedf1f6b6fbf7f5)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# AI Chat Summary | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#ai-what-is-chat-summary)

AI What is Chat Summary?

AI Chat Summary allows you to automatically generate short AI-powered summaries of conversations between users and your bots, AI agents or live agents. These summaries highlight the user’s intent, key questions, and final outcomes, helping teams quickly understand conversations without reading the full chat.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#benefits-of-configuring-ai-chat-summary)

Benefits of Configuring AI Chat Summary

*   ⚡ Saves time by eliminating the need to read full conversations.
    
*   🧠 Helps agents quickly understand user intent and context.
    
*   📊 Improves reporting and follow-up efficiency.
    
*   💬 Ensures consistent conversation summaries across the team.
    
*   💰 Optimizes AI credit usage with interaction-based restrictions.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#how-to-use-configure-chat-summary)

How to Use Configure Chat Summary

1.  Go to the **“Bots”** section from the left sidebar.
    
2.  Select the bot for which you want to enable chat summary.
    
3.  Navigate to **“AI Settings”**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRRuzoRmRuIFXy9pjZ7QT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d5a239-f62b-4753-a28d-0cec2a9419ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=715283e3&sv=2)

1.  Open **“Configure Chat Summary”**.
    
2.  Turn on the **“AI Chat Summary”** toggle.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FAYtHlV9p7Cd1kTaa9vzb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e58ac25-bae1-4fd7-9a11-87b8f45c1404&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdb88bf5&sv=2)

circle-info

Each summary generation uses **one AI message credit** from the configured LLM key. If no key is added, it will use the free credits provided by our platform to every user. Once enabled, the remaining configuration options will become available.

1.  Select your preferred language from **“Preferred Summary Language.”** For example, if **English** is selected, the summary will be generated in English.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2Y4Xt3zR7k6LVEOiPXqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10d493b1-d8da-4935-b078-c8cfee2339dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47d6b439&sv=2)

1.  Enable the toggle if you would like to **“Generate only if user interacted”** .
    

**ON:** The system will generate a chat summary only if the user has sent at least one message in the conversation.

**OFF:** The system will generate a chat summary for all chats, even if the user did not send any message.

1.  Enable **“Restrict based on number of messages”** and enter the minimum interaction count.
    
2.  Add your custom instructions in the **“Custom Prompt”** field to define how summaries should be generated.
    

circle-check

To learn best practices, go to this link : [Setting Up Your AI Agent: Guidelines and Best Practices](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/setting-up-your-ai-agent/setting-up-your-ai-agent-guidelines-and-best-practices)

1.  Click **“Save”** to apply the settings.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FjlqsfMqwZW4Eq8fFHNGE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8191d3f-7168-4f65-b2f0-a84b73cfcaa8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dcfd8917&sv=2)

1.  After saving the changes, the **AI Summary component** will appear in the **Inbox** section.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVXwEdqsBXGofZn9apRUV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daceb8915-bf3b-4a97-a215-7e15d1d61536&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e237589a&sv=2)

1.  Clicking the **AI Summary icon** opens a popup with options to:
    
    1.  Generate the AI summary
        
    2.  Go to the chat
        
    
2.  Clicking **“Generate”** will create a summary for that specific conversation.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FaSMYhC19xu4hzPtUMaiC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c193f38-bea1-49ec-9de0-6ee019684290&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a08d3537&sv=2)

1.  The AI summary will be generated once the chat is completed.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0OhirRCW44lviXHZoZ5B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa4bed84-eb13-442c-912b-9090bd72518a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e4be4d8&sv=2)

1.  You can also generate the summary from the chat itself by clicking on the **"Generate"** button.
    

circle-info

**The AI Summary icon will only be visible if:**

*   The **AI Assistance** toggle is enabled in the user’s plan, **and**
    
*   **AI Chat Summary** is enabled for the specific bot or agent.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FtYVx9Ux8y9zWqwSxesfy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De875c74d-8b71-4321-a52f-2869dc26f92a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4215550d&sv=2)

* * *

🎉 Congratulations, you have successfully completed this section! You're one step closer to mastering BotPenguin.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-right**Does generating a chat summary consume credits?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#does-generating-a-chat-summary-consume-credits)

Yes. Each time a summary is generated, one AI credit is consumed from your available AI messages or API key credits.

chevron-right**When is the AI summary generated automatically?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#when-is-the-ai-summary-generated-automatically)

The summary is generated automatically once the chat is completed, based on the configuration you have set, such as interaction limits or user participation.

chevron-right**Can I control when summaries are generated?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#can-i-control-when-summaries-are-generated)

Yes. You can enable options like “Generate only if user interacted” or set a minimum number of messages using the “Restrict based on number of messages” setting.

chevron-right**Where can I view the AI chat summary?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#where-can-i-view-the-ai-chat-summary)

You can view the summary in the Inbox by clicking the AI Summary icon. It opens a popup where you can generate or review the summary for that conversation.

chevron-right**If I enable the Chat Summary for one specific bot, will it be automatically enabled for the other bots as well?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#if-i-enable-the-chat-summary-for-one-specific-bot-will-it-be-automatically-enabled-for-the-other-bot)

No, the Chat Summary feature is bot-specific and must be enabled separately for each bot.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/ai-settings/ai-chat-summary#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

# Whatsapp Co-existence Feature | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#overview)

Overview

**WhatsApp Co-existence** allows you to use the **same WhatsApp phone number** on:

*   The **WhatsApp Business App**
    
*   **BotPenguin’s WhatsApp Bot**
    

at the same time.

This feature is enabled via **Meta’s Embedded Signup flow**, allowing businesses to start WhatsApp automation **without migrating or disconnecting** their existing WhatsApp Business account.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#what-is-whatsapp-co-existence)

What Is WhatsApp Co-existence?

Traditionally, WhatsApp API required **full number migration**, which removed the number from the WhatsApp app.

With **Co-existence**:

*   Your WhatsApp Business app **remains active**
    
*   BotPenguin can **send and receive messages via Bot**
    
*   Manual and automated conversations run together
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#when-should-you-use-whatsapp-co-existence)

When Should You Use WhatsApp Co-existence?

Use this feature if:

*   You already have an active WhatsApp Business App number
    
*   You want to keep manual conversations
    
*   You want to add bots, automation, and templates
    
*   You don’t want downtime or number migration
    
*   You are testing WhatsApp automation before scaling
    
*   You would like to sync the chats both in Whatsapp ChatBot as well as on Whatsapp business Account
    

circle-exclamation

Please note that we need an ACTIVE WhatsApp Business Acoount to onboard with Co-existance. The acount needs to be in active use for atleast 2-3 weeks before the onbaording via coexistance an be initiated.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#what-you-can-do-with-co-existence)

What You Can Do with Co-existence

With WhatsApp Co-existence enabled, you can:

*   Send & receive messages via WhatsApp API
    
*   Reply manually from the WhatsApp app
    
*   Run chatbots and automated workflows
    
*   Send approved WhatsApp template messages
    
*   Manage chats from both WhatsApp business app and BotPenguin
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before starting setup, ensure:

*   ✔ Active Facebook account
    
*   ✔ Business Manager access (Admin recommended)
    
*   ✔ Valid business website with Privacy Policy
    
*   ✔ WhatsApp-compliant use case
    
*   ✔ Active WhatsApp number (business app)
    
*   ✔ Phone number can receive SMS or voice OTP
    
*   ✔ Valid debit/credit card with international payments enabled
    
*   ✔ GSTIN (mandatory for Indian businesses)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#technical-requirements-mandatory)

Technical Requirements (Mandatory)

For this flow to work successfully:

*   WhatsApp Business App version **2.24.17 or higher**
    
*   Phone number country code must be **supported**
    
*   You must be a **Meta Solution Partner / Tech Provider**
    
*   You must be familiar with **WhatsApp Cloud API**
    
*   Webhook callback must successfully receive and process events
    
*   Embedded Signup must be enabled **with session logging**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-1-open-whatsapp-setup-in-botpenguin)

Step 1: Open WhatsApp Setup in BotPenguin

1.  Log in to **BotPenguin Dashboard**
    
2.  Go to **Bots**
    
3.  Select your bot
    
4.  Click **Replace Demo WhatsApp Number**
    
5.  Choose **Connect your WhatsApp Number**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnLf23cSaE2UM4ooTAkJ5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d0b1bdb-37d6-42fc-b7ef-58d940ebdba4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f50ffe59&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-2-accept-whatsapp-prerequisites)

Step 2: Accept WhatsApp Prerequisites

You will see a prerequisites checklist.

*   Select **All**
    
*   Confirm you meet WhatsApp requirements
    
*   Click **Proceed**
    

(This step confirms compliance with Meta policies.)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8CCtOLfad5Qu7FinyAaK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc58d00df-9edd-4ae4-a497-966e4979e242&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a15be824&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-3-meta-embedded-signup-facebook-login)

Step 3: Meta Embedded Signup (Facebook Login)

You’ll be redirected to Meta’s **Embedded Signup** screen.

Here you need to:

*   Log in using your Facebook account
    
*   Select an existing **Business Manager** or create a new one
    
*   Grant required permissions to BotPenguin
    

Click **Continue**.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQkniqB6BkWLGXfy1qJQz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3da93cc-dbb5-4819-92c4-3ef674208ba5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ea03a3a&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-4-seamlessly-connect-your-account-to-botpenguin)

Step 4: Seamlessly connect your account to BotPenguin

Connect your account to the BotPenguin by giving permissions by clicking on continue button.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPy4s4gn4XAsZaIuLrQlN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debc9ce6f-2616-4823-a434-60c3b2ca46b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd0b5301&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-5-connect-your-business-portfolio-and-choose-the-option-whether-you-want-to-create-or-connect-a)

Step 5: Connect your Business portfolio and Choose the option whether you want to create or connect a Business Account

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3gNC3C5Ld7wBi3RTPlRo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D755eed55-8321-4519-9d2e-48f4f4027a9b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96325da&sv=2)

When configuring **Embedded Signup** for **WhatsApp Business App phone numbers**, business users are given the option to **connect their existing WhatsApp Business App account to the WhatsApp Cloud API** (Co-existence mode).

This allows the same phone number to be used on:

*   WhatsApp Business App
    
*   BotPenguin (via Cloud API)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FC3cqMTN7DQX79OQhxT4l%252Fimg%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a24326b-ef2e-43c7-b2a9-90287ddde00d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e98c2ea0&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-by-step-verification-inside-whatsapp-business-app)

Step-by-Step: Verification Inside WhatsApp Business App

If the user selects **Use an existing WhatsApp Business App number**, the following process occurs:

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-1-enter-whatsapp-business-app-phone-number)

Step 1: Enter WhatsApp Business App Phone Number

*   The user enters their **WhatsApp Business App phone number**
    
*   Meta generates a **verification code**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZXitbG6cvXw9AB1Kcked%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0f685cb-9872-48a2-b5f7-1e6a8544d7d1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=273f6b01&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-2-receive-verification-message-in-whatsapp-business-app)

Step 2: Receive Verification Message in WhatsApp Business App

The business will receive a message from the **official Facebook Business Account** inside the WhatsApp Business App.

The message instructs the business to:

*   Copy the verification code or scan the QR
    
*   Follow the on-screen connection steps
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLlYbxK3dtKqTeIvVjvVW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbee960a4-41a8-43c7-8d07-3bb708ef293f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee5cfaeb&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-3-tap-connect-in-whatsapp-business-app)

Step 3: Tap “Connect” in WhatsApp Business App

Inside the WhatsApp Business App:

1.  Tap **Connect**
    
2.  Tap **Connect to the Business Platform** to continue onboarding
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FvPY0v83J9HmjG1m3mKpg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb95658e-fe9d-4217-b48e-99042602979b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f55e74d1&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-4-confirm-chat-history-sharing-optional)

Step 4: Confirm Chat History Sharing (Optional)

*   Tap **Confirm** when prompted
    
*   This allows the business to **share chat history and contacts** with the platform (BotPenguin)
    
*   Permission is optional but recommended for a smoother transition
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FeicJ6aJ01GLFEbbwrxSv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D563dd181-e766-46bf-8e82-4abbc8309462&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3996a82&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-5-paste-the-verification-code)

Step 5: Paste the Verification Code

*   Paste the verification code received earlier or scan the QR
    
*   This confirms ownership of the WhatsApp Business App number
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FLlYbxK3dtKqTeIvVjvVW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbee960a4-41a8-43c7-8d07-3bb708ef293f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee5cfaeb&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-6-you-are-now-connected-to-the-botpenguin)

Step 6: You are now Connected to the BotPenguin

**Business Platform Connection (WhatsApp)**

This screen shows that your WhatsApp Business app is currently connected to the **BotPenguin Business Platform**.

*   You can be connected to **only one Business Platform at a time**.
    
*   If you disconnect from BotPenguin, you will lose access to BotPenguin features, but **your WhatsApp Business app will remain unaffected**.
    
*   To keep the connection active, make sure to **open your WhatsApp Business app at least once every 14 days**.
    
*   If setup is incomplete, tap **“Finish setting up on BotPenguin”** to complete the integration.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQuEXUICXYP6sKfMrICIq%252FWhatsApp%2520Image%25202026-01-06%2520at%252011.32.12%2520AM.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D643db084-d560-4b5a-aeed-a7595038ff7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e9ec1bc6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-7-confirm-or-edit-your-whatsapp-business-account)

**Step 7: Confirm or Edit Your WhatsApp Business Account**

Your WhatsApp Business account has been successfully linked to your business portfolio. By proceeding, you agree to share your WhatsApp Business account and business profile details with BotPenguin. Please review and, if required, update your **WhatsApp Business account name** and **time zone** before continuing.

circle-info

Please ensure that all the fields are filled for smooth onboarding .

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FsxOKj3oQRe5Ozu2Ndso3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9a6a878-2cf6-4325-bc73-17b7d8f5fa0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=97f2d0af&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-8-review-and-confirm-access-permissions)

**Step 8: Review and Confirm Access Permissions**

On this screen, review the permissions that **BotPenguin v2** is requesting for your WhatsApp Business account. BotPenguin will be able to manage your WhatsApp accounts, access and manage conversations, handle product catalogues, and log events on behalf of your WhatsApp Business account. Carefully verify the details, then click **Confirm** to grant access and complete the connection, or click **Back** if you want to make changes.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3HtkslyjtPUnjSmcxP4R%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5cce480-392f-4fba-8a78-66fd350c9aee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c36dc24&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-9-you-are-now-connected-to-the-botpenguin)

Step 9 : You are now connected to the BotPenguin

This screen confirms that your WhatsApp Business account has been successfully connected to **BotPenguin**. Meta will review your business to ensure it complies with WhatsApp’s Commerce Policy and will notify you within **24 hours** if any action is required. You can manage or opt out of event activity sharing at any time from **Business Settings**. Click **Add Payment Method** to enable marketing or drip campaigns, then select **Finish** to complete the setup.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FW5gSGPFbphpdUXCymILG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf8db3b5-d739-4fb9-b688-b9a816931236&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=111647&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#step-10-whatsapp-account-approved-and-bot-created)

**Step 10: WhatsApp Account Approved & Bot Created**

This screen confirms that your WhatsApp number has been approved and your bot has been created successfully. You can now start using your bot by sending your first message, editing your chat flow, or viewing the bot overview. Make sure your payment method is added to begin your marketing or drip campaigns and fully activate your WhatsApp bot.

[whatsappWhatsapp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPvK37HX1RPt0rTpEXP5E%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7076f378-d0b8-4924-b852-0aa7b12bb9cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c50933c3&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#limitations)

Limitations

*   Phone numbers used in **both WhatsApp Business App and Cloud API** have a **fixed throughput of 20 messages per second (20 MPS)**
    
*   If the business previously worked with another partner and still shares the same **credit line**, they may see an error when switching partners → Follow Meta’s **credit line migration guide** to resolve this
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#feature-comparison-whatsapp-business-app-vs-botpenguin-cloud-api)

Feature Comparison: WhatsApp Business App vs BotPenguin (Cloud API)

WhatsApp Business App Feature

Behavior After Co-existence

Supported on BotPenguin (Cloud API)

**Individual (1:1) Chats**

Message edit/revoke disabled Messages mirrored between app & BotPenguin Last 6 months chat sync

✅ Supported

**Contacts**

No change Contacts synced

✅ Supported

**Group Chats**

No change

❌ Not Supported

**Disappearing Messages**

Automatically turned off

❌ Not Supported

**View Once Messages**

Disabled

❌ Not Supported

**Live Location**

Disabled

❌ Not Supported

**Broadcast Lists**

Disabled Existing lists read-only

❌ Not Supported

**Voice & Video Calls**

No change

❌ Not Supported

**Business Tools (Catalog, Orders, Status)**

No change

❌ Not Supported

**Messaging Tools (Greeting, Away, Quick Replies, Labels)**

No change

❌ Not Supported

**Business Profile**

No change

❌ Not Supported

**Channels**

No change

❌ Not Supported

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#important-notes)

Important Notes

*   Co-existence is ideal for businesses needing **both automation and manual control**
    
*   Some WhatsApp features are disabled intentionally to maintain API compatibility
    
*   BotPenguin handles automation, templates, analytics, and integrations
    
*   The WhatsApp Business App remains fully usable for manual chats
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#when-to-contact-support)

When to Contact Support

Contact **BotPenguin Support** if:

*   Verification fails repeatedly
    
*   You see partner credit line errors
    
*   Messages are not syncing
    
*   Templates fail after onboarding
    

Provide:

*   Business Manager ID
    
*   WhatsApp Business Account ID
    
*   Phone Number ID
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightWill my WhatsApp Business App stop working after enabling Co-existence?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#will-my-whatsapp-business-app-stop-working-after-enabling-co-existence)

No. Your **WhatsApp Business App remains fully active**. You can continue manual conversations while BotPenguin handles automated chats in parallel.

chevron-rightDo I need to migrate my WhatsApp number to use Co-existence?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#do-i-need-to-migrate-my-whatsapp-number-to-use-co-existence)

No. Unlike traditional WhatsApp API onboarding, **number migration is not required**. Co-existence works without downtime or number removal.

chevron-rightCan I send and receive messages from both the app and BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#can-i-send-and-receive-messages-from-both-the-app-and-botpenguin)

Yes. You can:

*   Reply manually from the WhatsApp Business App
    
*   Send and receive automated messages via BotPenguin Both manual and automated conversations work together.
    

chevron-rightAre chats synced between WhatsApp Business App and BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#are-chats-synced-between-whatsapp-business-app-and-botpenguin)

Yes, chats can sync across both platforms. During setup, Meta may ask for **chat history sharing permission**—this is optional but recommended for smoother synchronization.

chevron-rightCan I use WhatsApp templates with Co-existence?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#can-i-use-whatsapp-templates-with-co-existence)

Yes. You can send **approved WhatsApp template messages** via BotPenguin while continuing manual chats from the WhatsApp Business App.

chevron-rightIs WhatsApp Co-existence suitable for testing automation?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#is-whatsapp-co-existence-suitable-for-testing-automation)

Absolutely. Co-existence is ideal for businesses that want to **test automation before scaling**, without impacting their existing WhatsApp workflows.

chevron-rightWill any WhatsApp features be disabled?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/whatsapp-co-existence-feature#will-any-whatsapp-features-be-disabled)

Yes, some WhatsApp Business App features may be intentionally limited to ensure **Cloud API compatibility**, while automation, templates, analytics, and integrations are managed by BotPenguin.

[PreviousGetting a Blue Tick (previously Green Tick) on WhatsAppchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/bot-setup/getting-a-blue-tick-previously-green-tick-on-whatsapp)
[NextManage Chatflowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow)

# Other Sources | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#interactive-guide)

**Interactive Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#what-is-training-via-other-sources)

What is Training via Other Sources?

**Training your AI chatbot via external sources** allows you to provide additional knowledge beyond uploaded files or FAQs.

*   **Notion:** Connect your Notion workspace to enable the chatbot to retrieve content from pages, databases, or documentation.
    
*   **Dropbox:** Connect your Dropbox account to provide your bot access to stored files like PDFs, documents, and spreadsheets.
    

This integration ensures that your chatbot can reference multiple content repositories for accurate, context-aware answers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#benefits-of-using-other-sources)

Benefits of Using Other Sources

*   🎯 **Expanded Knowledge Base:** Utilize content from Notion and Dropbox for richer chatbot responses.
    
*   🟢 **Centralized Content Management:** Keep your information in familiar platforms while enabling the chatbot to access it.
    
*   ⚡ **Dynamic Updates:** Any changes in connected Notion pages or Dropbox files can automatically update your bot’s knowledge.
    
*   🔧 **Seamless Integration:** No coding required—simply connect accounts and start training.
    
*   📈 **Enhanced User Engagement:** Provides precise answers and reduces unanswered queries.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#how-to-train-your-ai-chatbot)

**How to train your AI Chatbot?**

1.  To manage all your chatbots, you first need to visit the BotPenguin Dashboard: [https://app.botpenguin.com/homearrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)
    
2.  To manage your bot, select it from the left sidebar.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMJ11YxblCjSiqTu11pGx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c9e63e5-b0a8-4c4b-bf52-9bd5c6628e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=539ea4ea&sv=2)

1.  Click on **Bot Training** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmG7i0trwy9WwAezFjI1f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf238ba9-e91b-4e7c-b904-ca888067aceb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbbcea1a&sv=2)

1.  Click on **"Other sources"** tab.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#other-sources)

Other Sources

1.  You can connect your Notion Page and your chatbot will retrieve information from it.
    
2.  Similarly you can connect your Google Drive and your chatbot will retrieve information from it.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F5ifsYkV0FVeVdxD5iTex%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55b81d46-e2b9-454f-a424-765d5d380ad1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c6dfda0&sv=2)

Your AI-powered chatbot is now fully equipped to handle and answer all user queries seamlessly!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#id-5.-faqs)

5\. FAQs

chevron-rightCan I connect both Notion and Dropbox at the same time?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#can-i-connect-both-notion-and-dropbox-at-the-same-time)

Yes, you can connect multiple sources, and the chatbot will reference content from all connected platforms.

chevron-rightDo changes in Notion or Dropbox update the chatbot automatically?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#do-changes-in-notion-or-dropbox-update-the-chatbot-automatically)

Yes, once synced, updates in connected pages or files will reflect in the chatbot after the next sync.

chevron-rightIs authorization required for both platforms?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#is-authorization-required-for-both-platforms)

Yes, you need to authorize BotPenguin to access your Notion and Dropbox accounts.

chevron-rightCan I select specific pages or files to train the chatbot?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#can-i-select-specific-pages-or-files-to-train-the-chatbot)

Yes, you can choose which Notion pages, databases, or Dropbox folders/files should be used for training.

chevron-rightDoes this integration require coding knowledge?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/train-your-ai-chatbot/other-sources#does-this-integration-require-coding-knowledge)

No, connecting and syncing content is completely code-free.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a3d0d6d3d3ccd1d7e3c1ccd7d3c6cdc4d6cacd8dc0ccce)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[NextWhatsapp Automationchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/whatsapp-automation)
