# BotPenguin Integrations | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/website-mobile-app-bot/3rd-party-integrations/botpenguin-integrations#botpenguin-integration-with-available-apps)

BotPenguin Integration with Available Apps

1.  Log in to the BotPenguin dashboard using the link [https://app.botpenguin.com/arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
    .
    
2.  Navigate your bot and find the `3rd Party Apps Integrations` option on the dashboard.
    
3.  Once you find the list of all integrations available, search for the desired integrations.
    
4.  Once you find your integrations in the list, click on the connect button and follow the on-screen steps.
    
5.  If you are facing issues with the integration, you can look for detailed integration tutorials.

# Google Calendar Appointment | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#what-is-the-appointment-component)

What is the Appointment Component?

The Appointment Component enables end-to-end appointment scheduling inside a chat flow. Once configured, users can select a date/time, and the system creates or updates events in the connected calendar automatically.

*   **Google Appointment** – Direct Google Calendar–based booking
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#when-to-use-it)

When to Use It

Use the Appointment Component when you want to:

*   Let users **book appointments via chat**
    
*   Sync appointments with **Google Calendar**
    
*   Allow **reschedule or cancellation** without agent involvement
    
*   Send **automatic confirmation emails**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#how-it-works-flow-overview)

How It Works (Flow Overview)

1.  Ask the user for appointment date/time
    
2.  Collect required details (email, phone, etc.)
    
3.  Configure the Appointment Component
    
4.  Create/update the event in Google Calendar
    
5.  Send confirmation to the user
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#how-to-add-the-appointment-component)

How to Add the Appointment Component

1.  Open **Bot → Select your bot and Go to Chat Flows**
    
2.  Click **Add Chat Component**
    
3.  Select **Google Appointment**
    
4.  Drag and drop it into the desired position in the flow
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdPJkbZMQadATjpUYBq8h%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D589727c8-4b59-4ee7-877b-c4b87ecf3e28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0255cc2&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-1.-create-event-flow)

1\. Create Event Flow

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#configuration-options-right-panel)

Configuration Options (Right Panel)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-1.-calendar-provider)

1\. Calendar Provider

*   Select **Google Calendar**
    
*   Required for Google Appointment component
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FXbzndco5MMJHeZvyqz1T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D462c6be9-8b80-407c-880f-81f4fd6ba5fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b890e09a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-2.-action-type)

2\. Action Type

Choose what action the bot should perform:

*   **Create Event** – Book a new appointment
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F1Idmb2i40uOnqGBd0J5f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95adf046-c9dd-47b2-91f5-b3bc3ef89b7c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fdca0ff3&sv=2)

*   **Reschedule Event** – Modify an existing booking
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fcd5UCIfeNb9DZJDBXaLZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D267fa451-6a59-4846-84bb-3e925985547c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e538e04&sv=2)

*   **Cancel Event** – Cancel an appointment
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fss1BnC76KeRSa76eXTxX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f609ad1-eb38-437a-ba48-439c3b08c7eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eb0aaa7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-3.-calendar-account)

3\. Calendar Account

*   Select the connected Google account from the dropdown if already connected
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FnNPqZFCamTj3iHaVhCaw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deff24d44-624f-4a57-b4a7-03908e8d4309&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fd4f51f&sv=2)

*   If your calendar is not connected:
    
    *   Click on Add Account Button
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FHpCPDMSTS05gNcRjO4mp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65c27601-fccd-4f73-99a9-f26571b20cd6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6aec6a1f&sv=2)

*   Choose your Google account
    
*   Review all the permissions and policies and click on continue.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFIKcoVbrD7PjwfRijU03%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44cb3254-1e24-436a-be4e-e74fa98fdadd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81d90bcd&sv=2)

*   Click on allow to give the access of your calendar.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FSBhhzApLGevoCMc0jkLB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D301ae56c-315f-4c6d-a9e2-5f587f659579&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1fbe5da0&sv=2)

*   So the account is connected and mentioned in the dropdown.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FB0zuQmg1QYIwI9QprLBC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a41113a-a2d4-4f2b-8297-38a22f6527ab&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6b5b8b0&sv=2)

*   Select your account and click on update and Next button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FE4QNKrXeIODOEW5o6EkP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96abff26-8d5a-480d-b96b-5fbdec868c23&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df26e7c9&sv=2)

*   Appointments will be created in this calendar
    
*   Make sure the account has **calendar write permissions**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#configure-your-appointment-details)

**Configure your Appointment Details:**

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-1.-basic-details-live)

1\. Basic Details (Live)

*   **Appointment Name**: Custom name for the appointment (e.g., _Google Appointment_)
    
*   **Appointment Slot Duration**: Slot length (e.g., 30 minutes)
    
*   **Per-Day Availability**: Max number of appointments allowed per day
    
*   **Availability Schedule**:
    
    *   Select existing schedule or **Add New Schedule**
        
    *   Clicking on Add new schedule will allow to configure your working hours
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FpvJwzIKgZHhkKqKKA4KK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded45f963-5d3f-4bbf-a809-58b7d0d28aea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=586b26d&sv=2)

*   Click on Add Business Hours button to add your business hours.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0xQOZ8hTRPPvv2QR9Dm7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64b13b20-fc08-4ce0-b192-4d04ffe55464&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aec42174&sv=2)

*   Add your schedule here so that your calendar can show the availability accordingly by adding the following details:
    
    *   Name
        
    *   Short Description
        
    *   Select your Time Zone
        
    *   Add your Business Hours including your days and Timings.
        
    *   After adding it will be reflected in the list.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F9gjGDJjtqk36U5gPPT64%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9937308-842e-4cdc-a4d9-8635745f1db8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d580b0e&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FiCo3jQWKusZvQTbaL7E0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7926fafe-8f35-4101-917b-1bbe91c1adde&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=309db8a8&sv=2)

> Edit and Delete the working hours accordingly.

*   Select your Added working schedule.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FSaWeCLMyJO604XjL7aJv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9d6e002-4ac4-49c7-a613-a8b6111d8652&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b48e9627&sv=2)

*   **Customer Timezone**: Timezone used for slot display (e.g., Asia/Kolkata)
    
*   **Dependency Check**:
    
    *   Name, Email, and Phone components must be added **before** this component
        
    
*   **Next Message After Completion**: Route the flow after booking completes
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F6k5a2ocfIXrMTfz5yetC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D602a14e9-fdb8-4286-aa2c-c93ed9155df5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c199b1a3&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-2.-message-text-customization-live)

2\. Message Text Customization (Live)

Fully configurable system messages:

*   **Date Selection Message** _“Please select a date for your appointment.”_
    
*   **Slot Selection Message** _“Choose an appointment slot from the available options.”_
    
*   **Booking Failed Message** _“We couldn’t complete the appointment booking. Please try again.”_
    
*   **Appointment Success Message** _“Your appointment has been booked successfully!”_
    
*   **Slot Unavailability Message** _“This appointment slot is no longer available. Please choose another one.”_
    
*   **View More Options Text** (when >10 slots) _“View More Options”_
    

➡️ Supports **dynamic variables** using `/`

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FGP0pZhMc6RRgOD4QVfuD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De60f9ef7-0332-4a8d-a49c-513138cbbf0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb4916e8&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-3.-data-mapping-live)

3\. Data Mapping (Live)

*   **Primary Attendee**
    
    *   Map appointment attendee to a **Custom Attribute** (e.g., Email)
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F947ydaG5iY3VFI3Ba7fd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D613734db-3243-4ae4-8f08-1ba7fcfc2b6c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be6a94d3&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-4.-advance-options-live)

4\. Advance Options (Live)

Select the checkboxes to enable the permissions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#booking-and-meeting-controls)

Booking & Meeting Controls

*   **Include a Google Meet link with each appointment** Automatically adds a Meet link to the booked event.
    
*   **Allow users to invite additional guests** Users can add extra attendees while booking.
    
*   **Allow multiple bookings on the same appointment slot** Enables overlapping bookings for the same time slot (useful for group sessions).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#appointment-details)

Appointment Details

*   **Allow users to add an agenda for appointment** Users can enter agenda/notes during booking.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#reliability-and-retry)

Reliability & Retry

*   **Retry booking once upon failure** Automatically retries booking if the first attempt fails.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#notifications-and-messaging)

Notifications & Messaging

*   **Send notification for the user reply** Triggers notification when user responds.
    
*   **Rephrase Messages** AI-assisted rephrasing of normal system messages.
    
*   **Rephrase Error Messages** AI-assisted rephrasing specifically for error states.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#message-timing)

Message Timing

*   **Add delay before message is displayed** Set a delay (in seconds) before sending the next message (e.g., 1 second).
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#actions)

Actions

*   **Back**: Go to previous step
    
*   **Update**: Save advanced configuration
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-5.-actions-available)

5\. Actions Available

*   **Update**: Save all configuration changes
    
*   **Back**: Navigate to previous step
    
*   **Test Live on WhatsApp Web**: End-to-end booking validation
    

Whenever an appointment is booked via the chatbot, it will automatically appear in the **Inbox → Appointments** tab. This section lets you view and manage all upcoming and past appointments in one place

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFfKex2RtvGoFPbRaWq8B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ab9417b-8992-45b4-a92d-6c6170ce6829&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe332e5f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-2.-reschedule-event)

2\. Reschedule Event

It Updates an existing appointment with a new date/time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#connect-configuration-google-appointment)

Connect Configuration (Google Appointment)

**Calendar Provider**

*   Select **Google Calendar** to sync bookings with your Google account.
    

**Action Type**

*   **New Appointment** → Creates a fresh calendar event.
    
*   **Reschedule Event** → Updates an existing appointment with a new date/time (used for rescheduling flows).
    
*   It allow the users to the reschedule the meeting
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FvTyxGvF01puEV6aWrTo3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7b38b8c-3b2e-4e85-b5bb-fe64b28e5dbd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a44e76d&sv=2)

*   Edit or keep the configure details same for the Reschedule flow.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQjYuEO26nqUhTaZMWgRz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D176f7506-d2d1-4003-9661-c3eee3ec4617&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36ea38ab&sv=2)

**Calendar Account**

*   Choose the connected Google account where appointments will be created or updated.
    
*   If no account is connected, click **Add Account** to authorize Google Calendar.
    

**Behavior**

*   On successful booking or reschedule:
    
    *   The event is created/updated in Google Calendar.
        
    *   Confirmation is sent to the user (email / chat message based on flow setup).
        
    *   Appointment details are stored internally.
        
    

**Post-Booking Visibility**

*   All booked or rescheduled appointments are reflected in:
    
    *   **Inbox → Appointments** tab
        
    *   Allows filtering by **Upcoming / Past**, date range, email, or phone number.
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-3.-cancel-event)

3\. Cancel Event

This flow Allows you to cancel the meeting Event.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-1.-entry-point)

1\. Entry Point

**Trigger**

*   Keyword: `Cancel appointment`
    
*   Button: _Cancel Appointment_
    
*   Or from menu / fallback option
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fss1BnC76KeRSa76eXTxX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f609ad1-eb38-437a-ba48-439c3b08c7eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eb0aaa7&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-2.-collect-user-identity)

2\. Collect User Identity

**Message**

> “Sure 👍 I can help you cancel your appointment. Please confirm your details to proceed.”

**Components (in this order – mandatory)**

*   **Name**
    
*   **Email**
    
*   **Phone Number**
    

> These are required to identify the correct calendar event.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-3.-fetch-existing-appointment)

3\. Fetch Existing Appointment

**Appointment Component**

*   **Calendar Provider:** Google Calendar
    
*   **Action Type:** **Cancel Event**
    
*   **Calendar Account:** Select connected Google account
    

**Configuration**

*   **Count of Previous Scheduled Events:** `1` (Fetches the most recent upcoming appointment for this user)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-4.-confirmation-step-recommended)

4\. Confirmation Step (Recommended)

**Message**

> “I found your upcoming appointment scheduled on 📅 {{date}} at ⏰ {{time}}. Do you want to cancel this appointment?”

**Single Choice**

*   ✅ Yes, cancel it
    
*   ❌ No, keep it
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-5.-cancel-event-action)

5\. Cancel Event Action

**Condition**

*   If user selects **Yes, cancel it**
    

**Appointment Component**

*   Executes **Cancel Event**
    
*   Removes the event from Google Calendar
    
*   Updates internal appointment status
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-6.-success-message)

6\. Success Message

**Message**

> “✅ Your appointment has been successfully cancelled. If you need to reschedule or book a new appointment, just let me know!”

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-7.-failure-no-appointment-found)

7\. Failure / No Appointment Found

**Fallback Message**

> “⚠️ We couldn’t find any upcoming appointment with the provided details. Please double-check your information or contact support.”

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#id-8.-post-cancellation-visibility)

8\. Post-Cancellation Visibility

*   Cancelled appointment will:
    
    *   Be removed from **Google Calendar**
        
    *   Appear as **Cancelled** in **Inbox → Appointments**
        
    *   Be available for audit/logs
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#optional-enhancements-advanced-options)

Optional Enhancements (Advanced Options)

*   ⏱ Retry cancellation once on failure
    
*   🔔 Send cancellation confirmation email
    
*   ✨ Rephrase success/error messages using AI
    
*   ➕ Offer **Reschedule** CTA immediately after cancel
    

circle-info

All the Appointments will be visible in the Inbox Tab

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F3gX0XZJb1Sfkgg1wPOTI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D718d1080-b2ad-44b9-b189-1f0cd80d2cd8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c90fba21&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightWhat is the Appointment Component?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#what-is-the-appointment-component-1)

The Appointment Component lets users book, reschedule, or cancel appointments directly inside the chatbot. It automatically creates or updates events in the connected Google Calendar.

chevron-rightDo I need to connect Google Calendar?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#do-i-need-to-connect-google-calendar)

Yes. A Google Calendar account with write access is required. All appointments booked via the chatbot will be created, updated, or cancelled in this calendar.

chevron-rightWhat actions does the Appointment Component support?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#what-actions-does-the-appointment-component-support)

The component supports three key actions:

*   **Create Event** – Book a new appointment
    
*   **Reschedule Event** – Change date or time of an existing booking
    
*   **Cancel Event** – Cancel an upcoming appointment
    

chevron-rightWhat user details are required before booking?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#what-user-details-are-required-before-booking)

Before using the Appointment Component, the flow must collect:

*   **Name**
    
*   **Email**
    
*   **Phone number** These details are required to identify and manage appointments.
    

chevron-rightWhere can I view and manage all appointments?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/manage-chatflow/google-calendar-appointment#where-can-i-view-and-manage-all-appointments)

All booked, rescheduled, and cancelled appointments are available under Inbox → Appointments tab, where you can view upcoming and past appointments.

# What to Do If WhatsApp Display Name Is Approved but Not Visible | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

If your **WhatsApp display name is approved in Meta**, but users still see only the phone number or an old name, this is usually caused by a **Meta sync or authorization error**. Follow the steps below to resolve the issue.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#why-this-issue-happens-meta-error-reasons)

Why This Issue Happens (Meta Error Reasons)

This issue can occur due to one or more of the following Meta-related reasons:

*   Delay in **Meta server sync** after display name approval
    
*   **Expired or broken Meta authorization** between the bot and WhatsApp
    
*   WhatsApp number not fully **connected or active** in WhatsApp Manager
    
*   Recent changes in **Meta Business Manager** or WhatsApp settings
    
*   **Payment or billing issues** in Meta Business Manager
    
*   **Policy or quality rating warnings** on the WhatsApp number
    
*   WhatsApp number recently **migrated, reassigned, or reconnected**
    
*   Display name approved but **profile not refreshed or published**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#step-1-reconnect-the-bot-recommended-first)

Step 1: Reconnect the Bot (Recommended First)

Most display name visibility issues are resolved by reconnecting the bot, as this refreshes Meta permissions and syncs the latest profile data.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#how-to-reconnect-the-bot)

How to Reconnect the Bot

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**
    
2.  Open the affected **Bot**
    
3.  Go to **Integrations / WhatsApp Settings**
    
4.  Click **Disconnect**
    
5.  Reconnect the bot and complete the Meta authorization flow
    
6.  Send a **new test message** from the WhatsApp number
    

👉 In most cases, the approved display name becomes visible within **a few minutes to a few hours** after reconnection.

[♻️Reconnecting Whatsapp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number/reconnecting-whatsapp-bot)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#step-2-remake-the-bot-if-reconnecting-does-not-work)

Step 2: Remake the Bot (If Reconnecting Does Not Work)

If the display name is still not visible after reconnecting and waiting up to **24–48 hours**, you should **create a new bot**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#while-remaking-the-bot-ensure-the-following)

While Remaking the Bot, Ensure the Following:

*   Use the **same WhatsApp Business Account (WABA)**
    
*   Connect the **same WhatsApp phone number** (if available)
    
*   Complete Meta authorization **without skipping any steps**
    
*   Confirm the phone number status is **Connected and Active** in WhatsApp Manager
    
*   Ensure there are **no policy or quality warnings** on the number
    
*   Verify that the **payment method is active** in Meta Business Manager
    
*   Send a **fresh outbound message** after setup
    

⚠️ Remaking the bot creates a clean Meta–Bot connection, which resolves persistent Meta sync errors.

[whatsappWhatsapp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#important-notes)

Important Notes

*   Display name changes **do not update old chats** — they appear in new conversations
    
*   Some users may see the number until WhatsApp refreshes their app cache
    
*   BotPenguin cannot directly control display name visibility
    
*   Final display name rendering is handled entirely by **Meta/WhatsApp systems**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#kv3gzu3jags5)

FAQ's

chevron-rightHow long does it take for the display name to appear?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#how-long-does-it-take-for-the-display-name-to-appear)

Usually **24–48 hours** after approval or reconnection. In rare cases, it may take up to **72 hours**.

chevron-rightWhy do some users see the name while others don’t?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#why-do-some-users-see-the-name-while-others-dont)

WhatsApp updates display names gradually and may depend on user app cache or region.

chevron-rightDoes reconnecting or remaking the bot delete chats?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#does-reconnecting-or-remaking-the-bot-delete-chats)

*   Reconnecting: ❌ No
    
*   Remaking: ⚠️ Existing chats may not carry over
    

chevron-rightCan BotPenguin force the display name to update?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#can-botpenguin-force-the-display-name-to-update)

No. Display name visibility is controlled by **Meta**.

[PreviousReconnecting Whatsapp Botchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number/reconnecting-whatsapp-bot)
[NextInstagram Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/instagram-bot)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Step 1: Reconnect the Bot (Recommended First)](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/what-to-do-if-whatsapp-display-name-is-approved-but-not-visible#step-1-reconnect-the-bot-recommended-first)

# Using Third-Party APIs with BotPenguin | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#what-are-apis-in-botpenguin)

What are API's in BotPenguin?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **API Section in BotPenguin** allows you to connect your chatbot with external services, fetch real-time data, and send dynamic information to users during a conversation. Instead of relying only on static messages, you can integrate APIs to fetch product details, check order status, or push data to your CRM directly from the chatbot flow.

This enables your chatbot to become more intelligent, versatile, and personalized, thereby improving user engagement and automating tasks seamlessly.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#benefits-of-using-apis-in-botpenguin)

Benefits of using APIs in BotPenguin


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Enable dynamic conversations** by fetching real-time data from external systems.
    
*   **Improve personalization** by mapping API responses to user attributes.
    
*   **Automate workflows** by sending and receiving data without manual intervention.
    
*   **Increase reliability** with error handling and fallback messages when APIs fail.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#setting-up-apis-in-botpenguin)

Setting up API's in BotPenguin


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Login to your [**BotPenguin Dashboard**arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
    **.**
    
2.  Go to the **Developer Section** from the sidebar.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8d6W8VSbPBnzZBr6fR3u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84867631-18e3-42c0-be18-2f9f3fa2f294&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a77a57d3&sv=2)

1.  Click on **“Create API”** to add a new API.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FNV7jcejFsXOkUNmIBYfz%252FScreenshot%25202025-09-25%2520at%252012.05.35%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82f9a428-1cd9-46d4-a45e-a804db3e4368&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b34ed51a&sv=2)

1.  To create an API, enter the following details:
    
    1.  Enter a **Name** for your API (e.g., _Products API_).
        
    2.  Paste the **API URL** you want to use.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCn19gywsqz9UIJ7Hbv10%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a1f5a37-c130-4c22-93b0-b31bcd465fc2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f34e1fc&sv=2)

1.  Click **Test** to see the API response. The response will appear in the **Response Section**.
    
2.  Save the API configuration after testing. The user can also configure the parameters, headers, body, etc.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#configure-api-details)

Configure API Details

1.  **Parameters Section**
    
    *   Add variables to your API URL.
        
    *   Map **custom attributes** to dynamically pass user inputs.
        
    
2.  **Headers Section**
    
    *   Add headers required by your API.
        
    *   You can also map attributes here for dynamic values.
        
    
3.  **Body Section**
    
    *   Add request payload in **JSON format**.
        
    *   Supports **static values** or mapped attributes.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#manage-api-responses)

Manage API Responses

1.  Once the API is tested, you can **map API responses to custom attributes**.
    
2.  Example: Map the API’s `title` field to a chatbot’s custom attribute.
    
3.  These attributes can then be reused later in the conversation flow.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#use-api-in-chatbot-flow)

Use API in Chatbot Flow

1.  Create a new flow (e.g., _Products Test_).
    
2.  Add default or custom **questions** to capture user inputs.
    
3.  Open the **Request Information Tab** and select the **API Component**.
    
4.  Choose the API you created earlier.
    
5.  Set up response handling:
    
    *   **Success (200 status code):** Redirect user to success message or next step.
        
    *   **Failure (4xx codes):** Redirect user to a fallback message.
        
    *   **Server Errors (5xx codes):** Redirect to another prompt (e.g., _How was your day?_).
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#testing-and-api-logs)

Testing & API Logs

1.  Test your API flow using **“Test Live on WhatsApp Web”**.
    
2.  Navigate to **Developer Section → Your APIs → Logs**.
    
3.  Here, you can check:
    
    *   API call history
        
    *   Response codes (200, 400, 500, etc.)
        
    *   Errors and reasons for failure
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#faqs)

FAQ's


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightCan I use multiple APIs in one chatbot flow?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#can-i-use-multiple-apis-in-one-chatbot-flow)

Yes, you can configure multiple APIs and call them at different stages in your flow.

chevron-rightWhat if my API requires authentication headers?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#what-if-my-api-requires-authentication-headers)

You can add authorization tokens or keys in the \*\*Headers section\*\* of your API setup.

chevron-rightCan I pass user inputs dynamically to the API?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#can-i-pass-user-inputs-dynamically-to-the-api)

Yes, by mapping \*\*custom attributes\*\* to API parameters, headers, or body fields.

chevron-rightWhat happens if the API fails?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#what-happens-if-the-api-fails)

BotPenguin automatically follows your \*\*fallback path\*\* (error or unknown error configuration).

chevron-rightWhere can I debug API failures?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#where-can-i-debug-api-failures)

Check the \*\*API Logs\*\* section in the Developer tab to see request and response details.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
**. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousAPI Access Tokenchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token)
[NextWebhookschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Guidance Video](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#guidance-video)
    
*   [What are API's in BotPenguin?](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#what-are-apis-in-botpenguin)
    
*   [Benefits of using APIs in BotPenguin](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin#benefits-of-using-apis-in-botpenguin)

# Settings | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/settings#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/settings#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/settings#settings-configure-and-personalize-your-bot-experience)

Settings – Configure and Personalize Your Bot Experience

The **Settings** section on BotPenguin provides a centralized control panel to manage your chatbot’s configuration, personalization, and response management capabilities. It enables users to optimize how conversations are handled, organized, and displayed within the platform—tailored to fit their operational workflows.

To access Settings, go to the sidebar, click on **More**, and select **Settings**.

Inside this section, you'll find five key configuration tools:

*   **Custom Attributes** Define and capture unique data fields from users to support advanced personalization and reporting needs.
    

[users-rectangleManaging Custom Attributechevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute)

*   **Tags** Categorize conversations in the inbox with easily searchable tags. Tags help teams segment chats by topic, department, priority, or workflow.
    

[tagManage Tagschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags)

*   **Custom Status** Create status labels such as “Open,” “Escalated,” or “In Progress” to better track the lifecycle of every conversation.
    

[chart-radarManage Custom Statuschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status)

*   **Quick Replies** Save frequently used responses and deploy them in one click to reduce reply time and maintain consistency in support.
    

[replyQuick Replieschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies)

*   **Custom Tabs** Organize and filter chats based on user-defined tabs—designed to match your business logic, teams, or funnel stages.
    

[browsersCustom Tabschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/custom-tabs)

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#1a696f6a6a75686e5a78756e6a7f747d6f737434797577)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousPricing FAQschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs)
[NextUsers & Teams Managementchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management)

# Manage Tags | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#what-are-tags-in-botpenguin)

What are Tags in BotPenguin?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Tags** section in BotPenguin allows you to create and manage custom **labels** that help you organize and categorize conversations within the **Inbox**. Tags provide a flexible way to mark and track chats based on status, priority, customer type, support category, or any custom logic that suits your business workflows.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#benefits-of-tags)

Benefits of Tags:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Better Chat Organization**: Group conversations based on relevance or context to manage your inbox more efficiently.
    
*   **Quick Filtering**: Instantly search and filter chats by tags for faster response and resolution.
    
*   **Custom Classification**: Tailor tags to match your internal workflows, such as "High Priority", "Lead", "Issue", etc.
    
*   **Bulk Actions**: Apply or delete multiple tags at once to save time on admin tasks.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#how-to-create-and-manage-tags-in-botpenguin)

How To Create and Manage Tags in BotPenguin


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log into your BotPenguin Account.
    
2.  From the left-hand sidebar, scroll down and click on “More” then Click on tag
    
3.  In the Settings interface, click on the second tab labeled **“Tags”**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQepVPUU8tDXTQWFtTp4N%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea464193-f441-4fd7-8fce-973724bed4d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae515a13&sv=2)

1.  You’ll see a table listing all your existing tags. The table includes:
    
    1.  A **Select** column to choose one or more tags
        
    2.  The **Tag Name** column showing the tag label
        
    3.  The **Actions** column, where you can click **Edit** or **Delete**
        
    4.  Edit button will open the particular tag in prepopulated form and user can edit the name of tag.
        
    
2.  Click on the **“Create Tag”** button in the top-right corner. A modal will appear where you can:
    
    1.  Enter the **Tag Name**
        
    2.  Click **“Create Tag”** to save the new tag
        
    3.  Or click **“Discard”** to cancel the action
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FC8dPiF3BkrJBduRWDBAM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5dad8cb7-cd3b-455d-8d80-3eabc25577c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5dd29476&sv=2)

1.  **Search Tags by Name:** Use the search bar at the top to quickly find a tag by typing in its name.
    
2.  **Bulk Delete Tags:** Use the checkboxes in the Select column to choose multiple tags. You can then delete all selected tags at once using the **Select All** option.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUObn5XB4Te8BYZVwZuVE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4de55a58-7cc4-4d47-b959-cf02ea6d440a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb630d86&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#faqs)

FAQ's


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightWhere can I find the Tags section in BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#where-can-i-find-the-tags-section-in-botpenguin)

Go to **More → Tags** (third tab under Settings).

chevron-rightWhat are Tags used for in BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#what-are-tags-used-for-in-botpenguin)

Tags help you label, organize, and filter chats within your **Inbox** for better visibility and task tracking.

chevron-rightCan I delete multiple tags at once?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#can-i-delete-multiple-tags-at-once)

Yes, use the checkboxes to select multiple tags and delete them in bulk using the **Select All** bar.

chevron-rightIs there a limit to how many tags I can create?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#is-there-a-limit-to-how-many-tags-i-can-create)

There’s no specified limit in the UI, but it’s recommended to keep tags manageable for better usability.

chevron-rightCan I edit an existing tag name?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#can-i-edit-an-existing-tag-name)

Yes, under the **Actions** column, click **Edit** next to the tag you want to update.

chevron-rightWill deleting a tag remove it from chats it was applied to?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags#will-deleting-a-tag-remove-it-from-chats-it-was-applied-to)

Yes, once a tag is deleted, it will no longer be associated with any past conversations.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#abd8dedbdbc4d9dfebc9c4dfdbcec5ccdec2c585c8c4c6)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[NextManage Custom Statuschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status)

# Subscription Plans | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#subscription)

Subscription

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**.
    
2.  Click on **Subscriptions** .
    
3.  You will be redirected to **Subscriptions → Plan** tab.
    
4.  Here, you will see two pricing plans:
    

*   **Omnichannel** – Includes features for all bots and agents across channels.
    
*   **WhatsApp** – A WhatsApp-only plan designed for businesses that want to automate conversations, campaigns, and support exclusively on WhatsApp, without AI features.
    

[whatsappWhatsapp Only Planschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans)

**When you select Omnichannel, you will see the available plans and their features:**

1.  **Baby Plan** – This is the default plan assigned when a user first joins the platform. It is ideal for beginners who want to explore chatbots without risk.
    
2.  **Little Plan** – Users can upgrade from the Baby Plan to the Little Plan. It is suitable for automating leads, bookings, and bulk messaging.
    
3.  **King Plan** – Designed for businesses handling higher volumes and requiring deeper integrations.
    
4.  **Emperor Plan** – Best suited for enterprises with custom requirements and very high usage.
    

You can choose the plan that best fits your needs. You also have the option to switch between **monthly** and **yearly** billing by simply toggling the plan duration.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F06AelwuXfm0LZhHrPW4J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c8c24ce-0c2f-4b71-a86a-bf3b5e41125e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1010e3d5&sv=2)

1.  At the top, you will see the "**Set Up Auto Pay"** button, which allows you to enable automatic payments so the amount can be deducted directly from your bank account.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FdyLo1JYztsjnQH6S1HVT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D641f58a7-d23e-472b-b1d9-b48f5ca2885a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b616ab4&sv=2)

1.  Click **Change Plan** to switch to your preferred plan.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F19bGotkHJQgy4BTzQYa9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b4501c7-77ce-49c0-901a-9333989d0c5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8384255&sv=2)

1.  A pop-up will appear to add your billing details if they are missing.
    
2.  Click on "**Update Billing"**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCBOXaCdHlhcUzeQ0FA3F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85ae9560-dadd-4836-94b8-38bed7d152b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea52fa58&sv=2)

1.  You will be redirected to the Billing screen.
    
2.  Add your billing address and payment method.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRKtIzycRTK9t2KutSb68%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca0625b7-f3ed-466e-b3e5-f2ddffceda2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d509830b&sv=2)

1.  After adding the details, go back to the **Plans** screen.
    
2.  Select your desired plan and click on "**Change Plan" button**.
    
3.  Click on the "**Upgrade"** button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPmATrI2BeLzzdm4tsFGc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5337d79-7a24-444e-adb2-4195ddec6954&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce9153bb&sv=2)

1.  You will be redirected to the payment gateway.
    
2.  Choose your payment method and confirm the payment.
    
3.  After successful payment, your account will be activated.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#downgrade-your-subscription)

Downgrade Your Subscription

To downgrade your plan:

1.  Select the desired plan and click **Change Plan**.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FieQ0Jl0z8naN5DXEvp1x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba918e89-5bf4-4fec-90a1-f20a6d60fde6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cc370fe&sv=2)

1.  Confirm the downgrade request.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPEuKw4zFCYJVamjMItRA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde4fd531-339f-4b03-9d45-959ee6e235b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10aa07e7&sv=2)

1.  Once confirmed, the downgrade request will be submitted and will be displayed on the Plan screen.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FZXtcsORZUskO8k8NGVmr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D430c2c68-73b5-496a-be3b-981d523c1d8d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dff5fdfe&sv=2)

**Important:**

*   Downgrades take effect at the end of the current billing cycle.
    
*   Any features that exceed the limits of the new plan will be paused.
    

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#faq)

FAQ


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-right**Will my bots stop working if I cancel?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#will-my-bots-stop-working-if-i-cancel)

Bots continue working until the end of your billing cycle.

chevron-right**Can I upgrade anytime?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#can-i-upgrade-anytime)

Yes, upgrades are applied instantly.

chevron-right**Can I get a refund?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#can-i-get-a-refund)

There is no refund policy.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/subscription-plans#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

# Whatsapp Only Plans | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#whatsapp-only-plans)

WhatsApp-Only Plans

The **WhatsApp-Only Plan** is designed for businesses that want to automate conversations, campaigns, and support exclusively on WhatsApp without using AI features.

This plan provides all core WhatsApp automation capabilities, but **does not include AI components** in the chatflow and AI agents.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#when-to-choose-a-whatsapp-only-plan)

When to Choose a WhatsApp-Only Plan

This plan is ideal if you:

*   Only want WhatsApp automation
    
*   Do not need AI responses
    
*   Want a lower-cost, focused messaging solution
    
*   Use structured chatflows instead of AI conversations
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#whats-not-included)

What’s Not Included

The following AI features are **not available** in WhatsApp-only plans:

*   AI chatflow components
    
*   AI agents
    
*   AI-generated responses
    

All conversations will work using **predefined chatflows and automation logic only**.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#how-to-access-whatsapp-only-plans)

How to Access WhatsApp-Only Plans

1.  Log in to your dashboard.
    
2.  Go to **Subscriptions** from the left menu.
    
3.  Click on the **Plan** tab.
    
4.  Select the **WhatsApp** tab at the top.
    
5.  Browse the available WhatsApp-only plans and switch the toggle to monthly or yearly to view the plans accordingly.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fp4q58QFfPqb9M3l5JGek%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D999568cf-8e9e-4474-87a2-cac758bffb36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71995590&sv=2)

1.  Click **Change Plan** to change the plan.
    
2.  Change plan will initiate the plan change request.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCBOXaCdHlhcUzeQ0FA3F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85ae9560-dadd-4836-94b8-38bed7d152b7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea52fa58&sv=2)

1.  A pop-up will appear to add your billing details if they are missing.
    
2.  Click on the **"Update Billing"** button.
    
3.  You will be redirected to the Billing screen.
    
4.  Add your billing address and payment method.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRKtIzycRTK9t2KutSb68%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca0625b7-f3ed-466e-b3e5-f2ddffceda2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d509830b&sv=2)

1.  After adding the details, go back to the "**Plans"** screen.
    
2.  Select your desired plan and click on "**Change Plan" button**.
    
3.  Click on the "**Upgrade"** button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPmATrI2BeLzzdm4tsFGc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5337d79-7a24-444e-adb2-4195ddec6954&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce9153bb&sv=2)

1.  You will be redirected to the payment gateway.
    
2.  Choose your payment method and confirm the payment.
    
3.  After successful payment, your account will be activated.
    

* * *

If you need AI-powered conversations later, you can upgrade to an **Omnichannel** from the **Subscriptions** section.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-right**What is a WhatsApp-Only plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#what-is-a-whatsapp-only-plan)

A WhatsApp-Only plan is designed for businesses that want to automate conversations, campaigns, and support only on WhatsApp, without using any AI features.

chevron-right**Does the WhatsApp-Only plan include AI features?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#does-the-whatsapp-only-plan-include-ai-features)

No. AI chatflow components, AI agents, and AI-generated responses are not included. All conversations run through predefined chatflows and automation logic.

chevron-right**Who should choose a WhatsApp-Only plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#who-should-choose-a-whatsapp-only-plan)

This plan is ideal for businesses that:

*   Only want WhatsApp automation
    
*   Do not need AI responses
    
*   Prefer a lower-cost solution
    
*   Use structured chatflows instead of AI conversations
    

chevron-right**How many WhatsApp Business numbers are required for this plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#how-many-whatsapp-business-numbers-are-required-for-this-plan)

You need **two WhatsApp numbers**:

*   **Primary number** – used for customer conversations
    
*   **Automation number** – used for campaigns and automation
    

chevron-right**What happens if my billing details are missing?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#what-happens-if-my-billing-details-are-missing)

A pop-up will appear asking you to add your billing details. You must complete this step before upgrading the plan.

chevron-right**Will my current data or bots be affected after upgrading?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#will-my-current-data-or-bots-be-affected-after-upgrading)

No, your existing data, bots, and settings remain unchanged. Only your plan limits and features are updated.

chevron-right**Can I switch between monthly and yearly billing during the upgrade?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#can-i-switch-between-monthly-and-yearly-billing-during-the-upgrade)

Yes, while upgrading you can choose either **Monthly** or **Yearly** billing based on your preference.

chevron-right**What should I do if my upgrade payment fails?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#what-should-i-do-if-my-upgrade-payment-fails)

Try the payment again using the same or a different payment method. If the issue continues, contact the support team for assistance.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/whatsapp-only-plans#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

# Managing My Account | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **My Account** section in BotPenguin is your central hub for managing both your **personal profile settings** and **account security**. From here, you can update user details, business information, and platform preferences, or securely change your login password.

The page is divided into two key sub-sections:

*   **Account Settings** – Manage your profile image, email, contact information, business details, company size, and industry.
    

[Accountchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-my-account/account)

*   **Password Settings** – Update your current password to keep your account secure.
    

[Passwordchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-my-account/password)

> Use the sidebar navigation to access either tab and make necessary updates. All changes are saved in real-time after clicking the **Submit** button.

If you still have some questions for our team, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e695939696899492a684899296838881938f88c885898b)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousNotificationschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications)
[NextAccountchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-my-account/account)

# Managing Custom Attribute | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#what-are-custom-attributes)

What are Custom Attributes?

Custom attributes are user-defined data fields that your chatbot can save and recall. In BotPenguin, a custom attribute is like a named variable or property attached to a user’s profile. For example, if you ask a user for their city in a chat flow, you can store that answer in a custom attribute called “city.” The bot will remember this information and can use it later in the conversation. Custom attributes let your chatbot capture and store specific information about each user, making it possible to personalize messages and experiences based on that data.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#benefits-of-using-custom-attributes)

Benefits of using Custom Attributes:

*   **Personalized Conversations** – Tailor interactions by recalling user details like names or interests, making them feel recognized.
    
*   **Structured Data Collection** – Easily gather and organize user info (e.g., emails, preferences) in a structured way.
    
*   **Targeted Messaging** – Filter users by attributes for relevant broadcasts (e.g., special offers based on location or interests).
    
*   **Improved Engagement** – Use stored data to suggest products or answer questions, boosting satisfaction.
    
*   **Seamless Integrations** – Sync attributes with CRMs or APIs to automate workflows and enhance functionality.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#guidance-video)

Guidance Video

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#how-to-set-up-custom-attributes)

How to Set up Custom Attributes:

Follow these steps to set up a new custom attribute in BotPenguin:

1.  Go to BotPenguin and sign in to your account. After logging in, you’ll see the main BotPenguin dashboard with navigation menus.
    
2.  On the dashboard side menu, click the **More** button (often marked with three dots or a gear icon).
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8UosAsj1tvGZXfdhhhcn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d85783d-18b2-4bdd-a507-3af174fcfc02&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bef8fa89&sv=2)

1.  In the more section, click on the 2nd tab **Custom Attributes** . This takes you to the Custom Attributes page, where all your attributes are listed. (If this is your first time, the list may be empty.) On this page you can manage existing attributes or add new ones.
    
2.  Click the **Add Attribute** (or **Add New Attribute**) button. A form will appear with fields to fill out:
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FyjmNpnQbIg1fxoFjxrky%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De97b5d12-cc1b-4316-9587-6454d94a06a0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=785f261c&sv=2)

1.  Choose one of the following options:
    
    *   **“To Save API Responses”** – Stores the responses received from the API.
        
    *   **“To Map Chatbot Responses”** – Saves the chatbot’s responses within the flow.
        
    *   **“To Save Agent Responses”** – Stores the responses provided by the agent.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FweEwjAl11xXio4cTiknv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da051005c-9ba1-41c6-8651-5f5d29cc01d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1b8a638&sv=2)

*   **Attribute Key:** Enter a short, unique key name for the attribute. Use only lowercase letters with no spaces or special characters (for example, `city` or `email`). This key is how BotPenguin stores the data internally.
    

*   **Attribute Name:** Enter a friendly display name (e.g. `City` or `Email Address`). This is what you or other team members will see in the interface.
    

*   **Attribute Type:** Select the Attribute type.
    

1.  Click on "Add Attribute" to add the attribute.
    

And that's it, now you can use this custom attribute at any place you desire!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#faqs)

FAQ's:

chevron-rightWhat are custom attributes?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#what-are-custom-attributes-1)

Custom attributes are extra pieces of information you can collect and save about each user, like their city, favorite product, or subscription plan.

chevron-rightWhy should I use custom attributes?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#why-should-i-use-custom-attributes)

They help you personalize messages, filter contacts, and automate chatbot conversations based on user preferences or data.

chevron-rightCan I dynamically update a custom attribute during a conversation?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#can-i-dynamically-update-a-custom-attribute-during-a-conversation)

Yes. You can capture and update values through chat inputs using Question Blocks or automation rules, ensuring the attribute always reflects the latest information.

chevron-rightWhat’s the difference between custom attributes and tags?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#whats-the-difference-between-custom-attributes-and-tags)

Tags categorize users into groups (like labels), while custom attributes hold specific data (like age, plan type, or company name) that can be used in logic or personalization.

chevron-rightCan I set default values for custom attributes if the user hasn't provided any?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#can-i-set-default-values-for-custom-attributes-if-the-user-hasnt-provided-any)

Yes. You can configure fallback values using the `{{customAttribute || defaultValue}}` syntax in messages or set them via automation flows.

chevron-rightIs it possible to use custom attributes for lead segmentation?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-custom-attribute#is-it-possible-to-use-custom-attributes-for-lead-segmentation)

Absolutely. You can segment users based on attribute values—like filtering users by “Plan Type = Premium” or “Location = New York”—and send targeted messages accordingly.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c8bbbdb8b8a7babc88aaa7bcb8ada6afbda1a6e6aba7a5)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousUsing Teams in Chatflowchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management/using-teams-in-chatflow)
[NextManage Tagschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags)

Last updated 19 days ago

# API Access Token | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#what-is-api-access-token)

What is API Access Token


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**API Access Token** is a secure key that allows developers to interact with BotPenguin’s platform APIs. It is used for authenticating third-party or custom applications with BotPenguin’s services. The token acts as a password for machines, enabling secure access without manual logins.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#benefits-of-using-the-api-access-token-section)

Benefits of using the API Access Token Section


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Secure access** to BotPenguin’s backend APIs without exposing your login credentials.
    
*   Enables **automation and integration** with third-party tools and systems.
    
*   Supports **scalable developer operations** and bot management via API endpoints.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#how-to-use-the-api-access-token-section)

How to use the API Access Token Section


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Navigate to “Developers”:** From the left navigation panel, click on **“More”,** then on **"Developer"**
    
2.  **Select “API Access Token”:** Go to the **second tab** under Developers labeled **“API Access Token”**.
    
3.  **Locate the Auto-Generated Token:** A unique token is generated and displayed automatically in a secure input box.
    
4.  **Copy the Token:** Click on the **“Copy”** !\[📋\] button to copy the token to your clipboard.
    
    > Example: Click **“Copy”** to securely copy the key for use.
    
5.  **Revoke and Regenerate the Token:** Click on **“Revoke API Token”** to immediately invalidate the current token and generate a new one.
    
    > Example: Click **“Revoke API Token”** to regenerate a fresh key instantly.
    
6.  **Security Tip:** Treat the token like a password. Share it **only** with trusted parties. Regenerate it if exposed.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#faqs)

FAQ's


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightWhat is the use of an API Access Token?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#what-is-the-use-of-an-api-access-token)

It enables secure access to BotPenguin APIs for third-party tools or custom scripts.

chevron-rightHow can I regenerate my token?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#how-can-i-regenerate-my-token)

Click on **“Revoke API Token”**. A new one will be auto-generated instantly.

chevron-rightCan I have multiple API tokens?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#can-i-have-multiple-api-tokens)

No. BotPenguin supports **only one active token** per user account at a time.

chevron-rightIs the API token specific to a bot or account-wide?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#is-the-api-token-specific-to-a-bot-or-account-wide)

It is tied to your **BotPenguin user account** and provides access across all your bots.

chevron-rightCan I limit the scope of this token?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#can-i-limit-the-scope-of-this-token)

Currently, scope-based restrictions are not supported.

chevron-rightWhat should I do if I accidentally exposed my token?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/api-access-token#what-should-i-do-if-i-accidentally-exposed-my-token)

Immediately click on **“Revoke API Token”** to invalidate the exposed token and generate a new one.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9eedebeeeef1eceadefcf1eaeefbf0f9ebf7f0b0fdf1f3)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousPOST Send Message APIchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api/post-send-message-api)
[NextUsing Third-Party APIs with BotPenguinchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/using-third-party-apis-with-botpenguin)
