# Webhooks | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#what-are-webhooks)

What are Webhooks?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A **webhook** is a way for one app to automatically send data to another app when something happens. Instead of checking for updates all the time, the receiving app gives a special URL, and the sending app sends information to that URL as soon as the event occurs. This helps automate tasks, keep data updated in real-time, and connect different systems without manual work.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#how-to-use-webhooks-on-botpenguin)

How to use Webhooks on BotPenguin:

1.  Log into your BotPenguin account, and then go **Developer** section under the More section.
    
2.  Click on the third tab to access the "Webhooks" section.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fz1CU8SjGkLyeC4iM6v3C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00910c62-9d05-4faf-8050-ed41023718d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f907c5e5&sv=2)

1.  Here, the user has the options to configure webhooks for 3 types, WhatsApp, Instagram and Account Level.
    
2.  Click on a card(WhatsApp, Instagram or Account Level) to configure the section.
    
3.  Click on "Subscribe Webhooks".
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FhcqNTEvVudPGqNgh0jze%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D784e709c-751e-46e9-824c-2c226ab3f18e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88cb74d&sv=2)

1.  A small popup window will open up. Enter your Webhook Endpoint, and verification key. Then, select the bots that you want the webhooks to be triggered for.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUd0028PgsEpyLD25fZzd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca8f9306-ee38-4446-84e5-1142d43c1e81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3925c8e0&sv=2)

1.  Once selected, the webhooks will be configured. Now, we can go into the specifics of each and select the ones to turn on.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#whatsapp-webhooks)

WhatsApp Webhook's

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FqolsMaySueorsNMx1YF3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2073a23-6371-4533-85a0-3b63e855639c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=961f8d09&sv=2)

1.  There are many webhooks that have been created for WhatsApp. Some of them are as follows:
    
    Failed Message
    
    Tells when a message could not be delivered
    
    Account Alerts
    
    Tells when your account does not meet our notability requirements. You can edit the display name and submit another request after 30 days.
    
    Account Review Update
    
    Tells when account review request gets approved.
    
    Account Update
    
    Update on the business verification of the WhatsApp account.
    
    Business Capability Update
    
    Updates on the max daily limits per day
    
    Business Status Update
    
    Updates the status of the business
    
    Template Quality Update
    
    Updates on the template quality.
    
    Template Status Update
    
    Tells of the approval status of the template.
    
    Messages
    
    Tells of the messages that are recieved.
    
    Phone Number Name Update
    
    Updates you when the name related to a phone number is updated
    
    Phone Number Quality Update
    
    Tells of the plan quality of a new user.
    
    Security
    
    Tells information regarding the security of the PIN's.
    
    Template Category Update
    
    Updates the template category.
    

1.  To edit any webhook, click on the "Edit Webhook Subscription" button.
    
2.  To disconnect the webhook, turn off the status of the webhook. To disconnect all the webhooks status, click on the "Unsubscribe Webhooks" button and confirm the unhook process.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#instagram-webhook)

Instagram Webhook

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fhg90KT8B8YqinOcnM7Mf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3c07d41-237e-4d0d-98a7-7b133ea4ad51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54ede8a3&sv=2)

1.  Instagram webhooks work similar in manner to WhatsApp Webhooks.
    
2.  To edit any webhook subscription, click on the "Edit Webhook Subscription" button.
    
3.  To disconnect the webhook, turn off the status of the webhook. To disconnect all the webhooks status, click on the "Unsubscribe Webhooks" button and confirm the unhook process.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fz6QDXlYgmPkHQw1tpHOd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b211bed-617e-49b9-81f1-6b33c6468e99&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=387f341&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#website-webhooks)

Website Webhooks

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwGevw7tPXeFvZDQHoAf4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37e33ec5-509a-449a-a7a1-a5b83c3dc5f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96a81b69&sv=2)

1.  To subscribe to the website webhooks, first go the website card on the developers section.
    
2.  Click on the "Subscribe Webhook" button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FVbaI24c3LWWnYoYuMuCB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3bd764b-f797-488c-a2e2-5430ed325f3e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca1eab20&sv=2)

1.  Enter the webhook, verification token, and choose the bot for which the webhook will work.
    
2.  Once all the details are filled, click on the "Subscribe" token.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8LtvSLLzJvzEqx409atX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4048385-4442-4363-baa1-4cee6ca2782d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c1cf71f&sv=2)

1.  Once the webhook is successfully subscribed, the user will have the option to opt for the following webhooks
    

Webhook Name

Use Case

Incoming Messages

Triggered when a message is incoming on the particular bot

OutGoing Messages

Triggered when a message is outgoing from the particular bot

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#telegram-webhooks)

Telegram Webhooks

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FwGevw7tPXeFvZDQHoAf4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37e33ec5-509a-449a-a7a1-a5b83c3dc5f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96a81b69&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#account-level-webhooks)

Account Level Webhooks

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fk56GhWBAXzQA4z8eym5D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec55cef0-d932-416a-a42d-85f6b99520fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=306a06b5&sv=2)

Webhook Name

Use Case

Message limit exhausted

Notifies the customer when their available message quota has been fully utilized. Customers can customize this notification to trigger when a certain percentage of their plan has been exhausted.

Conversation limit exhausted

Alerts the customer when their WhatsApp conversation limit is reached.

Plan expired

Sends a notification when the customer's subscription plan has expired.

Account freeze

Notifies the customer when their account is temporarily frozen due to non-payment or policy violations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#faqs)

FAQ's

These are the commonly asked questions regarding Webhooks:

chevron-rightWhat are webhooks in BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#what-are-webhooks-in-botpenguin)

Webhooks are automated callbacks that notify your system in real-time when specific events occur on BotPenguin, such as message delivery failures or subscription changes.

chevron-rightWhich platforms do BotPenguin webhooks support?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#which-platforms-do-botpenguin-webhooks-support)

Webhooks are supported for WhatsApp, Instagram, and application-level events within the BotPenguin ecosystem.

chevron-rightWhat kind of events can trigger a webhook?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#what-kind-of-events-can-trigger-a-webhook)

Events include failed message delivery, auto-reply execution, message limit exhaustion, conversation usage updates, subscription expiry, and account freezes.

chevron-rightAre webhooks real-time?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#are-webhooks-real-time)

Yes. BotPenguin webhooks are designed to send event notifications immediately as they occur.

chevron-right**What format does the webhook payload use?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#what-format-does-the-webhook-payload-use)

Webhook payloads are sent in JSON format, containing structured data about the triggered event.

chevron-rightHow can I test if my webhook is working?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#how-can-i-test-if-my-webhook-is-working)

BotPenguin provides testing options within the webhook configuration section, allowing you to simulate event triggers and validate your endpoint setup.

chevron-rightWhat should I do if my webhook endpoint fails?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks#what-should-i-do-if-my-webhook-endpoint-fails)

Ensure your endpoint URL is active and accessible. BotPenguin may retry failed deliveries, but persistent failures will require you to debug and update your configuration.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#21525451514e535561434e5551444f4654484f0f424e4c)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

# Current Plan | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Current Plan** screen lets you view your active subscription details, usage, and plan limits in one place.

**Path:** Subscription → Current Plan

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#what-you-can-see-on-this-screen)

What You Can See on This Screen

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fd6fCxJqoUFR5QTpLKZSE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f15ff55-5552-44ab-9cd5-e3b4177d55d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8dfd6165&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#id-1.-current-plan-details)

1\. Current Plan Details

This section shows the key information about your active plan, including:

*   **Items** – Displays your currently active Subscription Plan.
    
*   **Started On** – Displays when the plan was activated.
    
*   **Next Due On** – The next billing or renewal date.
    
*   **Base Price** – The cost of the selected plan.
    
*   **Total Amount** – Final payable amount after taxes or add-ons.
    
*   **Status** – Active, Expired, or Pending.
    
*   **Type** – Subscription and Add-on plan.
    
*   **Limit-** Displays the limit of your account.
    
*   **Upgrade Now-** Allows you to upgrade your plan
    

You can click the **info icon** to view detailed plan limits and inclusions.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FoxfPwcNF3QlldWZjokBz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a31ce84-fcee-4cf0-a270-238fe9f738f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbf37141&sv=2)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F9CFRwcOTcfJ00zdKAXhy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a6944dc-62de-488a-b901-422e79ea732c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2d16234&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#upgrade-your-subscription)

Upgrade Your Subscription

To upgrade your plan:

1.  Click the **“Upgrade Now”** button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FH2V7afT7J7skBR5PqqIi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db76210ea-b266-40b4-9b14-4f205d0b6b2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=587e4960&sv=2)

1.  You will be redirected to the **Plans** screen where you can view all available plans.
    
2.  Compare the plans and their features.
    
3.  Select your preferred Monthly or Yearly billing option.
    
4.  Click on **“Change Plan”** button on the plan you want.
    
5.  You will then see the details of your **current plan** and the **new plan**. Review the information and click the **Upgrade** button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRXUy2hyGItd2MiN7BXws%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0db99f9-b88b-4d60-a9fd-130336b166c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af0fdd9e&sv=2)

1.  Complete the payment using any of the available payment methods.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#id-2.-usage-summary)

2\. Usage Summary

This section shows how much of your plan resources you have used.

Each item displays:

*   **Used amount**
    
*   **Total limit**
    
*   **Progress bar** for quick visual tracking
    

Metric

Description

**Messages**

Total number of messages sent and received across all supported channels (website, WhatsApp, Facebook, etc.) within the billing or reporting period.

**WhatsApp Messages**

Total number of messages exchanged specifically on the WhatsApp channel, including both incoming user messages and outgoing bot or agent messages.

**Voice Minutes**

Total duration of voice calls where the user initiates a live call and interacts directly with a human agent. The minutes are calculated based on the total call duration between the user and the agent.

**AI Voice Minutes**

Total minutes of voice conversations specifically handled by the AI voice agent, excluding human agent calls.

**WhatsApp Bots**

Number of active bots deployed on the WhatsApp channel under the account.

**Website Bots**

Number of bots installed and running on website chat widgets.

**Facebook Bots**

Number of bots connected to Facebook Messenger pages.

**Telegram Bots**

Number of bots integrated with Telegram accounts or channels.

**Instagram Bots**

Number of bots connected to Instagram messaging.

**Team Members**

Total number of users or agents added to the platform with access to the account. This may include admins, agents, and other roles.

**Integrations**

Number of active third-party or channel integrations connected to the account (e.g., WhatsApp, CRM, calendar, payment systems).

**Total Bots**

Overall count of all bots created across all channels within the account.

**AI Messages**

Total number of messages generated or handled by the AI agent, including responses created using AI across channels.

**Whitelabel Bot License**

License that allows removal of the “Powered by BotPenguin” branding from the bot interface, enabling partners or customers to use the platform under their own branding.

Once payment is successful:

*   The new plan is activated immediately
    
*   Limits and features are updated in real time
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-right**Where can I view my current subscription details?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#where-can-i-view-my-current-subscription-details)

Go to **Subscription → Current Plan** to see your active plan, usage summary, limits, and billing details.

chevron-right**What information is shown in the Usage Summary?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#what-information-is-shown-in-the-usage-summary)

The Usage Summary displays how much of your plan resources you have used, such as messages, bots, integrations, AI usage, team members, and more. It also shows the total limits and a progress bar for each item.

chevron-right**How can I check the limits of my current plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#how-can-i-check-the-limits-of-my-current-plan)

Click the **info icon** next to the plan details to view the limits and features included in your plan.

chevron-right**How do I upgrade my plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#how-do-i-upgrade-my-plan)

*   Go to **Subscription → Current Plan**.
    
*   Click **Upgrade Now**.
    
*   Select a new plan.
    
*   Choose **Monthly** or **Yearly** billing.
    
*   Click **Change Plan**.
    
*   Click **Initiate Payment** and complete the payment.
    

chevron-right**What happens after I upgrade my plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#what-happens-after-i-upgrade-my-plan)

Once the payment is successful, the new plan is activated immediately. Your limits and features are updated in real time.

chevron-right**Will my current data or bots be affected after upgrading?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#will-my-current-data-or-bots-be-affected-after-upgrading)

No, your existing data, bots, and settings remain unchanged. Only your plan limits and features are updated.

chevron-right**Can I switch between monthly and yearly billing during the upgrade?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#can-i-switch-between-monthly-and-yearly-billing-during-the-upgrade)

Yes, while upgrading you can choose either **Monthly** or **Yearly** billing based on your preference.

chevron-right**What should I do if my upgrade payment fails?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#what-should-i-do-if-my-upgrade-payment-fails)

Try the payment again using the same or a different payment method. If the issue continues, contact the support team for assistance.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/current-plan#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#what-is-the-inbox)

What is the Inbox?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Inbox** is where you can view, manage, and respond to all the conversations your chatbot handles. It acts as a unified space for communication across different platforms connected to BotPenguin.

Whether the messages come from your website chatbot, WhatsApp, Facebook Messenger, or other integrated platforms — the Inbox keeps them all organized in one place.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#benefits-of-using-the-inbox)

Benefits of Using the Inbox:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Unified Conversation View**: All chats from your website, WhatsApp, Messenger, and other channels appear in one place, so you never have to switch tabs.
    
*   **User Details Panel**: Each chat shows important user information such as name, contact, and the channel they came from, helping you answer with context.
    
*   **Search & Filters**: Powerful tools to quickly locate past chats or narrow down conversations by channel, date, or keyword.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#video-guide)

Video Guide


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#managing-inbox)

Managing Inbox:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  To manage your chatbot, you need to first visit the **BotPenguin Dashboard:** [https://app.botpenguin.com/homearrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/home)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FX57s4X09miOPc8nEUI3o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d4106a6-2ac3-4255-9ea2-60300a8fa3ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1159e&sv=2)

1.  Click on **“Inbox”** to view all the chats.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fndwul9j9UOA5LEtMnjcL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5bf126f-6563-43e4-872f-95eda97b2a9d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24823e06&sv=2)

1.  You can view all the chats across all your chatbots here.
    
    1.  You can select any chat you want by clicking on ☑️ icon.
        
    2.  **Status:** You can assign status to any specific chat like Inprogress, Reviewed or Closed. You can also create your own status according to your requirements.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPXh2vRpJOzk4KIy0lFmx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcb742a2-65b4-4420-8d63-be75b22d90c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0deccf3&sv=2)

1.  You can assign a status by selecting it from the dropdown menu.
    
2.  You can mark the status of any chat as **“Closed”** by either selecting it from dropdown menu or clicking on the marked button.
    
3.  **Create Status:** Click on Create status to start creating new status.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2MFIdxuZ8TRQ9b6cqAW9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1f70775-b46f-4c81-afb0-8f95b01f643b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9d21e2f&sv=2)

1.  Here you can see all your status you have created. Click on **“Create Status”.**
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fpn8W2kSkVR07lHh35oBL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57a9d4a8-1160-4ca8-8001-db62934177f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87fbca40&sv=2)

1.  Enter Status Name and select the status color code Then click on **“Create Status”.**
    
2.  **Assign:** You can assign any chat to any of your agents. Assigned agent will have the entire access for this chat.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FeZi84I6ru4sAVyP1Kqpq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9169ce36-e092-412b-a831-6f648044d6c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b1068c7&sv=2)

1.  You can assign a status by selecting it from the dropdown menu or by clicking the marked button.
    
2.  Create Agent: Click on Create Agent to start creating new agent
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRhQJcvmYPMYP0bqPgT3b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52b530f7-eeb7-4628-9973-c8e87fd3d7db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8eed49b&sv=2)

1.  Click on **“Add Team Member”** to start adding new team member.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FRYhAjOxNF4dshgGDon7b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D569ce1fd-2afc-42c8-8d66-10bbddcefe82&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a4e0492&sv=2)

1.  Enter all the details of your team member.
    
    1.  **Select Lead Visibility:** Select whether you want to give access to all chats or only to assigned chats.
        
    2.  Select Lead Reassign Permission:
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#tags)

Tags:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJG3WRL1OptGUAQ5vOY0U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fc0d602-1569-4844-bb98-bd3c15d22ef1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb7aaa4c&sv=2)

1.  You can add tag to any chat by selecting from dropdown menu or by clicking the marked button.
    
2.  You can export the entire data by clicking on the below marked button.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FhpWVWwnsF3NP5A0xKyUc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22ff90dc-5184-4c49-bb32-4f9fd7be5a60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a721f03&sv=2)

1.  **Filter:** You can apply filters to view the leads according to your requirements.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fdt4esjtJSXPiduD0mXFI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4728e617-5ef0-4eac-a035-e1747e45a81d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c3b3d2c7&sv=2)

1.  Orders: Click on **“Orders”** to view all your orders.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FDBjwKRjF9BWhAlgpgUCg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13068903-16d7-455d-bbde-f4339d481c6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=23d06a0a&sv=2)

1.  You can assign **“Status”** and **“Tag”** to your orders.
    
2.  **Contacts:** You can view all your Leads/Contacts here.
    

*   **Contacts:** Contacts are the new customers who have shared their contact information during a chat with the bot.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F0zrGAqZ8LY7VpHkewatg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3a662f4-2d33-44c3-8b1f-e83597ba93f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5221f5f4&sv=2)

1.  **Groups:** You can group your leads.
    
2.  You can view all your groups you have created here.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FlVbNnnWIfeOK294MbQap%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65e0110d-d51e-4963-a8dd-26c89f4ef4bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf33082d&sv=2)

1.  **Create Group**
    
2.  Enter Group Name.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FM0AL0ksTTaOPduehPIKP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d738bca-a98e-49a1-a985-276fcb174422&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4294c09e&sv=2)

1.  Then select the filter and all the contacts that fall under this filter criteria will be added.
    
2.  You can also assign leads to any specific group.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F2oqzkhqZ0SZJ2BvGgEI7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d5a9cb6-c81b-453e-8eea-ad7a8bc3f7f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73ce0cc1&sv=2)

1.  Select the group using the dropdown menu.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some commonly asked questions regarding Inbox:

chevron-rightHow long are my chats retained?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#how-long-are-my-chats-retained)

Chat are based on your plan with BotPenguin. They can be retained from 30 days(for the Baby and Little Plan) to upto Lifetime Retainment (King, Emperor Plan)

chevron-rightCan I assign multiple statuses to a single chat?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#can-i-assign-multiple-statuses-to-a-single-chat)

No, each chat can only have one active status at a time. You can update it as the conversation progresses.

chevron-rightIs it possible to automate assigning statuses based on user actions?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#is-it-possible-to-automate-assigning-statuses-based-on-user-actions)

Currently, status assignment is manual. Automation may require integration with custom workflows or external tools.

chevron-rightWhat’s the difference between “Reviewed” and “Closed” status?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#whats-the-difference-between-reviewed-and-closed-status)

"Reviewed" means the chat has been looked into but may require follow-up. "Closed" means the conversation is considered complete.

chevron-rightHow many custom statuses can I create?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#how-many-custom-statuses-can-i-create)

There's no hard limit, but for clarity and performance, it's best to keep your list concise and meaningful.

chevron-rightCan chats be reassigned from one agent to another?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#can-chats-be-reassigned-from-one-agent-to-another)

Yes, agents with lead reassign permission can reallocate chats to different team members.

chevron-rightWhat happens if no agent is assigned to a chat?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#what-happens-if-no-agent-is-assigned-to-a-chat)

Unassigned chats remain visible in the inbox but may be missed without proper filters or notifications set up.

chevron-rightCan I export chats with filters applied (e.g., only "Closed" chats)?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#can-i-export-chats-with-filters-applied-e.g.-only-closed-chats)

Yes, use the filter to view specific chats, then click the export button to download filtered data.

chevron-rightWhat are tags used for, and can they be customized?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#what-are-tags-used-for-and-can-they-be-customized)

Tags are used to categorize chats by topic, urgency, department, etc. You can customize and apply them as needed.

chevron-rightWhat’s the difference between Contacts and Leads?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#whats-the-difference-between-contacts-and-leads)

In BotPenguin, **Contacts** are users who’ve provided their information, whereas **Leads** may refer more broadly to potential customers in your funnel.

chevron-rightWhat is the purpose of creating groups under Contacts?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats#what-is-the-purpose-of-creating-groups-under-contacts)

Groups help you segment leads for targeted communication or follow-ups. You can assign leads based on filters like location, behavior, or tag.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c7b4b2b7b7a8b5b387a5a8b3b7a2a9a0b2aea9e9a4a8aa)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousHow To Transfer A Chat To Another Agentchevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/ai-agents/creating-ai-agents-in-botpenguin/how-to-transfer-a-chat-to-another-agent)
[NextChats windowchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/inbox-chats/inbox-chats/chats-window)

Last updated 3 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Notifications | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#overview)

📌 Overview

The **Notifications** section in BotPenguin helps you stay informed about important activities such as new chat requests, user messages, live chat requests, and new lead creation. You can view all notifications in one place and customize how and when you receive them.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#notifications-dashboard)

🔔 Notifications Dashboard

The **Notifications** tab displays a complete list of alerts generated by your bots and users.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#what-youll-see)

What You’ll See

Each notification includes:

*   **Type** – Nature of the notification (e.g., New Chat Request)
    
*   **Message** – Details about the activity
    
*   **Action Status** – Accepted or Rejected (for actionable notifications)
    
*   **Timestamp** – Date and time when the event occurred
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#supported-notification-types)

Supported Notification Types

*   New Chat Request
    
*   User Messages
    
*   Live Chat Requests
    
*   New Lead Creation
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJ9cxdOAkoTqVo8eC4e7Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D015f9c5d-02ea-48e9-b346-0a2bebcf52e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d54eb9d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#chat-request-actions)

🟢 Chat Request Actions

For **New Chat Requests**, you can take immediate action:

*   **Accept** – Start the conversation with the user
    
*   **Reject** – Decline the chat request
    

Once an action is taken, the status is clearly shown as **Accepted** or **Rejected**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#notification-settings)

⚙️ Notification Settings

The **Notification Settings** tab allows you to customize which notifications you want to receive and how you receive them.

Navigate to: **More** **→ Notifications → Notification Settings**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#customize-notifications)

🛠 Customize Notifications

You can configure notifications separately for different events.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#id-1.-user-message-notifications)

1\. User Message Notifications

Receive alerts whenever a user sends a message.

**Available Settings**

*   Receive notifications for:
    
    *   All Users
        
    *   Assigned users
        
    
*   **Desktop Notifications** – Enable/disable browser alerts
    
*   **Mobile Push Notifications** – Enable/disable mobile alerts
    

Click **Update** to save changes.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQzfwW05wzBybkwfcjh5x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d24aae9-1841-4011-ba52-7be53a4c7dcb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e21f0188&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#id-2.-live-chat-request-notifications)

2\. Live Chat Request Notifications

Get notified whenever a user requests a live chat with an agent.

**Available Settings**

*   Desktop Notifications toggle
    
*   Mobile Push Notifications toggle
    

This ensures you never miss a live chat opportunity.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FIoDFrZpSdza5Kxms7txI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ae00804-f471-4997-8e7d-382ce6604f3f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6c9f5fa&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#id-3.-new-lead-notifications)

3\. New Lead Notifications

Receive alerts when a new lead is created via bot interactions.

**Available Settings**

*   Desktop Notifications toggle
    
*   Mobile Push Notifications toggle
    

Ideal for sales and marketing teams to act quickly on new leads.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FI8fcarIRfItRasZuTgoL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9af74dd5-51b3-4cc5-9540-0897e4ccc345&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4650a74&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#saving-or-discarding-changes)

💾 Saving or Discarding Changes

*   **Update** – Saves your notification preferences
    
*   **Discard** – Reverts changes to the last saved state
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#notification-delivery-channels)

🔔 Notification Delivery Channels

BotPenguin supports:

*   **Desktop Notifications** (browser-based)
    
*   **Mobile Push Notifications**
    

You can enable either or both based on your preference.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/notifications#best-practices)

🧪 Best Practices

*   Enable **Live Chat Request notifications** for faster response times
    
*   Turn on **New Lead notifications** for sales follow-ups
    
*   Use desktop notifications during work hours
    
*   Use mobile push notifications for on-the-go alerts

[NextManaging My Accountchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/managing-my-account)

# Changing a Whatsapp bots number | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

Changing your WhatsApp bot number requires disconnecting the existing number and integrating a new one. WhatsApp does not allow replacing a number directly on an active integration.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#before-you-begin-important)

Before You Begin (Important)

*   You must have **access to the new WhatsApp number**.
    
*   The new number **must not be already connected** to another WhatsApp Business API account.
    
*   Ensure you have the **OTP access** for the new number.
    
*   Existing chats and history **will not transfer** to the new number.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#steps-to-release-delete-a-whatsapp-bot-number)

Steps to Release (Delete) a WhatsApp Bot Number

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#step-1-remove-the-number-from-meta-facebook-business)

Step 1: Remove the Number from Meta (Facebook Business)

1.  Go to **business.facebook.com** and log in
    
2.  Select the **Business Portfolio** where the WhatsApp bot was created
    
3.  Click on **Business Settings**
    
4.  From the left sidebar, select **WhatsApp Accounts**
    
5.  Choose the WhatsApp account linked to your bot
    
6.  Scroll down and click **WhatsApp Manager**
    
7.  Open the **Phone Numbers** section
    
8.  Locate the number you want to release
    
9.  Click **Delete**
    
10.  If prompted, select a reason and **confirm deletion**
    

[❎Deleting a WhatsApp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number/deleting-a-whatsapp-bot)

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPV8kDqwm1Gicjwh7EhXt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd65608f3-3de2-4227-bf63-12801ec0e7b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=180de6ba&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#step-2-delete-the-whatsapp-bot-in-botpenguin)

Step 2: Delete the WhatsApp Bot in BotPenguin

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**
    
2.  Go to Bots
    
3.  Open the WhatsApp bot associated with the deleted number
    
4.  Delete or disconnect the WhatsApp bot
    

Once this is done, the number is fully released from BotPenguin.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F4Ey42rRqf9izmDl2yQ4I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd887eab5-a81b-4964-9f74-c3344d705818&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=843f54f0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#step-3-create-a-new-whatsapp-bot-with-the-new-number)

Step 3: Create a New WhatsApp Bot with the New Number

1.  Go to **Bots**
    
2.  Click **Create Whatsapp Bot**
    
3.  Select **WhatsApp** as the channel
    
4.  Enter and verify the **new WhatsApp number** (OTP required)
    
5.  Complete the onboarding steps.
    

A **new WhatsApp bot** is now created with the new number.

View Reconnecting Whatsapp Bot here:

[♻️Reconnecting Whatsapp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number/reconnecting-whatsapp-bot)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#faqs)

FAQs

chevron-rightCan I directly edit my WhatsApp bot number?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#can-i-directly-edit-my-whatsapp-bot-number)

No. WhatsApp numbers cannot be changed once a bot is created.

chevron-rightWhy is a new bot required?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#why-is-a-new-bot-required)

Meta does not allow phone numbers to be reassigned within an active WhatsApp Business API setup.

chevron-rightWill my old chats be available?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#will-my-old-chats-be-available)

No. WhatsApp does not support chat history migration between numbers.

chevron-rightCan I reuse the number on any WhatsApp account?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#can-i-reuse-the-number-on-any-whatsapp-account)

Yes, once the number is released from Meta, it can be reused on a new bot or WhatsApp account.

chevron-rightIs there any downtime?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#is-there-any-downtime)

Yes. The bot will be unavailable until the new number is verified and the new bot is live.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#196a6c6969766b6d597b766d697c777e6c7077377a7674)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousIntegrate BotPenguin with Worldpaychevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/3rd-party-apps-integrations/botpenguin-integrations/integrate-botpenguin-with-worldpay)
[NextDeleting a WhatsApp Botchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number/deleting-a-whatsapp-bot)

Last updated 16 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Before You Begin (Important)](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#before-you-begin-important)
    
*   [Steps to Release (Delete) a WhatsApp Bot Number](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#steps-to-release-delete-a-whatsapp-bot-number)
    
*   [FAQs](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/whatsapp-bot/changing-a-whatsapp-bots-number#faqs)
    

Was this helpful?

# Recovering Your Restricted Meta Account | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#recovering-your-restricted-meta-account)

🔏Recovering Your Restricted Meta Account


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page gives an in depth guide on how to recover your restricted Meta Business Account

Meta Business Accounts, now called Business Portfolios, are essential for managing ad campaigns, Facebook Pages, and Business Manager operations. However, due to policy violations, security triggers, or suspicious activity, your Meta account (or one of its assets) may get restricted or disabled. This document guides you through identifying, appealing, and recovering access where possible.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#why-meta-account-restrictions-happen)

Why Meta Account Restrictions Happen:

1.  Policy Violations: Breaching Meta’s Advertising, Community, or Commerce Policies.
    
2.  Suspicious Activity: Irregular login attempts, IP changes, or bot-like behavior.
    
3.  Unverified Business Information: Missing or incomplete domain and business verification.
    
4.  Negative User Feedback: Poor ad relevance scores, repeated reports, or engagement bait.
    
5.  Linked Account Penalties: Associations with previously banned or restricted accounts.
    
6.  Fraudulent Payment Methods: Use of flagged or inconsistent billing information.
    
7.  Repeated Offenses: Multiple prior warnings or restrictions ignored.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#how-to-resolve-restriction)

How To Resolve Restriction:

1.  Login to [https://business.facebook.comarrow-up-right](https://business.facebook.com/)
    .
    
2.  Navigate to **All Tools**(represented as 3 horizontal lines) **> Business Support Home**.
    

To check for a particular Page, account, click on the name/icon of the account and switch between them.

1.  A page having the details of all activities related to Ad accounts, pages and WhatsApp accounts of that particular Business Portfolio will open.
    
2.  Click on "**Account Overview**", sole icon of the left sidebar, to see all the related accounts.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fu6p3a2Wn7TQ9Xut4wdh4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73eead29-f1e4-461d-96bb-1cf9eaeb3367&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39516da&sv=2)

1.  The status of all the accounts will be shown. Click on the "**View Account**" to see the detailed summary of the issues.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FISdnlyNTXLsQgFnJO5jA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D701de569-d839-4ae0-8077-dd2987ea78af&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3251d70&sv=2)

1.  Upon click the same, a detailed screen will open explaining the restrictions of the account.
    
2.  Click on the "**Request Review**".
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FOBydjpl1sVgSAVrRw5uR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1860b545-2a6f-40d9-af96-13073c1e77cf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=30596add&sv=2)

8\. Fill up the Request Review form, post which it will take Meta some time to process and respond to the review.

Some accounts may violate the policies of Meta to such an extent that review of the same might not be possible. In such cases, an example as shown below may appear.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F8gtPqU12twdTRHZPOVUF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4c92c3d-df59-46a8-a505-6c281fd78e4e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5d3d56d&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#faqs)

FAQ's:

Here are some frequently asked questions regrading getting disabled/restricted accounts from Meta.

chevron-rightHow long does Meta take to respond to a review request?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#how-long-does-meta-take-to-respond-to-a-review-request)

Meta usually responds within **24–72 hours**, though in some cases, especially if additional documentation is needed, it may take longer.

chevron-rightI don't see the review request button. what should I do ?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#i-dont-see-the-review-request-button.-what-should-i-do)

If the “Request Review” option is missing, it typically means:

*   The account is **not eligible for review**.
    
*   The issue has already been reviewed and closed.
    
*   The restriction is **permanent** due to severe policy violations.
    

In such cases, refer to the “If Review Option is Not Available” section of this guide for alternatives.

chevron-rightCan I appeal using different admin account?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#can-i-appeal-using-different-admin-account)

Yes, if you have **multiple verified admins**, another admin may attempt to raise the request or contact support. Ensure the admin has **sufficient access level** in the Business Portfolio.

chevron-rightWhat happens if my entire Business Portfolio is restricted?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#what-happens-if-my-entire-business-portfolio-is-restricted)

If your full Portfolio is restricted:

*   All linked assets (Ad Accounts, Pages, WhatsApp Numbers) will be affected.
    
*   You’ll need to identify if the restriction is on the Portfolio or individual assets.
    
*   If eligible, raise a review for the Portfolio itself under **Account Overview**.
    

chevron-rightWhat should I include in the Request review form ?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#what-should-i-include-in-the-request-review-form)

*   A **clear, concise justification** explaining that the restriction may be in error.
    
*   Evidence of compliance with Meta’s policies (e.g., verified domain, legitimate ad usage).
    
*   Mention any **corrective steps** you've already taken.
    

chevron-rightWill deleting and recreating my account solve the issue ?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#will-deleting-and-recreating-my-account-solve-the-issue)

No. Meta tracks behavior at multiple levels—**user, business, device, IP, and payment profile**. Simply creating a new account without resolving the root issue often results in further restrictions.

chevron-rightCan I prevent restrictions in the future ?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#can-i-prevent-restrictions-in-the-future)

Yes. Follow all the **Best Practices** outlined in this guide—especially:

*   Business verification
    
*   2FA security
    
*   Clean payment history
    
*   Clear policy-compliant ad content
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/recovering-your-restricted-meta-account#got-any-questions)

Got Any Questions?

If you can having any questions, you can look into our repository of FAQs. Most likely, you will find your answer here. If not, write us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#fb888e8b8b94898fbb99948f8b9e959c8e9295d5989496)
.

[PreviousWebhookschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/developers-guide/webhooks)
[NextUnlock Power of BotPenguinchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/platform-guidelines-and-trainings/unlock-power-of-botpenguin)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# WhatsApp Cloud API | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api#id-1.-create-and-sync-templates)

1\. Create and Sync Templates


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The team will be required to create and get the templates approved by the Facebook WhatsApp Business Manager or BotPenguin Dashboard. Once It is done,

1.  Go to BotPenguin Panel
    
2.  Navigate to WhatsApp Automation and Then go to the manage section.
    
3.  Under templates, You will be required to sync templates from Facebook, Once Done, App should use the get Templates API and save the template details. These details will be required to send Notifications.
    

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api#id-2.-api-key)

2\. API Key


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to generate the WhatsApp API key,

1.  Go to the BotPenguin Dashboard ( [https://app.botpenguin.com/arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
     )
    
2.  Find your bot and go to `WhatsApp Bot Settings` section.
    
3.  Under `WhatsApp Bot Settings`, Navigate to the API key and Click on generate an API key.
    
4.  You will require to update the webhook URL, on which we will send the delivery reports.
    
5.  Once done, Copy the key and save it yourself.
    

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api#id-3.-apis-endpoints)

3\. APIs Endpoints


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[message-textGET Templates Listchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api/get-templates-list)
[whatsappPOST WhatsApp Template Messagechevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api/post-whatsapp-template-message)
[comment-penPOST Send Message APIchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api/post-send-message-api)

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api#error-codes)

Error Codes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please refer to the link below for more info on the error codes

[https://developers.facebook.com/docs/whatsapp/on-premises/errorsarrow-up-right](https://developers.facebook.com/docs/whatsapp/on-premises/errors)

[PreviousWebsite Contacts & Meta Datachevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis/website-contacts-and-meta-data)
[NextGET Templates Listchevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/whatsapp-cloud-api/get-templates-list)

# Manage Custom Status | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#what-are-custom-status)

What are Custom Status


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Custom Status** section in BotPenguin allows you to define and manage your own chat statuses for better tracking and workflow alignment within the **Inbox**. These statuses serve as labels to help your team identify the state of a conversation—such as "Pending Response", "Escalated", "Resolved"—and more, all based on your operational needs.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#benefits-of-custom-status)

Benefits of Custom Status


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Workflow Clarity**: Clearly define stages in a customer conversation lifecycle such as “Follow-Up Needed” or “Waiting for User”.
    
*   **Color Coding**: Assign a unique color to each status for immediate visual identification inside the Inbox.
    
*   **Custom Typing**: Select the type of status—e.g., Open, Closed, or Pending—to fit your resolution flow.
    
*   **Inbox Optimization**: Quickly filter and manage chats based on their assigned custom status.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#steps-to-set-up-custom-status)

Steps to set up Custom Status


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log into your BotPenguin account by visiting **app.botpenguin.com**
    
2.  From the left-hand sidebar, scroll to the bottom and click on **“More”.**
    
3.  Click on the fourth tab **– “Custom Status”** under the more section.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FPEM1ybumFRQxLKzyaSnm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbce6e68-4855-4df0-b0e6-4d116bf0322e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=652e687a&sv=2)

1.  You will see a table listing all existing statuses, including their **Name, Type, Color**, and **Action buttons** like **Edit** or **Delete**.
    
2.  Use the **search bar** to quickly find a custom status by typing its name.
    
3.  To delete statuses, select one or multiple rows using the checkboxes. You can also use **“Select All”** to bulk delete.
    
4.  To create a new custom status, click on the **“Create Status”** button in the top-right corner.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F61v5WjpacdNot5h4zw3j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a753362-6959-4cbb-a992-3f472c7beee2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88ba0ea3&sv=2)

1.  In the modal that appears, fill in the following:
    
    1.  Enter the **Status Name**
        
    2.  Select a **Color** to visually represent the status
        
    
2.  Once complete, click **“Create Status”** to save or **“Discard”** to cancel.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#faq)

FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightWhere can I access the Custom Status section in BotPenguin?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#where-can-i-access-the-custom-status-section-in-botpenguin)

Go to **More → Custom Status**

chevron-rightWhat are custom statuses used for?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#what-are-custom-statuses-used-for)

They help categorize conversations in your Inbox based on your business-specific workflow stages.

chevron-rightCan I assign colors to statuses?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#can-i-assign-colors-to-statuses)

Yes, you can choose a color while creating each status for easy visual tracking.

chevron-rightWhat are the available status types?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#what-are-the-available-status-types)

You can choose types like **Open**, **Closed**, or **Pending**, depending on how you want to classify the chat.

chevron-rightCan I delete multiple statuses at once?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#can-i-delete-multiple-statuses-at-once)

Yes, use the Select checkboxes or **Select All** bar to delete multiple statuses in bulk.

chevron-rightCan I edit an existing custom status?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#can-i-edit-an-existing-custom-status)

Yes, click **Edit** under the **Actions** column next to the status you want to update.

chevron-rightAre these statuses visible in the Inbox?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#are-these-statuses-visible-in-the-inbox)

Yes, these custom statuses will reflect in the Inbox, helping your team manage and filter conversations.

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2f5c5a5f5f405d5b6f4d405b5f4a41485a4641014c4042)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousManage Tagschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-tags)
[NextQuick Replieschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies)

Last updated 19 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Interactive Guide](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#interactive-guide)
    
*   [What are Custom Status](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#what-are-custom-status)
    
*   [Benefits of Custom Status](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#benefits-of-custom-status)
    
*   [Guidance Video](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#guidance-video)
    
*   [Steps to set up Custom Status](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status#steps-to-set-up-custom-status)

# 3rd Party APIs | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#apis-management)

APIs Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **APIs Management** section allows you to add, configure, test, and manage all third-party APIs that can be used inside your chatbot flows.

You can use these APIs to:

*   Send data to external systems
    
*   Fetch customer details
    
*   Trigger third-party actions
    
*   Automate workflows after bot interactions
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#how-to-access-apis-management)

How to Access APIs Management

1.  Go to **More** from the left sidebar.
    
2.  Click on **3rd Party APIs**.
    
3.  You will land on the **APIs Management** page.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FCsSSwKuTLNdVKcigQvz3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5451910-862b-4344-bc13-bae9899cd0c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcff98f1&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#overview-of-the-apis-management-page)

Overview of the APIs Management Page

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#search-bar)

🔎 Search Bar

*   Use **Search by API name** to quickly find a configured API.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#add-api)

➕ Add API

*   Click **Add API** (top right) to create a new API configuration.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#api-list-table)

📋 API List Table

The table displays all configured APIs with the following details:

Column

Description

API Name

Name given to the API

Method

Request type (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE)

URL

Configured API endpoint

Actions

Edit (⚙️) or Delete (🗑️) the API

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FR9TdHMnqX1VhFYPaLgij%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9c1d7e4-fd80-4c8f-92e4-dfed25f18e58&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7008261a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#managing-an-existing-api)

Managing an Existing API

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#edit-api)

⚙️ Edit API

*   Click the **Settings (⚙️) icon** to modify:
    
    *   API URL
        
    *   Headers
        
    *   Parameters
        
    *   Body
        
    *   Response mapping
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fat1UkerS1pIw2Y8GIxCo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab7cbb95-44f3-4708-a1d8-14c8220b6c42&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d38967c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#delete-api)

🗑️ Delete API

*   Click the **Delete (🗑️) icon** will show the warning popup.
    
*   Confirming will permanently delete the API.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FX0OOD00IOL3uSE1f92ZJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ec0011e-1fd6-47ce-95a4-2a6b3373225a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24fb00e0&sv=2)

> ⚠️ Note: Deleting an API may impact any chatbot flow where it is currently used.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#setting-up-apis-in-botpenguin)

Setting up API's in BotPenguin


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Login to your [**BotPenguin Dashboard**arrow-up-right](https://app.botpenguin.com/)
    **.**
    
2.  Go to the **More** section from the sidebar.
    
3.  Click on the **3rd Party API** option.
    
4.  Click on **“Add API”** to add a new API.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYhpTFGEy0Zss0SqiChsi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e74c18d-c972-43d9-a05f-65c120189c7d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=187ecffe&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#configure-3rd-party-api)

Configure 3rd Party API

The **Configure API** section allows you to integrate external APIs with your bot to send or fetch data dynamically during conversations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#a.-basic-configuration)

a. Basic Configuration

1.  Go to **More** from the left sidebar.
    
2.  Click on **3rd Party APIs**.
    
3.  Select **Configure API**.
    

Now fill in:

*   **API Name** – Enter a unique name for the API.
    
*   **Method Type** – Choose from:
    
    *   GET
        
    *   POST
        
    *   PUT
        
    *   DELETE
        
    
*   **API URL** – Enter the complete endpoint URL.
    
*   **Description** – (Optional) Add internal notes about what this API does.
    

Click **Test** to check the API response before saving.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252F4OJsyTtQ6MDFarwtIc6V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25ea652c-d10b-4c8f-bdc8-75b5e264ed21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bffeca1b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#b.-configure-request-details)

b. Configure Request Details

1.  **Parameters Tab**
    
    1.  Add **Key–Value** pairs for query parameters.
        
    2.  Click **Add another field** to add more parameters.
        
    
2.  **Headers Tab**
    
    1.  Add required headers (e.g., Authorization, Content-Type).
        
    
3.  **Body Tab**
    
    1.  Required for POST/PUT requests.
        
    2.  Add JSON or form data based on API requirements.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#c.-manage-api-responses)

c. Manage API Responses

Use **Manage API responses** to:

*   Map response fields
    
*   Save API responses
    
*   Use values inside chatbot flows
    
*   Trigger conditional logic
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#d.-third-party-integration)

d. Third Party Integration

Configure how this API connects with:

*   Chatbot flows
    
*   AI Agents
    
*   Live Chat automation
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#e.-final-step)

e. Final Step

Click **Save** after successful testing.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#manage-api-responses)

Manage API Responses

1.  Once the API is tested, you can **map API responses to custom attributes**.
    
2.  Example: Map the API’s `title` field to a chatbot’s custom attribute.
    
3.  These attributes can then be reused later in the conversation flow.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#use-api-in-chatbot-flow)

Use API in Chatbot Flow

1.  Create a new flow (e.g., _Products Test_).
    
2.  Add default or custom **questions** to capture user inputs.
    
3.  Open the **Request Information Tab** and select the **API Component**.
    
4.  Choose the API you created earlier.
    
5.  Set up response handling:
    
    *   **Success (200 status code):** Redirect user to success message or next step.
        
    *   **Failure (4xx codes):** Redirect user to a fallback message.
        
    *   **Server Errors (5xx codes):** Redirect to another prompt (e.g., _How was your day?_).
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#testing-and-api-logs)

Testing & API Logs

1.  Test your API flow using **“Test Live on WhatsApp Web”**.
    
2.  Navigate to **More → third party APIs → select your API → API Logs → Click on view**
    
3.  Here, you can check:
    
    *   API call history
        
    *   Response codes (200, 400, 500, etc.)
        
    *   Errors and reasons for failure
        
    *   Actions - copy and delete
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fttztld3JMR5oXm5g8OuY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05744d26-c2de-4343-91a8-e91a7cbf4482&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe8a84b&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#faqs)

FAQ's


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightCan I use multiple APIs in one chatbot flow?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#can-i-use-multiple-apis-in-one-chatbot-flow)

Yes, you can configure multiple APIs and call them at different stages in your flow.

chevron-rightWhat if my API requires authentication headers?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#what-if-my-api-requires-authentication-headers)

You can add authorization tokens or keys in the \*\*Headers section\*\* of your API setup.

chevron-rightCan I pass user inputs dynamically to the API?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#can-i-pass-user-inputs-dynamically-to-the-api)

Yes, by mapping \*\*custom attributes\*\* to API parameters, headers, or body fields.

chevron-rightWhat happens if the API fails?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#what-happens-if-the-api-fails)

BotPenguin automatically follows your \*\*fallback path\*\* (error or unknown error configuration).

chevron-rightWhere can I debug API failures?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#where-can-i-debug-api-failures)

Check the \*\*API Logs\*\* section in the Developer tab to see request and response details.

* * *

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
**. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousCustom Tabschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/custom-tabs)
[NextIntegrationschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/integrations)

*   [FAQ's](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/3rd-party-apis#faqs)

# Contacts & Chats APIs | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **Contacts & Chats APIs** in BotPenguin allow developers and businesses to programmatically manage contacts, access chat conversations, and sync conversation data with external systems such as CRMs, analytics tools, or internal dashboards.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#what-are-contacts-and-chats-apis)

📌 What Are Contacts & Chats APIs?

These APIs provide secure access to:

*   Contact (visitor) details collected by bots
    
*   Chat conversations between users and bots/agents
    
*   Message history, metadata, and conversation status
    

They are commonly used for CRM integration, reporting, automation, and custom workflows.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#key-capabilities)

🔑 Key Capabilities

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#contacts-api)

Contacts API

Use the Contacts API to:

*   Fetch all contacts created by bots
    
*   Retrieve contact details (name, email, phone, channel, tags)
    
*   Sync contacts with CRMs or databases
    
*   Identify leads generated through bots
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#chats-api)

Chats API

Use the Chats API to:

*   Fetch chat conversations
    
*   Access message history (bot + user messages)
    
*   Track chat status (Open / Closed)
    
*   Identify assigned agents and bots
    
*   Analyze conversation timelines
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#common-use-cases)

🧩 Common Use Cases

*   Sync BotPenguin leads with CRM systems (HubSpot, Zoho, Salesforce)
    
*   Build custom analytics dashboards
    
*   Store chat transcripts for compliance or QA
    
*   Trigger workflows based on chat events
    
*   Monitor agent or bot performance externally
    

* * *

[PreviousCommon Meta Issueschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-meta-issues)
[NextGet All Contactschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis/get-all-contacts)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [📌 What Are Contacts & Chats APIs?](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#what-are-contacts-and-chats-apis)
    
*   [🔑 Key Capabilities](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#key-capabilities)
    
*   [🧩 Common Use Cases](https://help.botpenguin.com/api-documentation/contacts-and-chats-apis#common-use-cases)
