# Buying Add-Ons | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#what-are-add-on)

What Are Add-on?

Add-on let you extend your existing BotPenguin subscription by adding extra capacity or premium features. Add-ons do not replace your base plan—they work alongside it.

You should use add-ons when:

*   You are reaching your usage limits
    
*   Your team or traffic grows
    
*   You need advanced branding or AI capacity
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#how-to-access-add-on)

How to Access Add-on?

1.  Log in to your BotPenguin Dashboard
    
2.  Navigate to **Subscriptions**
    
3.  Click on the **Add-on** tab
    

You will see all available add-on categories on this page.

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FMFBu8PLFZsZUqQWVIiAC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da5aabb55-9c93-4cd4-bf5f-c3f5cca529d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2629d69&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-1.-message-add-on-packs)

1\. Message Add-on Packs

Message Add-on Packs increase the **total number of messages** your account can send across supported channels.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#available-packs)

Available Packs

*   Pack of **1,000 Messages**
    
*   Pack of **5,000 Messages**
    
*   Pack of **10,000 Messages**
    
*   Pack of **1,00,000 Messages**
    
*   Pack of **5,00,000 Messages**
    
*   Pack of **10,00,000 Messages**
    

Each pack shows:

*   Message count
    
*   Monthly price
    
*   **➕ Add** button to add the pack to your cart
    
*   Selected plan will be added to the cart
    
*   increase or decrease the quantity by clicking on + and -
    
*   Click on remove Add-on button to remove it.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrvSSgVxhJzwVW8TN1n3b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41054ace-b5bb-4c69-955f-e0a926272737&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7e97e85&sv=2)

*   Click on proceed to payment to enable the add on to the platfoem.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FUWp1w24EyMCfOL5M1fvK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df12b5dc9-d0a8-4510-b536-b10d5ba366f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f79887a6&sv=2)

**Use this add-on if:**

*   Your bots are handling high conversation volume, and
    
*   You want uninterrupted messaging
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-2.-whatsapp-wa-message-add-on-packs)

2\. WhatsApp (WA) Message Add-on Packs

These add-ons are dedicated to **WhatsApp messaging** and are consumed only for WhatsApp conversations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#available-packs-1)

Available Packs

*   Pack of **1,000 WA Messages**
    
*   Pack of **5,000 WA Messages**
    
*   Pack of **10,000 WA Messages**
    
*   Pack of **1,00,000 WA Messages**
    
*   Pack of **10,00,000 WA Messages**
    

Each pack displays:

*   WA message count
    
*   Monthly pricing
    
*   **➕ Add** option
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-3.-agents-add-on)

3\. Agents Add-on

Agents Add-ons allow you to add **more human agent seats** so your team can handle more live conversations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#available-agent-packs)

Available Agent Packs

*   **Additional Human Agent** – 1 Agent Seat
    
*   **Pack of 5 Human Agents** – 5 Agent Seats
    
*   **Pack of 10 Human Agents** – 10 Agent Seats
    

**Recommended when:**

*   Your support team is expanding
    
*   You need to manage multiple chats simultaneously
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-4.-ai-message-add-on-packs)

4\. AI Message Add-on Packs

AI Message Add-ons increase the number of **AI-powered responses** your bots can generate.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#available-ai-message-packs)

Available AI Message Packs

*   **1,000 AI Messages**
    
*   **5,000 AI Messages**
    
*   **10,000 AI Messages**
    
*   **100,000 AI Messages**
    
*   **1,000,000 AI Messages**
    

These are useful when:

*   You use AI Agents extensively
    
*   Your bots handle long or frequent conversations
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-5.-ai-database-add-on-packs)

5\. AI Database Add-on Packs

AI Database Add-ons increase your **AI training data storage limit**, allowing you to upload more documents and knowledge sources.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#available-storage-packs)

Available Storage Packs

*   **1 GB (1024 MB)** Database Limit
    
*   **5 GB (5120 MB)** Database Limit
    
*   **10 GB (10240 MB)** Database Limit
    
*   **50 GB (51200 MB)** Database Limit
    
*   **100 GB (102400 MB)** Database Limit
    

**Best for:**

*   Large documents
    
*   Extensive knowledge bases
    
*   Advanced AI training
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-6.-white-label-chat-window)

6\. White Label Chat Window

This add-on removes the **“Chat by BotPenguin”** branding from your chatbot widget.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#key-benefits)

Key Benefits

*   Clean, brand-first chat experience
    
*   Maintains your business identity
    

This add-on is billed monthly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#id-7.-agent-white-label-chat-window)

7\. Agent White Label Chat Window

This add-on removes BotPenguin branding from the **human agent chat interface**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#key-benefits-1)

Key Benefits

*   Fully branded agent conversations
    
*   Professional white-labeled support experience
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#adding-add-ons-to-cart)

Adding Add-ons to Cart

1.  Click the **➕ Add** button on any add-on card
    
2.  The selected add-on appears in **Your Cart** (right panel)
    
3.  Review selected add-ons before checkout
    

If no add-ons are selected, you’ll see:

> _Your Cart is empty, please add some add-ons_

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#checkout-and-billing)

Checkout & Billing

1.  Review your cart
    
2.  Proceed to payment
    
3.  Complete checkout using available payment methods
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#billing-notes)

Billing Notes

*   Add-ons are billed **monthly**
    
*   They renew with your main subscription
    
*   Pricing may vary based on add-on type
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#important-notes)

Important Notes

*   Add-ons do **not** change your base plan
    
*   Multiple add-ons can be purchased together
    
*   Unused limits may not roll over (as per policy)
    
*   Removing add-ons usually applies from the next billing cycle
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-right**Can I buy multiple add-ons?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#can-i-buy-multiple-add-ons)

Yes, you can purchase multiple add-ons based on your needs.

chevron-right**Q. Are WhatsApp add-ons separate from normal messages?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#q.-are-whatsapp-add-ons-separate-from-normal-messages)

Yes, WA message add-ons are consumed only for WhatsApp conversations.

chevron-right**Q. When do add-ons become active?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#q.-when-do-add-ons-become-active)

Add-ons are activated immediately after successful payment.

* * *

✅ _Tip:_ Monitor your usage regularly to choose the right add-on combination and avoid service interruptions.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/buying-add-ons#need-help)

Need Help?

If you face any issues managing your subscription, contact **[\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** from the dashboard or reach out via the official support channels.

# Meta Ads | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#overview)

Overview

Meta Ads integration allows you to connect your Facebook and Instagram ads with BotPenguin, enabling automated WhatsApp conversations from ad clicks. This helps you instantly engage leads, qualify them, and drive conversions using chatbots.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#what-is-meta-a-ds)

What Is Meta Ads?

Meta Ads are advertisements run on:

*   **Facebook**
    
*   **Instagram**
    
*   **Messenger**
    

When integrated with BotPenguin, users clicking your ads can be redirected to **WhatsApp**, where a bot automatically starts the conversation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#use-cases)

Use Cases

Use Meta Ads integration if you want to:

*   Capture leads directly on WhatsApp
    
*   Auto-reply to ad-generated inquiries
    
*   Qualify leads using chatbots
    
*   Reduce manual follow-ups
    
*   Increase ad conversion rates
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before setting up Meta Ads, ensure:

*   ✔ Active Facebook account
    
*   ✔ Facebook Business Manager access (Admin recommended)
    
*   ✔ Active Meta Ads account
    
*   ✔ WhatsApp Business number connected to BotPenguin
    
*   ✔ Approved WhatsApp templates (recommended)
    
*   ✔ Payment method added to Meta Ads account
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#how-meta-a-ds-work-with-botpenguin)

How Meta Ads Work with BotPenguin

1.  User clicks a Facebook or Instagram ad
    
2.  The ad redirects the user to WhatsApp
    
3.  BotPenguin automatically triggers a chatbot flow
    
4.  Bot qualifies the lead or shares information
    
5.  Conversation continues via automation or manual agent
    

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#step-by-step-setup)

Step-by-Step Setup

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#step-1-create-a-whatsapp-chatbot)

Step 1: Create a WhatsApp Chatbot

*   Log in to **BotPenguin**
    
*   Create or select a WhatsApp bot
    
*   Ensure the bot is active
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#step-2-connect-meta-a-ds-account)

Step 2: Connect Meta Ads Account

*   Go to **Integrations** → **Meta Ads**
    
*   Click **Connect**
    
*   Log in to your Facebook account
    
*   Grant required permissions
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#step-3-create-click-to-whatsapp-a-d)

Step 3: Create Click-to-WhatsApp Ad

*   Open **Meta Ads Manager**
    
*   Create a new campaign
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FBz13isSMWS05pxTBXKj5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18418ce6-ce77-4aa7-adba-11432785adcd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5d642ad&sv=2)

*   Click on Create Ad
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FmSa8Dpo4RnKA7hZ8r7bR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29606a5c-bdf5-4874-b1b6-40957ecfd378&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9df58878&sv=2)

*   Choose the **Buying Type** and select the **Campaign Objective** (Recommended: _Engagement_ or _Messages_)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FpfYchT8GKQsvI7sfiiY4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84a905ba-cff4-45ac-8dd6-00ec38d92f03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8141fe5&sv=2)

*   Select the **Campaign Setup** (Manual or Advantage+)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FjMB5A0fXn3pJRwctLlHN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De316900b-10b2-4cf4-ae15-e1023d159ea8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdbdf8b0&sv=2)

*   Choose your **Budget Strategy** (Daily or Lifetime)
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fv2YjlxEdStvK2dyH30Ks%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77260602-50f1-4ce0-8c13-fd0d0b24909e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e851ae5a&sv=2)

*   Choose where you want to drive the Engagement
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FrsMgTBjUwbypBBiXzIqj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffe5d843-82a6-4b9d-b7f2-42b3213aa05f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b928e175&sv=2)

*   Under **Engagement destination**, select **Messaging Apps**
    
*   Choose Destination
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252Fuq83B3PPY3sEaJtjcgT5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3359e3f-61ab-4993-bfa9-f6297464806a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9893e2ba&sv=2)

*   Review the settings and publish Ad.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FFx444WaSAIV7YMeQ5loi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c71e32b-3c35-4083-8ee3-7ec0873718e5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed8efdfa&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#meta-click-to-whatsapp-a-ds-with-botpenguin)

Meta Click-to-WhatsApp Ads with BotPenguin

Meta Click-to-WhatsApp Ads allow you to run ads on Facebook or Instagram that open a WhatsApp chat when users click them. When your WhatsApp number is connected to **BotPenguin**, all incoming ad leads are automatically captured in the BotPenguin Inbox with ad-level tracking.

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#step-1-view-a-d-leads-in-botpenguin-inbox)

Step 1: View Ad Leads in BotPenguin Inbox

1.  Log in to your **BotPenguin Dashboard**
    
2.  Go to **Inbox**
    
3.  All WhatsApp conversations generated from ads will appear automatically
    
4.  Go to Filters
    
5.  Select the Whatsapp Click to Ads option
    
6.  Toggle on the Acquired using Ads.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FsUMThdrBsvyPvSuid3Gg%252FWeb%25201920%2520%25E2%2580%2593%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78e71357-9b32-4be2-ad07-edcbe1949e8e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6230e37&sv=2)

1.  Filter the Chats by Ads.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FQHiYkN7d9DlzffTFeaFp%252FWeb%25201920%2520%25E2%2580%2593%25204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ad11835-6588-4233-a87e-cbbc9f467274&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e48e849&sv=2)

1.  After Filtering Chats are visible according to Ad.
    
2.  At the Right side bottom Details can be viewed by expanding the whatsapp click to ad Details.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FEapoBPDbSfxNF5eWuod1%252FWeb%25201920%2520%25E2%2580%2593%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D692bfd16-36ef-4d6c-b147-44527875acfa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ccb30413&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#key-benefits)

Key Benefits

*   Automatic capture of Meta ad leads
    
*   Clear tracking of Click-to-WhatsApp campaigns
    
*   Easy filtering and lead segmentation
    
*   Faster response using bots + live agents
    
*   Centralized inbox for all WhatsApp conversations
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads#notes-and-best-practices)

Notes & Best Practices

*   Always test your ad before scaling
    
*   Use clear CTA text to improve click rates
    
*   Keep bot flows ready for instant engagement
    
*   Tag ad leads for better reporting

# Quick Replies | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#interactive-guide)

Interactive Guide


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#what-are-quick-replies)

What are Quick Replies?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quick Replies are pre-built responses that can be saved and used during live chat interactions. They enhance efficiency by allowing users or live chat agents to quickly access and send commonly used phrases, images, or documents as responses to the customer. By entering '/' into the live chat input window(in the inbox), the system automatically fetches the list of saved Quick Replies, and enables users to select and send the appropriate response effortlessly.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#benefits-of-quick-replies)

Benefits of Quick Replies


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Efficiency**: Reduces response time of users and enhances customer satisfaction.
    
*   **Consistency**: Ensures uniform responses across customer interactions.
    
*   **Ease of Use**: Quick access via the '/' shortcut streamlines workflow.
    
*   **Productivity Boost**: Enables support agents to handle multiple conversations effectively.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#guidance-video)

Guidance Video


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#how-to-set-up-quick-replies)

How to set up Quick Replies


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Login to the Botpenguin
    
2.  Go to More section from the main menu then select the Quick replies tab.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FpHlEYR2YgzXiquTv7JjN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd7fddcd-0f38-49b6-b283-b27753e9fb29&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=251deb0d&sv=2)

1.  View all the pre-build replies in the column given, or we can create a new quick reply by clicking on the “**Add Quick Reply**” button.
    

circle-info

We can edit the name, message or attachment of any old quick reply simply by clicking on the edit button, or delete the reply using the delete icon in the row of the reply.

1.  Click on the “**Add Quick Reply**” button to start addition of custom quick replies
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FeHK29Svn0ClmUkVtY6On%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb85a2f2-b90d-4eaa-829b-b60622476519&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3860f53&sv=2)

1.  Add the required details:
    
    1.  Title: The name of the quick reply. This will be the name that is used to identify this particular quick reply during the chat.
        
    2.  Add Description: Text of the quick reply sent to the user.
        
    3.  Choose Your File(Optional): Add any JPG, PNG, PDF or JPEG file to be sent alongside the description.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYQaUOx0c4P7Bnz4Fwhft%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d2290c0-d8e9-45b0-bf40-4b367444d02b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b39ee5bb&sv=2)

1.  Save the quick reply by clicking on the “**Add New**” button.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#using-quick-replies)

Using Quick Replies


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to the inbox of the chat where you wish to use the quick reply.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FlmeBGMEjzCVByZQugbLT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D100e7fa6-dfd4-4204-94d0-c6ec581ca988&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56d3bfcd&sv=2)

1.  Enter the “/” character in the text box, this will open up a list of all quick replies.
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FJLSq2hklzOmEEeUWO8ZM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe767f33-9ace-4d8c-9f6c-df060a50c0a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d549da9e&sv=2)

1.  Select the desired quick reply by either:
    
    1.  Scrolling down to the desired reply, or
        
    2.  Continuing to enter the title of the quick reply after the “/” in the text box.
        
    

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FcX2keIdezR9g2jTKrefN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c5edcd0-83fb-4038-bb96-6ef3f46cd074&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=353663e8&sv=2)

1.  Send the desired quick reply.
    

circle-info

If the quick reply contains any file, a separate window confirming the reply will open up. Click on Send to confirm the same.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#faqs)

FAQ's


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some frequently asked questions regarding Quick Replies:

chevron-rightWhere can I find the Quick Replies configuration settings?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#where-can-i-find-the-quick-replies-configuration-settings)

Quick Replies can be accessed via the **“Settings” tab**, under the section labeled **“Quick Replies.”** This is the central hub for managing, editing, and adding new Quick Replies.

chevron-rightCan Quick Replies be categorized for different departments or use cases?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#can-quick-replies-be-categorized-for-different-departments-or-use-cases)

**No**, at present, the platform does not support grouping or categorizing Quick Replies by department or function. However, naming conventions can be used strategically to simulate categorization.

chevron-rightWhat file types are supported in Quick Replies?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#what-file-types-are-supported-in-quick-replies)

You can attach **JPG, JPEG, PNG, and PDF** files to Quick Replies. Ensure files meet these criteria to avoid upload errors.

chevron-rightIs there a maximum number of Quick Replies that can be created?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#is-there-a-maximum-number-of-quick-replies-that-can-be-created)

There is **no hard limit** currently in place. The system is optimized to manage a large number of Quick Replies efficiently.

chevron-rightCan I duplicate or reuse an existing Quick Reply?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#can-i-duplicate-or-reuse-an-existing-quick-reply)

**Yes**, while there is no direct “duplicate” feature, you can manually copy the content of an existing reply and create a new one using the **“Add Quick Reply”** option.

chevron-rightHow do I trigger Quick Replies during a live chat session?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#how-do-i-trigger-quick-replies-during-a-live-chat-session)

Simply enter **“/”** into the live chat input window to bring up the full list of available Quick Replies.

chevron-rightCan I search Quick Replies using the content of the message?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#can-i-search-quick-replies-using-the-content-of-the-message)

**No**, currently only the **title** of the Quick Reply is searchable. It’s advisable to use clear, descriptive titles for easier recall.

chevron-rightHow do I confirm a Quick Reply that includes an attachment?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#how-do-i-confirm-a-quick-reply-that-includes-an-attachment)

If a Quick Reply contains a file, a **confirmation window** will pop up before sending. Review and click **Send** to proceed.

chevron-rightCan I edit a Quick Reply after it has been saved?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#can-i-edit-a-quick-reply-after-it-has-been-saved)

**Yes**, simply click the **edit icon** in the reply’s row to modify the title, message, or attached file.

chevron-rightWhat happens if a frequently used Quick Reply is deleted?[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#what-happens-if-a-frequently-used-quick-reply-is-deleted)

Deleted Quick Replies are **not recoverable** and will no longer be accessible via the “/” command. You will need to **recreate the Quick Reply manually** if needed again.

* * *

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/quick-replies#having-trouble-lets-troubleshoot)

Having Trouble? Let's Troubleshoot


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you’re encountering issues while working with **quick replies**, check the below:

1.  **Reply not loading**: Make sure the “Add New” was clicked while saving the reply.
    
2.  **File not being uploaded**: Make sure the format of the file is either JPG, PNG, PDF or JPEG
    

If everything is correct and you are still unable to move forward, write to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#87f4f2f7f7e8f5f3c7e5e8f3f7e2e9e0f2eee9a9e4e8ea)
. We will respond back within 48 business hours.

[PreviousManage Custom Statuschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/manage-custom-status)
[NextCustom Tabschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/custom-tabs)

Last updated 19 days ago

# Users & Teams Management | BotPenguin Documentation

Interactive Guide

Teams Section


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BotPenguin allows you to onboard your team members, enabling better collaboration and management of your chatbots and enhancing the overall experience for your end-users.

In this documentation, we’ll guide you through:

*   **How to Add More Team Members**
    
*   **What Are Roles and How to Create New Roles**
    
*   **How to Assign Leads to Your Team Members**
    

The **Teams** section allows you to add other team members to your platform and manage their roles, departments, and working hours. This section is divided into four main parts:

![](https://help.botpenguin.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1745791824-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAPDb8cKQtGlIAfgHjcsQ%252Fuploads%252FYxQVt8VlDQVe6SPoCw0x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db90c8b20-47bd-4a0a-b347-b04951313250&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28f2fd0&sv=2)

[Creating and Managing Teamschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management/creating-and-managing-teams)
[Setting Business Hourschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management/setting-business-hours)
[Adding Team Memberschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management/adding-team-members)
[Creating and Managing Roleschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/users-and-teams-management/creating-and-managing-roles)

[PreviousSettingschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/settings)

# Common Errors & Troubleshooting | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

chevron-right**The Password field is not accepting my password**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#the-password-field-is-not-accepting-my-password)

Whenever you are setting up a password, make sure you use:

*   At least 8 characters —the more characters, the better
    
*   At least one uppercase letter
    
*   At least one numeric character
    
*   At least one special character, e.g.,! @ # ? \]
    

Failing to follow these guidelines may result in the issue you are facing.

chevron-right**The Email field is not accepting my email**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#the-email-field-is-not-accepting-my-email)

It may occur due to the following reasons:

1.  You already have an account on BotPenguin
    
2.  The email address you entered is invalid or has been blocked by BotPenguin
    

chevron-right**My WhatsApp API key is not working**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#my-whatsapp-api-key-is-not-working)

It is happening probably because of the below reasons:

1.  The key you are using may not be correct or have some error. Verify your key with your provider
    
2.  Your key is already in use.
    

chevron-right**My Telegram bot token is not working**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#my-telegram-bot-token-is-not-working)

It is happening probably because of the below reasons:

1.  The token you are using may not be correct or have some error.
    
2.  Your token is already in use.
    

chevron-right**I am unable to connect To my Facebook page**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-unable-to-connect-to-my-facebook-page)

It is happening probably because of the below reasons:

1.  You have not allowed all the permissions required for your Facebook page. Please note that you must be an admin of the Facebook page to initiate integration.
    
2.  You have already connected another application or bot to your Facebook page.
    
3.  Your Facebook business page or account is disabled temporarily or permanently.
    

chevron-right**I have installed the script on my website; however, a bot is not appearing**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-have-installed-the-script-on-my-website-however-a-bot-is-not-appearing)

Your bot may not appear due to the following reasons

1.  You have exceeded your message limit on your plan
    
2.  You have disabled your bot in the country, IP, region, the website you want to access BotPenguin.
    
3.  There might be some typo in the script that you used to install the chat widget.
    
4.  You have not installed the script in the right location, i.e., is the head tag.
    

chevron-right**I have connected the bot to my CRM. However, it is not sending leads**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-have-connected-the-bot-to-my-crm.-however-it-is-not-sending-leads)

It may occur due to the following reasons:

1.  Authentication credentials such as Auth Token or API key entered incorrectly or have expired, So try reconnecting the CRM.
    
2.  Make sure that your CRM account is working fine.
    
3.  Make sure all the parameters fields are mapped correctly
    
4.  Make sure you have a paid subscription to BotPenguin, and that You have not exhausted your message limit.
    

chevron-right**I am unable to connect to my CRM**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-unable-to-connect-to-my-crm)

It may occur due to the following reasons:

1.  Authentication credentials such as Auth Token or API key are entered incorrectly or have expired, So try reconnecting the CRM.
    
2.  Make sure that your CRM account is working fine.
    
3.  Make sure all parameter fields are mapped correctly.
    

chevron-right**I created the test lead. However, I cannot see it in my leads panel**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-created-the-test-lead.-however-i-cannot-see-it-in-my-leads-panel)

It may occur due to the following reasons:

1.  Your lead can be delayed for 15 min in some cases.
    
2.  Your visitor does not qualify for the leads.
    

chevron-right**I am not receiving new lead notifications**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-not-receiving-new-lead-notifications)

It may occur due to the following reasons:

1.  Your lead can be delayed for 15 min in some cases.
    
2.  Your visitor does not qualify for the leads.
    
3.  You will not receive a notification until you have closed the chat session by clicking on the X button if you haven't enabled the 'Send incomplete response' option.
    
4.  This feature is only available under the paid plan, So make sure you are not on a free plan.
    

chevron-right**My analytics seems to be wrong. It shows old data**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#my-analytics-seems-to-be-wrong.-it-shows-old-data)

Your Analytics will update at 24-hour intervals, So every time you see the analytics, it shows data since the previous day's end.

Please Note:

Currently, Analytics does not count any messages from Facebook, WhatsApp, or Telegram bot.

chevron-right**I am unable to add anything after three team members**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-unable-to-add-anything-after-three-team-members)

In the paid plan for BotPenguin, There is a limit of 3 team members. Suppose you want to add more than three members. You can contact us to set up more than three team members at an additional cost.

chevron-right**I am unable to apply the white label add-on**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-unable-to-apply-the-white-label-add-on)

This feature is only available to users with a King plan subscription and above. Hence, you must upgrade your subscription first to avail white label add-on.

chevron-right**I am unable to use the messages add-on**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-am-unable-to-use-the-messages-add-on)

This feature is only available to users with a King plan subscription and above. Hence, you must upgrade your subscription first to avail yourself of message add-ons.

chevron-right**My payment link has expired**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#my-payment-link-has-expired)

Due to security reasons, a payment link is only available for a specific period.

1.  If your payment link has expired, you must retry payment again by creating a new one from the payment gateway.
    
2.  If your money is deducted and the transaction has failed, it usually returns in three business days. If not, please contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#493a3c3939263b3d092b263d392c272e3c2027672a2624)
     .
    

chevron-right**I have made changes to my configuration. However, it is not reflected in the bot**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/common-errors-and-troubleshooting#i-have-made-changes-to-my-configuration.-however-it-is-not-reflected-in-the-bot)

All the changes of Bot Configuration get reflected after 15 mins. If you can't see the changes, Go to Bot Settings -> General and Click the `Invalidate cache` button.

[PreviousChatGPT FAQschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/faqs/chatgpt-faqs)
[NextMeta Adschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/faqs/meta-ads)

Last updated 18 days ago

# Pricing FAQs | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#general-pricing)

General Pricing


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-right**What plans does BotPenguin offer?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-plans-does-botpenguin-offer)

BotPenguin offers multiple subscription plans designed for different business needs. Each plan includes a fixed set of features, usage limits, and supported channels.

chevron-right**Can I start with a free plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#can-i-start-with-a-free-plan)

Yes. You can start with a free plan and upgrade anytime as your business grows.

chevron-right**Is pricing monthly or yearly?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#is-pricing-monthly-or-yearly)

Both exists. You can choose according to your feasibility.

chevron-right**Can I use BotPenguin for free?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#can-i-use-botpenguin-for-free)

Yes, BotPenguin’s baby plan is free forever. We don't hold you back in any way.

chevron-right**Do you have a trial account?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#do-you-have-a-trial-account)

Yes, trial plan is now available on the little and King Plans. With a 7 day trial period, check out all the offerings of BotPenguin! Additionally, use the baby plan as a FREE Plan forever!

chevron-right**How many chat agents can I include in the King plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#how-many-chat-agents-can-i-include-in-the-king-plan)

You can include 10 agents with the King plan. You can add more agents at additional charges using Add-ons.

chevron-right**What channels does the King plan include?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-channels-does-the-king-plan-include)

BotPenguin's King Plan allows you to create chatbots for Websites, Facebook, Instagram, Telegram, WhatsApp, and SMS.

chevron-right**What happens when I cross the response limit?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-happens-when-i-cross-the-response-limit)

Once the limit of your messages has been reached, you will get a warning on your dashboard and additional messages and conversations will not be initiated via your chatbot. You will be requested to upgrade your current plan, your bots will not be able to bring leads and talk to your customers until you upgrade.

chevron-right**How many Chatbots can be created in King Plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#how-many-chatbots-can-be-created-in-king-plan)

A total of 50 chatbots can be created on the King plan

chevron-right**What is your refund policy?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-is-your-refund-policy)

Get in touch with our friendly customer success manager who is handling your account, and they will make the process easy. Contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 for any refund related queries.

chevron-right**Is there any free plan of BotPenguin?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#is-there-any-free-plan-of-botpenguin)

Yes, the free plan includes one Bot and sends up to 1000 messages and 100 conversations per billing cycle. Create any one bot using the BotPenguin Baby Plan!

chevron-right**Does BotPenguin offer any discount?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#does-botpenguin-offer-any-discount)

BotPenguin gives you 5 times productivity and tenth of the price of its competitors. All the prices are set to make the decision of going with BotPenguin a no-brainer. We can make it an even sweeter deal, if you choose the yearly plan. You need to pay for 10 months, if you choose the yearly plan, two months on us. Also, we do provide a 100% discount to Nonprofit organizations.

chevron-right**Is there any discount on the yearly plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#is-there-any-discount-on-the-yearly-plan)

You get **two months free** if you opt for a yearly plan.

chevron-right**Can I cancel my subscription?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#can-i-cancel-my-subscription)

It is a decision smart people won't take, but we respect your choices, you can cancel your subscription in settings.

chevron-right**What if I cancel my plan?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-if-i-cancel-my-plan)

You can cancel your plan whenever you want. However, we will cancel your subscription only at the end of the billing cycle. Once you cancel your plan, you will not receive a new invoice from the next billing cycle. Hence, If you cancel your plan in January, you will not get a new bill in February.

chevron-right**What if I upgrade my plan in between?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-if-i-upgrade-my-plan-in-between)

If you upgrade your plan in between a billing cycle, we will deduct the price on your current plan from the new pricing, and you will only have to pay the rest. For example:- Suppose you upgrade to 7K monthly messages at 800 INR, and your current plan costs 400 INR. Then, you will have to pay 400 INR and 18% service tax (only if you reside in India) for upgradation.

chevron-right**What is the pricing for the Messages add-ons?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-is-the-pricing-for-the-messages-add-ons)

Messages Add-ons pricing depend on the quantity of messages purchased. The pricing for the same can be checked in the "Add-ons" section of the subscription panel.

chevron-right**What is the pricing for white labeling a chat window?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-is-the-pricing-for-white-labeling-a-chat-window)

You can check the pricing on the BotPengion Subscription panel.

chevron-right**How can I get my invoice?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#how-can-i-get-my-invoice)

Log in to Your BotPenguin Account

1.  Navigate to the `Subscriptions` in the side navigation panel and then move to the `Invoice` Tab
    
2.  Click on Invoices, Here you can get a list of all your invoice. You can also send them to your email.
    

chevron-right**Does BotPenguin store payment details?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#does-botpenguin-store-payment-details)

No, BotPenguin uses a secure payment gateway and does not store payment details. Your privacy and security are paramount to us.

chevron-right**What if my payment fails and my money gets deducted?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#what-if-my-payment-fails-and-my-money-gets-deducted)

If your payment is not completed successfully and money has already been deducted from your account. You can contact support (at [\[email protected\].envelope](https://help.botpenguin.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a7d4d2d7d7c8d5d3e7c5c8d3d7c2c9c0d2cec989c4c8ca)
) and your bank for further information. Usually, your bank refunds the deducted amount within three working days.

chevron-right**How do I make the payment?**[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/pricing-faqs#how-do-i-make-the-payment)

You can choose to pay via Stripe or Razor Pay, both are secure, encrypted gateways. Security is our topmost priority

[PreviousManaging Billing & Invoiceschevron-left](https://help.botpenguin.com/subscription/managing-billing-and-invoices)
[NextSettingschevron-right](https://help.botpenguin.com/settings/settings)

# MS Teams Bot | BotPenguin Documentation

[circle-info\
\
Tell us how we can improve docs for you.\
\
BotPenguin updatesarrow-up-right](https://updates.botpenguin.com/)
close

The **MS Teams Bot** by BotPenguin allows businesses to automate conversations and notifications directly within **Microsoft Teams**. It helps teams receive updates, handle internal queries, and streamline workflows inside their Teams workspace.

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/ms-teams-bot#what-you-can-do-with-an-ms-teams-bot)

What You Can Do With an MS Teams Bot

*   Send automated messages to Teams users or channels
    
*   Share alerts, updates, and notifications
    
*   Handle internal FAQs and HR queries
    
*   Collect information and user inputs
    
*   Automate workflows and internal support
    
*   Provide 24/7 assistance within MS Teams
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/ms-teams-bot#key-benefits)

Key Benefits

*   🧑‍💼 Improve internal team communication
    
*   ⚡ Deliver instant updates inside Teams
    
*   🤖 Reduce manual follow-ups and repetitive tasks
    
*   🔒 Secure communication within Microsoft ecosystem
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/ms-teams-bot#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases

*   Internal support and IT helpdesk
    
*   HR queries and onboarding assistance
    
*   Task reminders and alerts
    
*   Workflow automation
    
*   Team announcements
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://help.botpenguin.com/bots/ms-teams-bot#requirements-to-use-ms-teams-bot)

Requirements to Use MS Teams Bot

*   A Microsoft Teams account
    
*   Admin access to install bots in Teams
    
*   BotPenguin account with MS Teams integration enabled
    
*   An active bot with configured chat flows
